'phrul mthong // bsam pa brtan pas rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems kyang skyed// des ni stong gsum ma lus sa rnams rab bskyod nas// dran dang shes bzhin ting nge 'dzin las langs gyur te// mdog bzang ldan rol pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po bdun pa/ dge slong dag de ltar gzhon nu de de bas kyang ya zad skyes pa dang / dus gzhan zhig na rgyal po zas gtsang ma shAkya'i tshogs dang lhan cig tu 'dun sa na 'dug 'dug pa de'i tshe/ shAkya rgan rabs rgan rabs kha cig gis rgyal po zas gtsang ma la 'di skad ces smras so// lha mkhyen par mdzad du gsol/ gzhon nu don thams cad grub pa 'di ni bram ze ltas mkhan rnams dang / blo nges pa dang ldan pa'i lha mang pos 'di skad du bstan te/ gzhon nu 'di gal te mngon par byung bar gyur na ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur ro// ji ste mngon par ma byung na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhi las rnam par rgyal ba chos kyi rgyal po chos dang ldan zhing rin po che sna bdun dang ldan par 'gyur ro// de'i rin po che sna bdun ni 'di dag ste/ 'di ltar 'khor lo rin po che dang / glang po rin po che dang / rta rin po che dang / nor bu rin po che dang / bud med rin po che dang / khyim bdag rin po che dang / blon po rin po che dang bdun no// de la bu dpa' ba/ rtul phod pa/ yan lag mchog gi gzugs dang ldan pa/ gzhan gyi sde rab tu 'joms pa stong tshang ba 'byung ngo // de gnod par bya ba dang / mtshon cha med par chos dang 'thun pas sa'i dkyil 'khor 'di las mngon par rgyal bar byas te/ gcig pu gnas par 'gyur ro zhes mchi na/ de'i slad du gzhon nu de'i btsun mo blang bar bgyi'o// de ltar mdzad dang bud med kyi tshogs kyis yongs su bskor te/ dgyes pa la longs spyod cing mngon par 'byung bar yang mi 'gyur te/ de ltar gyur pa dang bdag cag gi 'khor los sgyur ba'i gdung yang mi 'chad/ khams kyi rgyal po thams cad kyis kyang mi snyan par mi brjod cing rim gror bgyi bar 'gyur ro// de nas rgyal po zas gtsang mas smras pa/ gal te de ltar bya na de'i phyir gzhon nu'i tshul dang 'thun pa'i bu mo gang zhig yod khyed kyis ltos shig // de'i tshe shAkya lnga brgya tsam so so nas 'di skad du bdag gi bu mo ni gzhon nu'i tshul dang 'thun no// bdag gi bu mo ni gzhon nu'i tshul dang 'thun no zhes zer ro// rgyal pos smras pa/ gzhon nu de ni shin tu phul che ba yin gyis/ gzhon nu nyid la khyod bu mo gang 'dod ces dri bar bya'o zhes/ de dag kun kyang 'dus te/ gzhon nu la dngos po de brjod do// gzhon nus smras pa/ da ste dgung bdun na 'di'i lan gsan par gsol/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'di snyam du bsams te/ 'dod pa'i skyon ni bdag gis mtha' yas rig // thab mo khon bcas mya ngan sdug bsngal rtsa// 'jigs byed dug gi lo ma 'dra ba ste// me dang 'dra zhing ral gri'i so dang 'dra// 'dod pa'i yon tan bdag 'dod ma yin te// bdag ni bud med tshogs dang mdzes ma yin// bsam gtan ting 'dzin bde bas zhi sems su// bdag ni mi smra nags tshal gnas par bya// yang des brtags nas thabs mkhas pa mngon du byas te/ sems can yongs su smin par bya ba la bltas nas/ snying rje chen po bskyed de/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// 'dam dang lcag lcig khrod nas pad ma rnam par 'phel// mi rnams gang ba'i nang na rgyal po mchod pa 'thob// gang tshe byang chub sems dpa' 'khor mchog thob gyur pa// de tshe sems can bye ba khrag khrig 'chi med 'dul// sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa' mkhas pa gang byung ba// de dag kun gyis btsun mo sras dang slas kyang bsten// 'on kyang 'dod pas chags med bsam gtan bde ma nyams// bdag kyang de dag yon tan rjes su bslab par bya// gang la spyod lam yon tan bden pa'i tshig med pa// bud med phal pa gang yang bdag gi tshul 'thun min// gang zhig bdag gi sems ni mngon par dga' byed cing // bag yod gzugs dang na tshod rus rigs dag pa 'os// des ni yon tan tshigs su bcad de yi ger bris// 'di 'dra'i bu mo mchis na bdag la bka' stsol cig // skye bo phal pa ma bsdams bdag la mkho ma lags// yon tan brjod pa 'di ldan mchis na bdag stsol cig // dar cing gzugs bzang ldan yang gzugs kyi dregs dang bral// phu nu ma la byams ltar byams pa'i sems ldan zhing // gtong la dga' ste dge sbyong bram ze sbyin tshul can// de 'dra'i bu mo mchis na yab kyis bdag stsol cig // gang la nga rgyal khengs dang zhe sdang ma mchis shing // g.yo dang phrag dog sgyu spangs drang ba'i ngang tshul can// rmi lam na yang skyes pa gzhan la chags dang bral// bdag gi khyos ni chog 'tshal rtag sdom bag mchis la// rgyags pa ma mchis mi g.yeng zung thub tshul 'chang zhing // nga rgyal ma mchis 'gying dang bral bas bran mo bzhin// sgra dri ro la ma chags chang la ma chags te// 'dod bral brnab sems ma mchis rang gi nor gyis 'tshal// bden la gnas shing mi 'phyar g.yeng ba ma lags pa// ngo tsha'i gos 'tshal rgod dang khengs pa ma mchis gnas// lha dang bkra shis ma chags rtag tu chos la brtson// lus dang ngag dang yid kyi dngos po rab dag pa// gnyid dang rmugs pa mi mang nga rgyal glen bral zhing // rtog dang ldan la legs pa'i las rnams rtag spyod de// gyos sgyug gnyis la'ang ston pa bzhin gyi rim gror ldan// bran dang bran mo kun la'ang bdag bzhin byams srel ba// smad 'tshong bzhin du bstan bcos cho ga 'tshal cing mkhas// slad kyis nyal zhing sngon du mal nas ldang bgyid pa// byams pas rjes snyegs ma bzhin tshul 'chos ma mchis pa// de 'dra'i bud med mchis na yab kyis bdag stsol cig // dge slong dag de nas rgyal po zas gtsang mas tshigs su bcad pa de dag thos nas/ mdun na 'don la smras pa/ bram ze chen po khyod ser skya'i gnas kyi grong khyer chen por song la/ khyim thams cad du'ang song ste/ bu mo dag ltos la gang la yang rung ste yon tan de lta bu dag yod na/ rgyal rigs kyi bu mo yang rung // bram ze'i bu mo yang rung // rje'u rigs kyi bu mo yang rung // dmangs rigs kyi bu mo yang rung gis/ bu mo de dag 'dir 'on cig // de ci'i phyir zhe na/ gzhon nu 'di ni rigs don du gnyer ba ma yin rus don du gnyer ba ma yin gyi/ gzhon nu 'di ni yon tan don du gnyer ba yin no// de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag kyang smras so// rgyal rigs bram ze'i bu mo dang // rje'u rigs dmangs rigs de bzhin te// su la yon tan 'di yod pa'i// bu mo de ni 'dir 'on cig // nga yi bu 'di rigs dag dang // rus la ngo mtshar 'dzin ma yin// yon tan bden pa chos kyi rnams// de la 'di yi yid dga' 'o// dge slong dag de nas bram ze mdun na 'don des tshigs su bcad pa yi ger bris ma mthong ste/ de nas rim gyis shAkya lag na be con can gyi khyim du phyin nas/ des bltas na/ bu mo gzugs mdzes shing blta na sdug la yid du 'ong ba/ mdog bzang po rgyas pa mchog dang ldan pa/ ha cang yang mi ring ba/ ha cang yang mi thung ba/ ha cang yang mi sbom pa/ ha cang yang mi skem pa/ ha cang yang mi dkar ba/ ha cang yang mi gnag pa/ gzod ma dar la bab pa/ bud med rin po che ltar snang ba chung mar 'os// zhes smras te/ des de la yi ge de byin no// de nas bu mo des tshigs su bcad pa'i yi ge de bklags nas/ bzhin 'dzum pa bstan te/ bram ze mdun na 'don de la tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ tshig 'chal med gyur la// dbang po sbas shing shin tu bsdams la yid dang ba// de lta bu dag gdong g.yogs te ni ci zhig bya// gal te lus la gos ni stong gis g.yogs gyur kyang // gang dag sems bshus ngo tsha med cing khrel med dang // gang dag 'di 'dra'i yon tan med cing bden tshig med// de dag sgren mo bas kyang sgren mor 'jig rten rgyu// gang zhig sems sbas rtag tu dbang po bsdams gyur cing // bdag gi khyos chog sems can gzhan la mi sems pa// de 'dra ba dag nyi zla bzhin du ma g.yogs sa snang // de 'dra ba dag gdong g.yogs te ni ci zhig bya// gzhan yang drang srong bdag nyid che dang gzhan sems blo mkhas dang // de bzhin lha tshogs dag gis kho mo'i bsam pa dang // kho mo'i tshul khrims yon tan sdom dang bag yod mkhyen// de lta bas na kho mos gdong bkab ci zhig dgos// dge slong dag rgyal po zas gtsang mas shAkya'i bu mo sa 'tsho ma'i spobs pa dang bstan pa'i tshigs su bcad pa rnam pa 'di lta bu 'di thos so// thos nas kyang tshim zhing mgu la yi rangs te rab tu dga' zhing dga' ba dang yid bde ba skyes nas/ ras bcos bu bzang po rin po che du mas spras pa zung gcig dang / mu tig gi do shal srang bye ba brgya stong ri ba dang / mu tig dmar po bzang pos spras pa'i gser gyi phreng bas shAkya'i bu mo sa 'tsho ma la bkab nas ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// kho bo'i bu ni yon tan ci 'dras brgyan pa dang // mna' ma rang gi yon tan ji ltar rab smra ba// sems can dag pa de gnyis phrad par gyur pa ni// mar dang mar gyi nying khu ji ltar 'dra ba bzhin// sgyu rtsal bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu gnyis pa'o// // 'phags pa rgya cher rol pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po brgyad sems can gang dag 'dis yun ring po nas bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi po sbyin pa dang / snyan par smra ba dang / don spyad pa dang / don 'thun pas yongs su smin par byas pa dang / gang dag 'dis byang chub mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'am cig tu mi 'gyur grang snyam mo// de nas de dag gus pa dang bcas zhe sa dang bcas par thal mo sbyar te/ byang chub sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal nas/ nam zhig na bdag cag gis byang chub sems dpa' dam pa mchog rab dag pa 'di mngon par byung ba dang / mngon par byung nas kyang shing gi rgyal po chen po de'i drung du 'dug ste/ bdud dpung dang bcas pa btul nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang ldan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mi 'jigs pa bzhi dang ldan pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa brgyad dang ldan pa dang / lan gsum du bzlas te rnam pa bcu gnyis su bskor ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo bla na med pa skor zhing sangs rgyas kyi rnam par rol pa chen pos lha dang mi dang lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du legs par bshad pas tshim par byed pa mthong bar 'gyur snyam pa'i bsam pa de lta bus sdod cing 'khod par gyur to// dge slong dag de la byang chub sems dpa' ni bskal pa grangs med pa'i yang grangs med pa nas bzung ste/ yun ring por rtag par rgyun tu 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos thams cad la gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog par gyur cing // dge ba'i chos spyod pa thams cad la bdag nyid slob dpon du gyur pa yin la/ yun ring po nas dus shes pa dang / tshod shes pa dang / ran pa shes par gyur pa dang / mngon par shes pa las ma nyams pa dang / mngon par shes pa lnga dang ldan pa dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pas rnam par rtse ba dang / sems can gyi bsam pa dang dbang po la mkhas pa dang / dus dang dus ma yin pa shes pa dang / dus la lta zhing rgya mtsho chen po ltar dus ran pa las mi yol bar gyur pa'o// de mngon par shes pa'i ye shes kyi stobs dang ldan pas 'di ni rab tu gzung ba'i dus so// 'di ni tshar gcad pa'i dus so// 'di ni bsdu ba'i dus so// 'di ni phan gdags pa'i dus so// 'di ni btang snyoms su gzhag pa'i dus so// 'di ni smra ba'i dus so// 'di ni mi smra bar bya ba'i dus so// 'di ni khyim nas 'byung ba'i dus so// 'di ni rab tu 'byung ba'i dus so// 'di ni kha ton bya ba'i dus so// 'di ni tshul bzhin yid la bya ba'i dus so// 'di ni rab tu dben par bya ba'i dus so// 'di ni rgyal rigs kyi 'khor gyi nang du 'gro ba'i dus so zhes bya ba nas/ 'di ni bram ze dang khyim bdag gi bar gyi 'khor gyi nang du 'gro ba'i dus so// 'di ni lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten skyong ba dang / dge slong dang / dge slong ma dang / dge bsnyen dang / dge bsnyen ma'i 'khor gyi nang du 'gro ba'i dus so// 'di ni chos bstan pa'i dus so// 'di ni nang du yang dag par gzhag pa'i dus so zhes bya ba thams cad bdag nyid kyis shes so// byang chub sems dpa' dus thams cad du rtag par 'du shes par gyur cing // dus la lta ba yin yang dge slong dag 'di ni chos nyid kyis thob pa yin te/ srid pa tha ma pa'i byang chub sems dpa' btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang na 'khod pa rnams la phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams na bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams glu dbyangs dang sil snyan gyi sgra las chos kyi sgo rnam pa 'di lta bu 'di dag gis yang dag par skul ba mdzad do// de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ sems can mchog gang phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten bzhugs// de dag mthu yis sil snyan sgra dag las// tshigs bcad sgra snyan 'di dag byung ba yis// mi mchog dam pa rnams la yang dag skul// sdug bsngal brgyas gang sems can mthong nas ni// 'gro ba'i mgon dang skyabs dang gnas 'gyur zhing // phan byed mchog dang dpung gnyen gyur cig ces// khyod kyis sngon ni smon lam de skad btab// dge ba dpa' bo sngon gyi spyod pa dang // 'gro phan bya zhes smon btab dran par byos// 'di ni khyod kyis dus man tshod yin gyis// drang srong mchog rab mngon par 'byung bar byos// sangs rgyas lha mi 'dul byed 'jig rten mchog // yon tan brgyas gang bar ni gyur cig ces// de'i phyir khyod sngon mgo dang rkang lag dang // nor gyi dam pa sna tshogs rnams kyang btang // khyod ni khrims kyis brtul zhugs dka' thub spyad// khyod ni bzod pas 'gro la phan pa byed// khyod ni brtson pas yon tan brgya yis gang // bsam gtan shes rab srid gsum mnyam pa med// khro bas non cing tha ba'i dri mang ba// de dag bde gshegs khyod kyi byams pas khyab// dge ba'i yon tan bral ba log nges pa// mi mkhas rnam mang dag la khyod snying rje// bsod nams ye shes dge ba'i lus khyab cing // rdul bral bsam gtan mngon shes lam mer 'dug // phyogs bcu 'di dag rnams su rab tu gsal// sprin med zla ba dri ma med pa 'dra// 'di dang gzhan yang snyan pa rnam mang gis// sil snyan dag las rgyal bas sgra bsgrags te// mngon par khyod 'byung dus ni 'di yin zhes// lha mis mchod par 'os la skul ma 'debs// dge slong dag byang chub sems dpa' khyim dam pa mchog yo byad phun sum tshogs pa thams cad dang ldan pa/ bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du bde bar gnas pa dang 'thun pa/ lha'i khang khyim lta bu stegs bu dang / sgo khang dang / rta babs dang / skar khung dang / bsil khang dang / khang pa brtsegs pa dang / khang mchog dang / rin po che sna tshogs kyi rgyan rnam pa tha dad pa dbye ba shin tu rnam par phye ba/ gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan bsgreng ba/ rin po che'i dril bu g.yer ka'i dra ba du mas legs par brgyan pa/ dar gyi lda ldi brgya stong du mas mngon par spyangs pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyis spras pa'i mu tig gi rgyan phreng rab tu spyangs pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi spang leb can gyi zam pas mdzes par byas pa/ me tog gi phreng ba dang chun po mang po spyangs pa/ pog snod nas spos kyis bdugs pa/ dar la'i bla re bres pa/ dus thams cad pa'i me tog dri mchog tu zhim zhing // shin tu mdzes pa dag bkram pa/ rdzing me tog pad ma dkar po dang / pad ma dang ldan pa'i chu'i gnas yongs su spyad par bya ba mang ba/ bya 'dab skyong dang / ne tso dang / ri skegs dang / khu byug dang / ngang pa dang / rma bya dang / ngur pa dang / ku na la dang / ka la ping ka dang / shang shang te'u la sogs pa bya rnam pa tha dad pa'i tshogs sgra snyan pa 'byin pa/ bai dUr+ya sngon po'i sa gzhi gnas yongs su spyad par bya ba/ gzugs thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan kun tu ston pa/ blta bas mi ngoms par nyams dga' ba/ dga' ba dang mchog tu dga' ba dam pa skyed pa'i khyim dam pa mchog de na 'dug ste/ byang chub sems dpa' khang pa mdzes pa chen po mchog na gnas pa/ dri ma med pa/ dri ma dang bral ba/ yan lag dri ma med pa/ phreng ba dang rgyan ma bor ba/ dri mchog tu zhim pa dam pa'i byug pas lus bskus pa/ dkar zhing bzang la dri ma med cing rnam par dag la dri ma dang bral ba'i gos gyon pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ mal cha lha'i ras bcos bu bzang po phra ba du ma bting ba 'jam pa ka tsa lin da'i gos ltar reg na bde ba/ yan lag dam pas spras pa'i mal bzang po'i steng na 'dug pa btsun mo'i 'khor dam pa lha'i bu mo dang 'dra ba/ thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med pa/ lta ba dang 'thun pa/ spyod pa bzang pos mdzes par byas pa/ gzugs bzang ba'i nang na 'dug pa/ dung dang / rnga dang / rdza rnga dang / khar rnga dang / pi bang dang / rgyud gsum pa dang / khar ba'i sil khrol dang / pheg dang / kim pa la dang / na ku la dang / sgra snyan dang / gling bu snyan pa'i sgra 'byung ba'i sgra dbyangs dang / sil snyan dang / glu dbyangs sna tshogs dang ldan pas bslang ba la/ bud med kyi tshogs kyis kyang // sgra mnyen zhing 'jam pa snyan la yid du 'ong ba dang / gling bu 'bud pa'i sgra dbyangs kyis byang chub sems dpa' slong ngo // phyogs bcu na bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gi byin gyi rlabs kyis sil snyan gyi sgra byung ba'i sgra skad de dag las byang chub sems dpa' la skul ba'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag byung ngo // bud med gang dag rab tu yid dga' sems dang bas// sil snyan yid du 'ong zhing snyan pa'i sgra 'byin tshe// phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba dam pa dag gi mthu yis ni// tshigs bcad rnam pa sna tshogs rnam mang 'di dag byung // rtag tu mgon med gyur pa'i 'gro ba 'di mthong nas// go 'phang mya ngan med mchog rdul med sangs rgyas te// skye dang rga dang sdug bsngal dag las dgrol lo zhes// dpa' bo khyod sngon smon lam de skad btab par gyur// de phyir dge myur grong khyer mchog 'di nas// byung la sngon gyi drang srong zhabs bcags pa// sa phyogs de ni rab tu mnan nas su// rgyal ba'i ye shes mtshungs med 'tshang rgyar gyis// khyod kyis sngon chad sna tshogs rin chen nor// rkang lag phangs pa'i lus kyang btang bar gyur// drang srong chen po khyod dus 'di// chos kyi chu bo mtha' yas 'gro la phye// khyod kyi tshul khrims ma nyams dri med dge// sngon chad khyod ni rtag tu mchog gis brgyan// drang srong chen po khyod khrims 'dra ba med// 'gro ba nyon mongs rnam pa mang las khrol// khyod kyis srid pa brgyar ni bzod pa spyad// khyod ni 'gro bas ngan brjod rnam mang bzod// bzod pas bzod cing dul bas des pa'i bdag // rkang gnyis dbang po mngon par 'byung blo gyis// khyod brtson brtan zhing mi g.yo g.yo ba med// bde bar gshegs pa sngon mthar rgya chen gyur// g.yon can bdud ni sde dang bcas btul te// ngan song gsum po mtha' dag skams par gyis// gang phyir khyod kyis brtul zhugs dka' thub spyad// dus ngan nyon mongs snyigs ma bsregs gyis la// khyod kyis bdud rtsi chu bo'i char phob ste// mgon med ring nas skom pa tshim par gyis// 'chi med mya ngan med gnas sangs rgyas te// skom pas nyam thag bdud rtsis tshim bya zhes// khyod kyis sngon smras tshig mchog dran byos te// grong khyer dam pa 'di nas myur du byung // khyod ni shes rab mchog gi spyod pa mkhas/ khyod kyi ye shes mtha' yas dri med che// rmongs pa yid gnyis lam la gnas rnams la// shes rab 'od dge dam pa mdzes par gyis// khyod kyis srid pa brgyar ni byams pa spyad// snying rje dang ni dga' mchog btang snyoms dang // khyod kyis spyod pa dam pa gang spyad pa// spyod pa de nyid 'gro la rnam par phye// phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba dag gi gzi brjid kyis// yon tan me tog sna tshogs tshigs bcad 'di// sil snyan dag las rnam mang yid 'ong grag // mal na 'dug pa'i gzhon nu de la skul// gang gi tshe na dag bud med rab tu dga' ba rnams// shin tu mdzes shing rab tu snyan pa'i sil snyan sgrogs pa'i tshe// phyogs bcu dag gi rgyal ba lha mi 'dul ba mdzad rnams kyang // sil snyan dag las gsung mchog ha cang mi che rjes su sgrog // 'gro la phan byed yon tan mang po ldan khyod 'gro rnams su// rnam par rgyu ba'i tshe na rgyal ba'i yon tan gnyug mar byas// sngon gyi brtul zhugs dka' thub spyad pa de dag dran gyis te// shing mchog drung du myur song 'chi med go 'phang thob par gyis// lha mi dag ni shin tu skom zhing rgyal ba'i yon tan bral// khyod ni shin tu stobs ldan bdud rtsi'i ro bro rtag tu sbyin// stobs bcu'i ro bro dam pa mkhas pa rnams kyis mchod byas pa// bdud rtsi de ni mi bdag khyod kyis myur du rnam par phye// rgyal ba'i yon tan 'gro la phan pa byed la dga' ba po// khyod kyis sngon gyi srid par nor dang nor bu gser rnams btang // chung ma bu sdug dag dang grong khyer grong rdal bcas pa dang // rang gi mgo dang mig dang lag pa dag dang rkang pa'ang btang // mi mchog khyod ni gna' sngon rgyal po dge bar gyur pa'i tshe// mi zhig khyod la mngon du phyogs nas 'di skad tshig smras te// grong khyer grong rdal bcas pa'i sa 'di kho la byin zhes byas// de yi tshe na rab tu dga' zhing 'khrugs par gyur pa med// gna' sngon khyod ni rgyal po'i bram ze dge bar gyur pa'i tshe// skye bo bla ma bsnyen bkur byed cing gzhan la 'khu mi byed// bram ze dam pa dag dang skye bo mang po dge la bkod// de nas shi 'phos srid pa'i 'gro ba lha yi gnas su skyes// sngon khyod rgyal po'i bu las drang srong dam par gyur pa'i tshe// rgyal po ngan pa khros pas khyod kyi yan lag bcad pa na// khyod ni yid 'khrugs gyur pa med par 'chi ba'i dus byas te// de yi tshe na khyod kyi rkang lag dag las 'o ma zag // khyod sngon drang srong sngo bsangs zhes byar gang tshe gyur pa na// ri mchog gnas na brtul zhugs dga' zhing bla ma la yang dga'// mi yi bdag pos dug mda' dag gis khyod la bsnun pa na// khyod ni rgyal po de la yid 'khrugs med cing snying brtser gyur// khyod sngon bdag po yon tan can du gyur pa'i tshe// ri gzar 'bab chu chen pos mi zhig khyer bar gyur pa na// phan dang ldan pa khyod kyis mi de phyung ste thang la bzhag // khyod kyi dgra bo khrid de 'ongs pa na yang yid ma 'khrugs// mi mchog khyod sngon bram ze'i bur ni gang tshe gyur pa na// khyod kyi nor bu rgya mtsho chen po yangs par lhung ba'i tshe// khyod kyis rgya mtsho chen po zad par bya bar brtsams pa dang // stobs brtan khyu mchog khyod kyi nor bu de tshe phyir yang rnyed// skyes bu mchog khyod gna' sngon drang srong dam par gyur pa'i tshe// bram ze zhig gis bdag gi skyabs gyur shog ces khyod gan 'ongs// smras pa bram ze dam pa kho bo dgra las byung zhes byas// khyod kyis rang lus btang gis bram ze de ni ma btang ngo // gna' sngon shing gi gnas su drang srong sngo bsangs drung 'ongs te// 'dod pas smras pa shing 'di lo ma du yod grongs zhes byas// shing de lo ma ji snyed yod pa rab bgrangs rab mkhas pas// khyod kyis de bzhin nor pa med cing 'thun par tshig tu brjod// khyod sngon ne tso yon tan ldan gyur shing la gnas pa'i tshe// zad par gyur kyang sngon gyi drin la bsams te de ma spangs// lha yi bdag pos khyod kyi yon tan dran nas rab tu dga'// snga mkho bzhin du shing mchog de ni dpal dang ldan par byas// khyod kyi brtul zhugs dka' thub spyad pa de dag mtshungs med de// yon tan ldan pa yon tan lam la spyad pas yon tan mang // khyod kyi dus la da bab grong khyer bcas pa'i sa yang thong // 'gro ba dag ni rgyal ba'i yon tan spyod la myur du khod// gang gi tshe na bud med rin chen bzang po'i gos kyis lus brgyan te// sil snyan dam pa mchog rab yid du 'ong ba'i sgra ni rab sgrog pa// de tshe phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba'i gzi yis tshigs su bcad pa sna tshogs pa// sgra dbyangs snyan pa 'di dag sil snyan dag gi sgra las rab tu byung // rga dang shi bas zin pa'i 'jig rten dag la bdag ni skyabs gyur ces// 'jig rten sgron ma khyod kyis bskal mang snga rol smon lam de skad btab// mi yi seng ge khyod kyis sngon gyi smon lam dag ni dran gyis shig // rkang gnyis dbang po khyod da mngon par 'byung ba'i dus ni 'di yin no// khyod 'dir srid pa khrag khrig dag tu sbyin pa mang po du ma byin// nor dang rin po che dang gser dang gos bzang rin chen spras pa dang // rkang lag dag dang mig dang phangs pa'i bu dang rgyal srid 'byor pa dag // khyod kyis btang yang khyod ni slong ba rnams la tha ba zhe sdang med// khyod 'dir zla ba'i tog dang mche ba bzang dang rgyal po zhi bar gyur// snying brtse snying rje'i yid dang zla ba'i sgron dang gtsug na nor bur gyur// rgyal po dpa' bo brtan dang mig dang ni de la sogs pa byas// rgyal po khrag khrig mang po sbyin dga' rnam par 'phrul pa de nyid khyod// bde bar gshegs pa khyod kyis bskal pa mang por tshul khrims spyod pa spyad// nor bu rin chen dri ma med pa lta bur tshul khrims rnam dag gyur// khyod kyis 'bri yi rnga ma ci 'dra de 'drar tshul khrims bsrungs shing spyad// tshul khrims dga' bas khyod kyis 'dir ni 'gro la rgya cher don yang byas// 'dir khyod glang po mchog tu gyur te rngon pa dgra yis mdas bsnun tshe// gtum po dgra la snying brtse snying rje bskyed nas de ni khyod kyis bskyabs// bzang zhing mdzes pa'i mche ba yongs su btang ste tshul khrims yong ma btang // khyod kyis de la sogs pa tshul khrims rnam par 'phrul pa mang po byas// bzod la dga' bas khyod kyis 'gro ba'i mi phan sdug bsngal stong mang dang // tshig rtsub ngag dang bsad pa dang ni bcing ba mang po bzod par byas// khyod kyis gna' sngon mi gang dag la bde ba kun gyis rim gror byas// de dag phyi nas khyod kyi gshed mar gyur kyang khyod kyis de dag bzod// mgon po khyod ni ri mchog gnas na gang tshe dred mor gyur pa'i tshe// kha ba bab cing chu brug pas ni 'jigs shing skrag pa'i mi bzung ste// rtsa ba 'bras bu rnam pa mang dang bde ba kun gyis rim gro byas// de yis myur du khyod la gsod pa khrid 'ongs khyod kyis de la bzod// byang chub btsal phyir brtul zhugs dka' thub yon tan rnam mang ye shes la// khyod kyis brtson 'grus shin tu brtan par gnas shing mi g.yo g.yo ba med// dbang sgyur bdud kyang khyod kyis brtson 'grus stobs kyis stobs ni med par byas// mi yi seng ge khyod 'dir mngon par 'byung ba'i dus la da bab bo// khyod 'dir gna' sngon kha ba'i kha dog 'dra ba'i rta mchog gyur pa'i tshe// snying rje bskyed nas nam mkha' las ni srin po'i gling du myur du song // de tshe phongs shing 'dug pa'i mi de blangs te bde la rab tu bzhag // khyod kyis 'di la sogs pa brtson 'grus rnam par 'phrul pa mang po byas// myur du 'gyur zhing g.yo la yul la dga' zhing rgod pa'i sems brtul te// bsam gtan par gyur dul des zhi gnas rnams kyis nyon mongs gtso bo bcom// khyod 'dir bsam gtan dga' bas rang gi yon tan dag gis 'gro don byas// da 'dir sems can mchog khyod bsam gtan rnam 'phrul bya ba'i dus la bab// gna' sngon khyod ni drang srong bsam gtan dga' zhing rab tu gnas par gyur// rgyal po med pa'i mi dag gis ni khyod khrid rgyal srid dbang yang bskur// khyod kyis skye bo dag ni dge ba bcu dang tshangs pa'i lam la bkod// de yi tshe na mi las shi 'phos thams cad tshangs pa'i gnas su dong // phyogs dang phyogs mtshams 'gro ba rnam mang shes pa'i cho ga khyod rab mkhas// gzhan gyi spyod dang 'gro ba'i skad shes pa dang dbang po shes pa dang // tshul dang 'dul dang blo gros rnam mang rgyu ba'i pha rol khyod phyin gyur// rgyal po'i sras khyod 'dir ni mngon par 'byung ba'i dus la da bab bo// khyod kyis gna' sngon skye bo lta ba log par zhugs par gyur pa dag // rga shi sdug bsngal rnam pa mang pos nyam thag 'khod pa 'di mthong nas// srid pa rnam par gzhig pa'i drang lam nyid kyis khong du chud byas te// mun pa bcom pa khyod kyis 'jig rten dag la don chen rab tu byas// tshigs bcad rnam pa mang po mdzes pa yon tan ldan pa sna tshogs 'dis// sil snyan sgra bsgrags de las rgyal ba'i gzi yis dpa' bo skul bar gyur// blo mchog ldan pa khyod 'dir mngon par 'byung ba'i dus ni da bab kyis// sdug bsngal gang ba'i skye bo 'di dag mthong nas btang snyoms ma byed cig // bud med gos dang rin po che dang do shal spos phreng sna tshogs kyis// brgyan pa dag kyang sems dang phangs pa skyes nas rab tu dga' ba rnams// sems can mchog la sil snyan rab tu sgrog cing slong bar byed pa na/ rgyal ba'i mthu yis sil snyan dag las tshigs su bcad pa 'di 'dra byung // gang gi don du khyod kyis 'gro la phan phyir bskal pa du mar ni// gtang bar dka' ba btang zhing tshul khrims bzod pa brtson 'grus shin tu spyad// bsam gtan shes rab shin tu bsgoms pa khyod kyis dus la da bab kyis// 'dren pa mngon par 'byung ba'i blo la myur soms phyir shol ma byed cig // sngon chad rin chen mdzod dang gser dang dngul dang rgyan rnams rab tu btang // skye ba de dang de dag tu ni mchod sbyin rnam pa mang po byas// khyod kyis chung ma bu pho bu mo lus dang rgyal srid srog btang ste// byang chub don du gtang bar dka' ba dpag tu med pa khyod kyis btang // khyod ni rgyal po mi dman bsod nams dpal gyis rnam par grags par gyur// mu khyud 'dzin dang mu khyud nag po tshangs pas byin dang ral pa can// mchod sbyin stong ldan dang ni chos sems 'od 'phro can dang nor brtan dang // shin tu don bsams gyur te sems can dman la gtang bar dka' ba btang // zla ba'i bu dang brtson 'grus 'bar dang bsod nams 'od zer can du gyur// gtong ba che dang ldan zhing mthu ldan khyod ni byas pa gzo bar gyur// rgyal po drang srong zla ba gzugs ldan dpa' bo bden pa 'phel ba dang // rgyal po legs par smra ba tshol dang blo gros bzang dang des par gyur// zla ba'i 'od dang khyad par 'gro dang rdul dang phyogs kyi bdag por gyur// rab sbyin dpa' bo ka shi rgyal po rin chen gtsug phud zhi ba ston// mi dbang de dag rnams dang gzhan du gyur te gtang bar dka' ba btang // khyod kyis ji ltar gtong ba'i char phab de bzhin chos kyi char pa phob// khyod kyis sngon chad sems can snying po gang gA'i bye ma snyed cig mthong // sems can thar bar bya phyir byang chub dam pa'i mchog ni tshol ba na// khyod kyis mchod pa dpag med bsam mi khyab pas sangs rgyas de dag mchod// dpa' bo grong khyer dam pa 'di nas 'byung ba'i dus la da bab bo// thog mar khyod kyis don yod mthong la sA la'i me tog gis ni mchod// rnam par snang mdzad la ni dang ba'i sems kyis skad cig rab tu bltas// rnga dbyangs ldan pa la ni khyod kyis a ru ra yi 'bru cig phul// tsan dan mthong nas khyod kyis rtswa yi me sgron blangs te khyim du bzung // rtul po grong khyer 'jug pa mthong nas phye ma spar gang rab tu gtor// chos kyi dbang phyug chos 'chad pa na legs zhes bya ba rab tu byin// kun tu gzigs pa mthong nas phyag 'tshal phyag 'tshal lo zhes tshig tu brjod// 'od 'phro chen po'i phung po la ni khyod kyis dga' bas gser phreng gtor// 'od zer rgyal mtshan la ni kha tshar phul zhing gsal la bal sran gtor// ye shes tog la mya ngan med pa'i me tog kha lo sgyur la 'jam// rin chen gtsug tor can la mar me pad ma ldan la sman yang phul// thams cad zil gnon mu tig do shal rgya mtsho la ni pad ma phul// pad ma'i snying po la ni bla re seng ge la ni char gding phul// sA la'i dbang po rgyal la mar phul me tog rgyas la 'o ma phul// grags sbyin kun da'i me tog phul te bden pa gzigs la zhal zas phul// ye shes lhun la lus btud klus byin la ni na bza' dbul ba byas// rab mthor gshegs dang tsan dan mchog dang 'od ldan la ni tshwa spar re// bkod pa che la pad ma dbul byas 'od zer rgyal la rin chen phul// shAkya thub la spar gang gser phul dbang po'i tog la bstod pa byas// nyi ma'i zhal la me tog rna rgyan blo gros bzang la gser cod pan// klu zil gnon la nor bu phul te rgyal la ras bcos gding ba phul// sman gyi rgyal la rin chen gdugs phul seng ge'i tog la khri gdan phul// yon tan mchog ldan rin chen dra ba 'od srung la ni glu dbyangs kun// spos mchog me tog phul zhing 'od 'phro'i tog la rtag tu me tog phul// mi 'khrugs rgyal la khang brtsegs phul zhing 'jig rten mchod la phreng ba phul// rgya spos gtsug lag rgyal srid dbul byas rgyal bar dga' la spos kun phul// sgron ma che la bdag phul pad ma'i mchog la rgyan rnams dbul ba byas// chos kyi tog la me tog sna tshogs sgron ma mdzad la ud pa la// mchod pa rnam pa sna tshogs tha dad gzhan dang gzhan dag byed pa na// khyod kyis sems can snying po de dag rnams dang gzhan yang sngon chad mchod// 'das pa'i sangs rgyas rnams dang ston pa de dag khyod mchod dran par gyis// sems can mgon med mya ngan gang ba yal bar ma dor mngon par byung // mar me mdzad pa mthong ba tsam gyis khyod kyis bzod pa mchog thob ste// rjes su 'thun pa'i mngon par shes pa lnga po nyams pa med pa thob// de nas rab tu dga' bas bskal pa grangs med 'jig rten khams kun du// sangs rgyas dag ni re re la yang mchod pa bsam gyis mi khyab byas// bskal pa dpag med de dag zad gyur sangs rgyas de dag mya ngan 'das// khyod kyi lus rnams thams cad dang ni de dag ming yang gang du song // dngos po thams cad tha mar 'dzad pa'i chos te 'dus byas rtag pa med// 'dod pa rgyal srid longs spyod rtag pa min gyis grong khyer mchog nas byung // bskal pa zad par 'gyur tshe gzi brjid drag po 'jigs pa'i me 'od ltar// rga dang na dang 'chi ba mi bzad 'jigs pa chen po 'ong bar 'gyur// dngos po thams cad tha mar 'dzad pa'i chos te 'dus byas rtag pa med// shin tu sdug bsngal sems can ltos la yon tan ldan pa mngon par byung // rgyal po bde ba'i mal na nyal gyur cing // gang tshe mo tshogs gling bu rgyud gcig dang // sil snyan sna tshogs sgra yis slong byed pa// de tshe sil snyan sgra las 'di dag byung // srid gsum rga dang nad kyi sdug bsngal 'bar// 'chi me rab 'bar 'di ni mgon med pa// srid las 'byung la 'gro ba rtag tu rmongs// bum par chud pa'i bung ba 'khor ba bzhin// srid gsum mi brtan ston ka'i sprin dang 'dra// 'gro ba'i skye 'chi gar la lta dang mtshungs// 'gro ba'i tshe 'gro nam mkha'i glog 'dra ste// ri gzar 'bab chu lta bur myur mgyogs 'gro// srid sred ma rig dbang gis skye bo rnams// mi dang lha gnas ngan song lam gsum po// 'gro ba lnga po dag tu mi mkhas 'khor// dper na rdza mkhan phang lo bskor ba bzhin// rtag tu gzugs sdug mchog dang sgra snyan dang // dri zhim ro mchog reg pa bde byed pa// dus ngan rnyi la 'gro ba 'di dag thogs// dper na rngon pa'i rnyi la spre'u thogs bzhin// 'dod pa'i yon tan mya ngan gnod pa mang // 'jigs bcas rtag tu dgra byed nyon mongs bcas// ral gri so 'dra dug sdong lo ma mtshungs// ngan skyugs snod ltar 'phags pa'i skye bos spangs// 'dod pa'i yon tan 'jigs bcas nyon mongs bcas// rtag tu rjed par byed pa mun pa 'dra// rtag tu 'jigs pa'i rgyu byed sdug bsngal rtsa// srid pa'i sred pa'i 'khri shing 'phel bar byed// ji ltar me 'bar 'obs ni 'jigs bcas pa// de ltar 'dod 'di 'phags pa'i skye bos rig // 'dam rdzab che 'dra ral gri gshegs gnas 'dra// ral gri'i so la sbrang rtsis bskus dang mtshungs// ji ltar sbrul gyi mgo dang ngan skyugs snod// de ltar 'dod 'di mkhas pa rnams kyis rig // bya sha kham bu 'dra zhing gsal shing 'dra// ro la khyi ltar dgra dang bcas pa yin// 'dod pa'i yon tan 'di dag chu zla 'dra// gzugs brnyan mtshungs shing brag ca 'dra ba dang // mig yor 'dra zhing gar la lta 'dra dang // rmi lam mnyam par 'phags pa'i skye bos rig // 'dod pa'i yon tan skad cig ya ma brla// sgyu ma smig rgyu 'dra zhing pa can// chu bur dbu ba lta bu yang dag min// yongs su btags las byung bar mkhas pas rtogs// na tshod thog mar gzugs mchog 'dzin pa'i tshe// phangs shing sdug 'dod 'di ni byis pa'i spyod// rga na sdug bsngal gzi brjid lus bcom nas// rnam par spong ste klung skam bzhin// nor 'bru dam pa rdzas mang stobs ldan tshe// phangs shing sdug 'dod 'di ni byis pa'i spyod// nor nyams sdug bsngal bar ni gyur pa'i tshe// rnam par spong ste mi yis 'brog stong bzhin// ji ltar me tog shing dang 'bras bcas shing // de ltar sbyin 'dod mi la dga' bar byed// nor nyams rga bas nyen cing spang ba na// de tshe dga' bar mi 'gyur bya rgod bzhin// rdzas ldan gzugs mchog ldan tshe dpon po bzhin// phrad na sdug cing dbang po dga' bar byed// dga' na sdug bsngal nyen cing nor zad na// de tshe 'dod par mi 'gyur 'chi bdag bzhin// rga bas rga byas na tshod yol gyur na// sdong po gnam lcags kyis ni bcom pa bzhin// rga bas 'khogs na 'jigs bcas khang rul 'dra// rga las byung ba thub pa myur du smros// bud med skyes pa'i tshogs rnams rga bas skems// ma lu'i 'khri shing sA la'i nags stug bzhin// rga bas brtson 'grus rtsal dang shugs 'phrog ste// dper na skyes bu 'dam du bying ba bzhin// rga bas gzugs sdug gzugs ni mi sdug byed// rga bas gzi brjid 'phrog cing mthu stobs 'phrog // rga bas bde ba 'phrog cing brnyas par byed// rga bas 'chi byed rga bas mdangs kyang 'phrog // nad brgya mang dang nad thibs sdug bsngal gyis// 'gro ba gtses te mi yis bzhin// rga dang na bas bcom pa'i 'gro ltos la// sdug bsngal las ni 'byung ba myur shod cig // dper na dgun smad rlung dang kha ba che// rtswa shing gel ba nags sman mdangs kyang 'phrog // de ltar nad 'di 'gro ba'i mdangs 'phrog cing // dbang po gzugs dang stobs ni nyams par byed// nor 'bru nor chen tha mar zad par byed// nad ni rtag tu 'gro ba brnyas par byed// gnod pa byed cing sdug la sdang bar byed// yongs su gdung byed mkha' las nyi ma bzhin// 'chi dang 'pho dang 'chi 'pho dus byed pa// phangs shing sdug pa'i skye bo rtag tu 'bral// phyir mi 'ong zhing 'phrad par 'gyur ma yin// shing las lo 'bru 'dra zhing klu yi rgyan dang mtshungs// zhi ba dbang yod pa dag dbang med byed// 'chi ba 'phrog byed chu bos shing ded bzhin// mi ni gnyis min grogs med gcig pur 'gro// rang las 'bras bu ldan pas dbang yang med// 'chi bas srog chags brgya phrag mang 'dzin te// 'byung po'i tshogs la rgya mtsho'i chu srin bzhin// klu la mkha' lding glang chen seng ge 'dra// rtswa rtsi 'byung po'i tshogs la me dang mtshungs// skyon brgya mang po 'di 'dra 'di dag las// 'gro ba sgrol zhes khyod kyis smon lam btab// sngon gyi smon lam spyod pa de dran byos// khyod ni mngon par 'byung ba'i dus la bab// gang tshe bud med tshogs ni rab dga' zhing // sil snyan dag gis thub chen slong byed pa// de tshe bde bar gshegs pa rnams kyi mthus// tshigs bcad sna tshogs sil snyan sgra las byung // 'dus byas thams cad myur du 'jig pa ste// mkha' la glog rgyun ring du mi gnas bzhin// khyod kyi dus 'di nye bar gnas gyur gyis// brtul zhugs bzang po mngon 'byung dus la bab// 'du byed mi rtag brtan pa ma yin te// rdza so ma btang lta bur 'jig pa'i bdag // gzhan gyi rdzas ni brnyan po byas dang mtshungs// bye ma'i grong khyer lta bur ring mi thogs// 'du byed 'di dag 'jig pa'i chos can te// dbyar gyi zhal zhal ji ltar 'gogs pa bzhin// chu ngogs bye ma yod pa 'dra ba ste// rkyen la rag las rang bzhin nyam chung ba// 'du byed mar me'i 'od 'phro 'dra ba ste// myur du 'byung zhing 'gag pa'i chos can yin// rlung dang mtshungs par ring du mi gnas la// dbu ba lta bur nyam chung snying po med// 'du byed g.yo ba med cing stong pa ste// brtags na chu shing dag gi phung po 'dra// sgyu ma lta bur sems ni rmongs par byed// lag bcangs stongs pas byis pa brid dang mtshungs// 'dus byas gyur pa thams cad rgyu dag dang // rkyen rnams kyis ni rab tu 'byung ba ste// gcig gis gcig rgyu byas te brten nas byung // byis pa'i skye bos 'di 'dra de ma rtogs// dper na gres ma mun dza brten byas la// rtsol ba'i stobs kyis thag par sgyur ba dang // zo chun rgyud mo 'khor lor bcas pa yang // de dag re res 'grub par 'gyur ba med// de ltar srid pa'i yan lag kun grub pa// gzhan dang gzhan tshogs pa la brten nas ni// de dag so so re rer 'grub par 'gyur// sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha' mi dmigs// sa bon yod na myu gu ji bzhin te// sa bon gang yin myu gu de nyid min// de las gzhan min de yang ma yin te// de ltar rtag min chad min chos nyid do// ma rig pa yi 'du byed rkyen yin te// 'du byed de yang yang dag nyid du med// ma rig pa dang 'du byed de dag kyang // rang bzhin stong ste g.yo ba med pa yin// rgya las rgya yi 'bur ni snang mod kyi// rgya de 'phos par gyur pa'ang yod ma yin// de la de med gzhan las ma yin te// de ltar 'dus byas rtag med chad pa med// mig dang gzugs la brten pa byas nas su// mig gi rnam par shes pa 'dir 'byung yang // mig ni gzugs la brten pa ma yin la// gzugs kyang mig la 'pho ba yod ma yin// 'di dag bdag med mi sdug chos can yang // de dag bdag dang sdug par brtags pa ste// nor pa yang dag ma yin brtags yin yang // de las mig gi rnam par shes pa 'byung // rnam par shes pa 'gags nas 'byung 'gyur te// mkhas pas skye dang 'jig pa rnam par mthong // gang du ma song gang nas 'ongs pa min// rnal 'byor pas ni stong pa sgyu ltar mthong // dper na gtsub shing dang ni gtsub stan dang // lag pas rtsol ba byas pa gsum tshogs pa// de la brten nas me ni 'byung 'gyur te// byung nas ring por mi thogs 'gag par 'gyur// de nas mkhas pa la las brtags byas te// 'di ni gang nas 'ongs la gar song zhes// phyogs dang phyogs mtshams kun tu brtags byas nas// de yi 'ong ba'am 'gro ba mi dmigs so// phung po dag dang skye mched khams rnams kyi// rkyen ni ma rig pa dang sred dang las// de dag tshogs pa sems can zhes brjod kyang // de ni dam pa'i don du dmigs su med// mchu dang lkog ma rkan la brten nas ni// lce bsgyur ba las yi ge'i sgra 'byung yang // lkog mar brten nas ma yin rkan las min// re re la ni yi ge dmigs su med// tshogs pa de la brten nas ngag de ni// yid kyi blo yi dbang gis 'byung mod kyi// yid dang ngag ni mi snang gzugs med de// nang dang phyi rol na yang dmigs su med// mkhas pas ngag skad sgra dang dbyangs rnams kyi// skye dang 'jig la rnam par brtags byas na// de tshe ngag kun brag ca lta bu dang // skad cig pa dang snying po med par byed gyur pa thams cad byung ba ste// yang dag mthong ba'i rnal 'byor pa yis ni// 'du byed stong pa g.yo ba med par mthong // phung po dag dang skye mched khams rnams ni// nang yang stong la phyi rol ba ni bstan/ 'dod pa'i dga' ba'i yul thams cad la 'dzin pa med par rang gi sems la dbang bsgyur ba ni bstan/ sngon gyi smon lam gyi stobs kyis grogs su gyur pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba bsags pa'i sems can rnams ni mtshungs par gnas pas yongs su smin par byas nas/ 'jig rten gyi kun nas nyon mongs pa'i dri ma thams cad kyis ni sems la kun nas nyon mongs pa med par btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang na gnas te/ ji ltar mgron du gnyer ba'i sems can gyi khams yongs su smin par bya ba'i dus la lta zhing // de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' shin tu rgya cher sngon gyi dam bcas pa rjes su dran no// sangs rgyas dang chos kyang mngon du byed do// smon lam gyi stobs kyang mngon par sgrub bo// sems can rnams la yang snying rje chen po gtong ngo // sems can rab tu thar bar bya bar yang sems so// 'byor pa thams cad kyi mtha' ni rgud pa yin par yang so sor rtog go// 'khor ba la gnod pa dang / 'jigs pa mang po du ma yod par yang rtog go// bdud dang nyes pa'i zhags pa yang yang dag par gcod do// 'khor ba'i rgyud byang chub sems dpa' ni sngon gyi mtha' nyid nas kyang 'khor ba'i skyon shin tu rig pa yin/ 'dus byas la bsam pa thag pa nas don du mi gnyer ba yin/ nye bar len pa yongs su 'dzin pa thams cad don du mi gnyer ba yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos don du gnyer ba yin/ mya ngan las 'das pa la mngon du phyogs pa yin/ 'khor ba la rgyab kyis bltas pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod yul la mngon du dga' ba yin/ bdud kyi spyod yul dang ma 'dres pa yin/ srid pa la 'bar bar skyon du mthong ba yin/ khams gsum pa las byung ba'i bsam pa can yin/ 'khor ba'i skyon dang nyes dmigs dang 'byung ba la mkhas pa yin/ rab tu 'byung bar 'dod pa yin/ mngon par 'byung ba'i bsam pa can yin/ bden pa la gzhol ba yin/ bden pa la 'bab pa yin/ dben pa la bab pa yin/ dgon pa dang bas mthar mngon par dga' ba yin/ rab tu dben pas rab tu zhi bar 'dod pa yin/ bdag dang gzhan la phan par zhugs pa yin/ bla na med pa'i nan tan la dpa' ba yin/ 'jig rten gyi don du 'dod pa yin/ phan par 'dod pa yin/ bde bar 'dod pa yin/ grub pa dang bde bar 'dod pa yin/ 'jig rten la snying brtse ba can yin/ phan par 'dod pa can yin/ byams pa la gnas pa can yin/ snying rje chen po dang ldan pa yin/ bsdu ba'i dngos po la mkhas pa yin/ rtag tu yid yongs su mi skyo ba yin/ sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang 'dul ba la mkhas pa yin/ sems can thams cad la bu gcig pa dang 'dra bar sdug par sems pa yid la byed pa dang ldan pa yin/ dngos po thams cad la mi lta bar yongs su btang ba yin/ sbyin pa 'ged pa la dga' ba yin/ lhug par gtong ba yin/ lag pa brkyang ba yin/ gtong ba la dpa' ba yin/ mchod sbyin byas pa yin/ bsod nams shin tu phun sum tshogs pa yin/ bsod nams kyi yo byad shin tu bzung ba yin/ dri ma dang ser sna dang bral ba yin/ sems kun tu ma bzung ba yin/ bla na med pa'i sbyin bdag chen po yin/ byin nas kyang rnam par smin pa la mi re ba yin/ sbyin pa la dpa' ba yin/ 'dod pa dang / 'dod pa che ba dang / chags pa dang / zhe sdang dang / rgyags pa dang / nga rgyal dang / gti mug dang / ser sna la sogs pa nyon mongs pa'i dgra'i tshogs phyir rgol ba thams cad tshar gcad pa'i phyir mngon par byung ba yin/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems bskyed pa'i rgyun las mi g.yo ba yin/ gtong ba chen po'i sems kyi go cha shin tu bgos pa yin/ 'jig rten la snying brtse ba can yin/ phan par 'dod pa can yin/ ya lad bgos pa yin/ go cha bgos pa yin/ sems can rab tu thar bar bya ba la dmigs pa yin/ snying rje chen po'i stobs dang rnam par gnon pa dang / pha rol gnon pa dang ldan pa yin/ phyir mi ldog pa yin/ sems can thams cad la sems mnyam pa yin/ gtong ba'i lag cha can yin/ sems can gyi bsam pa dang re ba ji lta ba bzhin du tshim par byed pa yin/ byang chub kyi snod du gyur pa yin/ dus dang phyad par chos rtogs pa yin/ smon lam byang chub tu yongs su bsngos pa yin/ rgyal mtshan ma bsnyal ba yin/ 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa'i sbyin pa yongs su gtong ba dang ldan pa yin/ ye shes mchog gi rdo rje'i mtshon cha sra ba dang ldan pa yin/ nyon mongs pa'i phyir rgol ba shin tu tshar gcod pa yin/ tshul khrims dang / yon tan dang / spyod pa dri ma dang bral la dri ma spangs pa'i sems dang ldan pa yin/ ngan du smras pa dang / ngan du brjod pa'i tshig gi lam dang / brgyad pa dang / spyo ba dang / smad pa dang / bshung ba dang / brdeg pa sems pa yin/ gnod pa mi byed pa yin/ gnod sems med pa'i sems dang ldan pa yin/ sems can thams cad la phan par bya ba'i brtson 'grus 'bar ba brtsams pa yin/ yi dam la brten pa yin/ dge ba'i chos thams cad yang dag par sgrub pa la phyir mi ldog pa yin/ dran pa dang ldan pa yin/ shes bzhin can yin/ shin tu mnyam par bzhag pa yin/ sems ma g.yengs pa yin/ bsam gtan la rtse gcig tu yid la byed pa yin/ chos rab tu rnam par 'byed pa la mkhas pa yin/ snang ba thob pa yin/ mun pa mun gnag dang bral ba yin/ mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal ba dang / bdag med pa dang / mi sdug pa'i rnam par sems yongs su bsgoms pa yin/ dran pa nye bar gzhag pa dang / yang dag pa'i spong ba dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa dang / dbang po dang / stobs dang / byang chub kyi yan lag dang / lam dang / byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos thams cad shin tu yongs su sbyang ba byas pa'i yid la byed pa dang ldan pa yin/ zhi gnas dang lhag mthong gis shin tu dkar bar byas pa'i blo dang ldan pa yin/ rten cing 'brel bar 'byung bar lta ba yin/ bden pa rjes su rtogs pas gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa yin/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum gyis rnam par rtse ba yin/ chos thams cad kyi tshul sgyu ma dang / smig rgyu dang / chu zla dang / brag ca dang / mig yor lta bur rtogs pa yin no// dge slong dag byang chub sems dpa' de ni de ltar rang bzhin gyis chos la gnas pa yin/ de ltar ye shes la gnas pa yin/ de ltar yon tan gyi che ba nyid la gnas pa yin/ de ltar sems can gyi don la brtson par gnas pa yin te/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyi byin gyis brlabs pas sil snyan dang glu dbyangs las byung ba'i tshigs su bcad pa de dag gis rgya cher bskul ba dang / de'i tshe sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa' srid pa tha ma par gyur pa rnams kyi btsun mo'i 'khor yongs su smin par bya ba'i phyir chos kyi sgo bzhi mngon du byed do// bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sbyin pa dang / snyan par smra ba dang / don bya ba dang / don 'thun pa bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi la sbyor ba sgrub pa rnam par dag pa zhes bya ba'i chos kyi sgo mngon du byed pa dang / dkon mchog gsum gyi rigs yang dag par 'dzin pa'i bsam pa chud mi za ba'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems smon lam gyi stobs bskyed pa'i phyir mi ldog pa'i yul zhes bya ba'i chos kyi sgo mngon du byed pa dang / sems can thams cad yongs su mi gtang ba'i lhag pa'i bsam pa snying rje chen po'i stobs la zhugs pa zhes bya ba'i chos kyi sgo mngon du byed pa dang / byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos thams cad kyi tshig rab tu dbye ba dang / don la rnam par nges pa'i ye shes kyi tshogs kyi stobs kyi khyad par yang dag par sgrub pa bkod pa chen po zhes bya ba'i chos kyi sgo mngon du byed pa'o// byang chub sems dpas chos kyi sgo bzhi po de dag mngon du byas nas/ btsun mo'i 'khor thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba'i phyir de'i tshe/ rnam pa ji lta bu'i rdzu 'phrul mngon par 'du bya ba mngon par 'dus byas pas byang chub sems dpa'i mthus sil snyan dang glu dbyangs de dag las chos kyi sgo rnam pa 'di lta bu brgya stong 'byung ba de lta bu'i rdzu 'phrul mngon par 'du bya ba mngon par byed do// mos pa rgya chen dang ni bsam pa dang // lhag pa'i bsam dang srog chags snying rje bas// byang chub dam pa'i mchog tu sems skye zhes// de 'dra'i sgra dag sil snyan rnams las byung // dang zhing dad dang mos dang gus pa dang // nga rgyal med cing bla la 'dud pa dang // 'dri dang dgi ba ci zhes tshol ba dang // rjes su dran pa bsgoms pa'i sgra byung ngo // sbyin dang dul dang sdom dang tshul khrims sgra// bzod pa'i sgra dang de bzhin brtson 'grus sgra// bsam gtan mngon par sgrub dang ting 'dzin sgra// shes rab dang ni thabs kyi sgra yang byung // byams pa'i sgra dang de bzhin snying rje'i sgra// dga' dang btang snyoms mngon par shes pa'i sgra// bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi po rnam nges pas// sems can yongs su smin bya'i sgra yang byung // dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rab dbye sgra// yang dag spong dang de bzhin rdzu 'phrul dang // dbang po lnga dang stobs lnga rab dbye dang // byang chub yan lag sgra ni sil snyan byung // yan lag brgyad pa'i 'phags lam mchog dbye dang // zhi gnas sgra dang de bzhin lhag mthong dang // mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal bdag med sgra// mi sdug sgra yang sil snyan rnams las byung // 'dod chags bral sgra de bzhin dben pa'i sgra// zad pa shes pa'i sgra dang mi skye sgra// 'gog pa'i sgra dang de bzhin gnas med sgra// mya ngan 'das pa'i sgra yang sil snyan byung // rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i mthu yis na// snyil snyan dag las 'di 'dra'i sgra byung ste// sgra de thos nas bud med thams cad kyis// sems can mchog rab rjes bslabs byang chub smon// dge slong dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang na 'dug pas bud med brgyad khri bzhi stong dang / lha'i bu brgya stong mang po gang dag der 'dus par gyur pa dag kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su smin par byas par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' mngon par 'byung ba'i dus la bab pa dang / dga' ldan gyi ris kyi lha'i bu khrel yod pa'i lha zhes bya ba bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog pa des mtshan mo mi nyal tsam na/ lha'i bu 'bum phrag sum cu rtsa gnyis kyis bskor cing mdun du bdar te byang chub sems dpa' la rim gro bya ba'i phyir khang ga la ba der song ste phyin nas nam mkha'i dkyil na 'dug ste/ byang chub sems dpa' la tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ shi 'pho ba ni shin tu bstan// skyes bu seng ges tshe yang bstan// btsun mo'i 'khor yang bstan pa mdzad// khyod kyis 'jig rten rjes 'thun mdzad// 'jig rten chos ni rjes thob pas// lha mi mang po yongs smin mdzad// mngon par 'byung ba'i blo dgongs pa'i// de yi dus la deng bab bo// ma grol bas ni dgrol mi nus// long bas lam yang ston mi nus// grol bas dgrol bar byed par nus// mig ldan long ba lam ston nus// sems can gang dag 'dod pas 'khol// khyim nor bu dang chung ma chags// de dag khyod kyi rjes slob cing // mngon par 'byung bar bzhed par mdzod// dbang phyug 'dod pas rtse ba dang // gling bzhi rin chen bdun spangs te// khyod ni mngon par 'byung rig nas// lha mir bcas pa'i 'jig rten mos// khyod ni 'dod la mi dgyes te// bsam gtan bde bas gnas mdzad kyang // lha mi brgya phrag mang po dag // gnyid kyis log las sad par mdzad// dar la bab 'di shin tu 'da'// ri gzar 'bab chu mgyogs 'gro bzhin// dar la bab pa yal gyur nas// mngon par 'byung ba mdzes ma lags// de slad thog mar gzhon pa'i tshe// dar bab dam par mngon byung ste// thugs dam nyams 'og chud mdzod la// lha mi don ni mdzad pa'i rigs// 'dod pa'i yon tan mi ngoms te// dper na lan tshwa'i chu dang mtshungs// 'phags pa rdul med 'jig rten 'das// shes rab gang ldan de dag ngoms// khyod 'dir rgyal po zas gtsang dang // yul 'khor rnams kyi yid 'ong sdug // 'dab ma brgya pa'i zhal 'dra ba// mngon par 'byung bar dgongs su gsol// nyon mongs gdung bas rab gdungs shing // 'byung med bcing bas dam bcings rnams// dpa' bos myur du mtshungs med pa// thar lam zhi la dgong du gsol// khyod ni sman pa khams la mkhas// sems can yun ring na rnams la// chos kyi sman ni sbyor mdzad de// mya ngan 'das bde myur du khod// mig med mun pa gti mug glags// lta ba'i dra bas dkris pa yi// lha rnams dang ni mi yi mig // shes rab sgron ma myur du sbyongs// byang chub thob par blta bya zhing // bla na med pa'i chos mnyan ces// lha dang lha min klu dag dang // gnod sbyin dri za mang po sdod// klu yi rgyal pos rang gi gnas// khyod kyi dpal gyis snang bar mthong // mchod pa dag ni mtha' yas bgyid// de yi brtul zhugs bsam pa skongs// byang chub shing drung yid rdzogs la// lhung bzed bzhi ni dbul lo zhes// 'jig rten skyong bzhi sder bcas pa// de dag khyod la sdod cing mchis// tshangs pa rab tu zhi spyod pa// byams ldan snying rje thob pa yang // bla med 'khor lo rab skor bar// mi dbang gsol snyam sdod cing mchis// byang chub bsnyen bkur byed pa'i lha// byang chub snying por gnas rnams kyang // byang chub rnam par 'tshang rgya ba// blta'o zhes te sdod cing mchis// byang chub sems dpa' btsun mo'i nang // bya ba ston pa gzhan yang mchis// de dag thog mar khyod gyur mdzod// de dag 'og tu lus sa re// dbyangs snyan cing ni dbyangs 'jam pa// mar me mdzad kyis lung bstan dgongs// yang dag de bzhin ma nor ba// rgyal ba'i sgra dbyangs bsgrag tu gsol// bskul ba'i le'u ste/ bcu gsum pa'o// // dge slong dag de ltar lha'i bu des byang chub sems dpa' bskul ma thag tu rgyal po zas gtsang ma la rmi lam 'di bstan to// rgyal po zas gtsang ma gnyid kyis log pa'i rmi lam du rmis pa/ byang chub sems dpa' mtshan mo mi nyal tsam na/ lha'i tshogs kyis bskor te mngon par 'byung zhing mngon par byung nas kyang rab tu byung ste/ gos ngur smrig gyon pa rmis so// de nas de sad pa dang / rings pa rings par nyung rum la dris pa/ gzhon nu btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang na 'dug gam/ des smras pa lha bzhugs so// de nas rgyal po zas gtsang ma 'di snyam du/ gzhon nu ni gdon mi za bar mngon par 'byung bar 'gyur te/ snga ltas su snang ba ni 'di dag yin snyam nas/ khong pa'i snying la mya ngan gyi zug rngus zug par gyur to// de yang 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gi gzhon nu ni skyed mos tshal gyi sar yang nam yang 'gro bar mi 'gyur te/ bud med kyi tshogs kyi nang na mngon par dga' bas 'di nyid du chags par 'gyur te/ mngon par 'byung bar ni mi 'gyur ro snyam mo// de nas rgyal po zas gtsang ma gzhon nu'i longs spyod kyi phyir/ dpyid dang / dbyar dang / ston gyi dus ji lta ba bzhin du khang gsum byed du bcug go// de la dpyid sa gang yin pa de ni shin tu bsil ba'o// dbyar sa gang yin pa de ni grang dro ran pa'o// dgun sa gang yin pa de ni rang bzhin gyis dro ba'o// khang re re'i gru skas rnams kyang mi lnga brgya lnga brgyas 'dzugs shing 'bebs so// de dag de ltar 'dzugs shing 'bebs pa na gzhon nu sus kyang ma tshor bar mngon par byung bar 'gyur du 'ong ngo zhes sgra dpag tshad phyed du grag pa byung ngo // ltas pa dang mtshan mkhan kun gyis kyang // gzhon nu ni chab sgo bkra shis pa nas mngon par 'byung bar 'gyur ro// zhes lung bstan to// de nas rgyal pos bkra shis kyi sgo'i sgo 'phar chen po byed du bcug ste/ sgo 'phar re re yang mi lnga brgya lnga brgyas 'byed cing gcod do// de dag gi sgra yang dpag tshad phyed du grag go// de la 'dod pa'i yon tan mtshungs pa med pa yang sbyor ro// glu dang rol mo'i sgra dbyangs len pa dang / gar byed pa'i na chung dag kyang rtag tu bzhag par gyur to// dge slong dag de nas byang chub sems dpas kha lo sgyur ba la smras pa/ deng skyed mos tshal gyi sar 'gros shing rta myur du sbyor cig // de nas kha lo sgyur ba rgyal po zas gtsang ma'i gan du song ste 'di skad ces smras so// lha gzhon nu skyed mos tshal gyi sar 'byung ngo zhes gsung ngo // de nas rgyal po zas gtsang ma 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gis gzhon nu skyed mos tshal gyi sar nam yang ma phyung bas sa bzang po blta bar bya ba'i phyir bdag gis gzhon nu skyed mos tshal gyi sar phyung na 'on tang gzhon nu bud med kyi tshogs kyis bskor te dga' ba myong bar 'gyur bas/ mngon par mi 'byung ngo snyam mo// de nas rgyal po zas gtsang ma byang chub sems dpa' la byams pa dang / rim gro byed pas da ste zhag bdun na gzhon nu sa bzang po blta ba'i phyir skyed mos tshal gyi sar 'byung gis/ der khyed kyis gzhon nu'i mig tu mi 'ong ba mthong bar mi 'gyur bar yid du mi 'ong ba thams cad ni sol cig // yid du 'ong ba dang / yul nyams dga' ba thams cad ni sbyor cig ces grong khyer du dril bsgrags so// de nas zhag bdun gyi nyin par grong khyer thams cad brgyan to// skyed mos tshal yang mdzes par byas te/ ras bcos bu kha dog tha dad pa'i bla re ni bres/ gdugs dang rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan gyis ni legs par brgyan to// byang chub sems dpa' lam gang nas 'gro ba'i lam de yang chag chag btab ste phyags nas/ spos chu'i chag chag btab ste/ me tog sil ma ni chal par bkram/ pog phor nas ni bdugs/ bum pa gang bas ni mdzes par byas/ chu shing ljon pa ni bsgreng // dar tha dad pa sna tshogs kyi bla re ni bres/ rin po che'i dril bu g.yer ka'i dra ba dang / rgyan phreng dang chun po ni spyangs/ dpung bzhi'i bkod pa ni byas so// g.yog 'khor kyang gzhon nu'i btsun mo'i 'khor brgyan pa'i phyir brtson par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' bkod pa chen pos grong khyer gyi shar phyogs kyi sgo nas skyed mos tshal gyi sar byung ngo // de nas byang chub sems dpa' nyid kyi mthus gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu rnams kyis mi rgan po gtugs pa/ 'khogs pa/ lus las rtsa rgyus 'thon pa/ so rgal ba/ lus gnyer mas gang ba/ skra byi ba/ sgur ba gdung rten ltar dgu ba/ zhom pa/ 'khar ba la rten pa/ mthu zad pa/ dar yal ba/ mid pa nas sgra ngar ngar po 'byung ba/ lus sgu bas 'khar ba la brten nas yan lag dang nying lag thams cad 'dar ba zhig lam kar bstan par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpas shes bzhin du kha lo sgyur ba la 'di skad ces smras so// kha lo sgyur ba mi rid nyam chung zhing // sha khrag skams la rgyus lpags nyi tshes dkris// mgo dkar so rgal lus ni rab skem la// 'khar ba brten cing mi bder 'khyor 'gros su// kha lo sgyur bas smras pa/ lha cig mi 'di rga bas zil gyis non// dbang po nyams shing sdug bsngal brtson stobs nyams// gnyen gyi skye bos brnyas shing mgon med gyur// don bgyid mi nus nags khrod shing ltar bor// byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ 'di yi chos 'di rigs kyi yin nam 'on tam ni// 'gro ba 'di kun la yang 'di srid de smros shig // tshig 'di yang dag ji bzhin myur du smros shig dang // thos nas de bzhin don la 'dir ni tshul bzhin bsam// kha lo sgyur bas smras pa/ lha 'di rigs chos ma lags yul 'khor chos ma lags// skye bo kun gyi dar la bab pa rga bas 'joms// khyod kyi yab dang yum dang nye du gnyen tshogs kyang // rga las mthar 'gro ba yi thabs ni gzhan ma mchis// byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ kha lo sgyur ba byis pa'i skye bo mi mkhas pa'i// blo ngan gzhon pas rgyags shing myos pas rga ma mthong // nga ni slar 'gro nga yi shing rta myur du sgyur// nga yang rga la gnas pas rtse dga' sa ci zhig bya// de nas byang chub sems dpa' shing rta'i mchog de slar bsgyur te phyir grong khyer du zhugs so// dge slong dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' dus gzhan zhig na/ bkod pa chen pos grong khyer gyi lho phyogs kyi sgo nas skyed mos tshal gyi sar zhugs pa dang / des lam ka na mi nad kyis nyen pa/ dmu rdzing can lus nyam chung ba/ rang gi gcinaskyag tu bying ba/ mgon med pa/ skyabs med pa/ shin tu sha thang bar dbugs dbyung zhing brngub dgos pa zhig mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang yang byang chub sems dpas shes bzhin du kha lo sgyur ba la 'di skad ces smras so// kha lo sgyur ba mi rtsub lus kyi mdog ngan la// dbang po thams cad nyams shing dbugs dbyung rab tu dka'// yan lag kun skams lto bas dkrugs shing nyam thag gyur// rang gi gcin rtug smad pa'i gnas na 'dug 'di su// kha lo sgyur bas smras pa/ lha cig mi 'di shin tu nad kyis btab pa ste// nad kyi 'jigs pa nye bar mchis pas 'gum la thug // nad med gzi brjid ma mchis stobs kyang rnam par nyams// mgon dang skyabs dang gling dang dpung gnyen ma mchis lags// byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ nad med pa yang rmi lam na ni rtse dang mtshungs// nad kyi 'jigs pa 'di ltar shin tu mi bzad pa// skyes bu mkhas pas gnas 'di mthong nas ji lta bur// rtse la dga' dang sdug pa'i 'du shes bskyed par 'gyur// dge slong dag de nas byang chub sems dpa' shing rta'i mchog de slar bsgyur te phyir yang grong khyer du zhugs so// dge slong dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' dus gzhan zhig na bkod pa chen pos grong khyer gyi nub phyogs kyi sgo nas skyed mos tshal gyi sar zhugs pa dang / des lam ka na mi shi bar gyur pa/ khyogs la bzhag pa/ ras kyi bla re phub pa/ nye du'i tshogs kyis bskor te/ kun kyang ngu zhing skad phyung ste/ ngu la smre sngags 'don cing skra bshig la mgo las sa 'thor zhing brang rdung la cho nge 'don cing phyi bzhin 'brang bar gyur pa mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang yang byang chub sems dpas shes bzhin du kha lo sgyur ba la 'di skad ces smras so// kha lo sgyur ba mi 'di khyogs la bzhag nas ni// mi dag skra bshig mgo la sa yis 'thor byed cing // sna tshogs dag gi tshig ni brjod la brang rdung bas// kun nas bskor ba byas te khyer ba su zhig yin// kha lo sgyur bas smras pa/ lha cig mi 'di 'dzam bu'i gling du gum pa ste// slan chad pha ma mchis brang bu rnams mthong mi 'gyur// longs spyod khyim dang mdza' gnyen tshogs rnams spangs nas ni// 'jig rten pha rol mchis te slan chad gnyen mi mthong // byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ rga bas gnod par 'gyur ba'i gzhon pa cir mi rung // sna tshogs nad kyis gnod 'gyur nad med cir mi rung // ring du mi gson gson pa mkhas la cir mi rung // rga la chags pa skyes bu mkhas la cir mi rung // gal te rga med nad med 'chi ba med gyur kyang // 'on kyang phung po lnga 'dzin sdug bsngal che yin na// rga na 'chi ba rtag tu 'brang ba smos ci dgos// legs par slar zlog rab tu thar bar bya ba bsam// dge slong dag de nas byang chub sems dpa' shing rta mchog de slar bzlog ste/ phyir yang grong khyer du zhugs so// dge slong dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' dus gzhan zhig na grong khyer gyi byang phyogs kyi sgo nas skyed mos tshal gyi sar zhugs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i mthus lha'i bu de dag nyid kyis lam ka der dge slong zhig mngon par sprul pa dang / byang chub sems dpas dge slong zhi ba/ dul ba yang dag par bsdams pa/ tshangs par spyod pa/ mig phab pa/ gnya' shing gang tsam du lta ba/ spyod lam mdzes pa phun sum tshogs pa/ 'gro ba dang ldog pa mdzes pa phun sum tshogs pa/ mdun du lta ba dang / g.yas g.yos su lta ba mdzes pa/ bskum pa dang smyang ba mdzes pa/ chos gos snam sbyar dang lhung bzed dang chos gos thogs pa mdzes pa zhig lam ka na 'dug pa de mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang byang chub sems dpas shes bzhin du kha lo sgyur ba la 'di skad ces smras so// kha lo sgyur ba skyes bu sems zhi rab zhi zhing // mig phab 'gro la gnya' shing gang tsam lta byed cing // ngur smrig gos gyon shin tu rab tu zhi bar spyod// lhung bzed thogs nas mi rgod ma khengs su zhig yin// kha lo sgyur bas smras pa/ lha cig mi 'di dge slong zhes ni bgyi ba lags// 'dod pa'i dga' ba spangs shing shin tu dul bar spyod// bdag nyid zhi ba tshol zhing rab tu byung bar gyur// 'dod chags zhe sdang bral bar bsod snyoms spyod cing rgyu// byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ 'di ni dge bar legs smras nga yang 'dod pa ste// rab tu byung ba mkhas pa rnams kyis rtag tu bsngags// de ni bdag la phan zhing sems can gzhan la'ang phan// 'tsho ba bde zhing nyams 'thun 'chi med 'bras bur 'gyur// dge slong dag de nas byang chub sems dpas shing rta mchog de slar bsgyur te phyir yang grong khyer du zhugs so// dge slong dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' la bskul ba rnam pa 'di lta bu 'di dag rgyal po zas gtsang mas mthong zhing thos nas/ byang chub sems dpa' yongs su bsrung ba'i phyir ra ba rgya chen po byed du bcug ste/ 'obs kyang rkor bcug // sgo gtan dam po yang 'dzugs su bcug // srungs ma yang bkod/ dpa' bo rnams kyang sbran/ bzhon pa yang sta gon byas/ go cha yang gyon du bcug go// byang chub sems dpa' bsrung ba'i phyir/ grong khyer chen po'i sgo bzhi'i lam gyi sum mdo rnams su dpung chen po'i bkod pa bzhag ste/ byang chub sems dpa' mngon par byung nga re zhes de dag de srung du bcug go// btsun mo'i 'khor la yang res 'ga' tsam yang glu dbyangs kyi rgyun chad da re/ dga' ba dang rtse ba thams cad kyang sbyor cig // ci nas kyang gzhon nu chags nas rab tu 'byung bar mi 'gyur ba dang / mgu bar 'gyur bar bud med kyi sgyu yang ston cig ces bsgo'o// de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ thab mo mos pa'i skyes bu lag na ral gri mtshon thogs sgo gar bkod// go bgos mi rta glang po shing rta mi bskyon glang po'i phreng ba'ang bkod// 'obs dang shing thags dag dang rta babs phyir mthon po'ang byed du bcug // sgo mo rgyang grags grag pa'i sgra 'byung ba yang gtan pa dam po bcug // shAkya'i tshogs rnams thams cad yid mi dga' zhing nyin mtshan srung bar byed// dpung chen de dag rnams kyang sgra skad chen po shin tu grag par byed// des pa 'di nas 'byung du 'ong zhes grong khyer 'khrugs shing yid sngangs skrag // shAkya'i rigs skyes song na rigs 'di chad par mi 'gyur grang snyam byed// skye bo bud med dag la bsgo ba rtag tu glu dbyangs rgyun ma bcad// rtse bas dga' ba rnams kyi bsnyen bkur gyis shing yid kyang mgu bar gyis// bud med sgyu thabs spyod pa gang yin rnam pa du ma mang po ston// des pa 'gror mi 'gyur bar bsrung bar byos shing bgegs kyang rab tu byos// kha lo sgyur ba mchog de mngon par 'byung ba'i snga ltas 'di dag ste// ngang pa khrung khrung dag dang rma bya ri skegs dag dang ne tsho rnams// khang skar khung rta babs mchog dang yang thog khri la 'khod nas ni// dman zhing dman la mi dga' mi bde mgo smad sems shing sgra mi 'byin// rdzing dang rdzing chen dag gi pad ma dag kyang rnyis shing rnyis par gyur// shing ljon skams shing yal ga me tog lhags la me tog slar mi 'chags// pi bang gling bu rgyud gsum rgyud kyis brgyan pa de tshe glo bur chad// rnga dang rdza rnga dag kyang lag pas brdungs na 'chags cing sgra mi 'byung // grong khyer de dag thams cad 'khrugs par gyur cing shin tu gnyid kyis non// gang gi yid kyang gar byed pa dang glu len pa la dga' ba med// rgyal po'ang mchog tu rab tu yid dman gyur te sems khongs chud cing 'dug // e ma ma rung shAka rigs rdzu 'phrul rgya chen mi tshig grang snyam byed// sa 'tsho ma dang rgyal bu mal gcig na ni nyal zhing 'khod pa'i tshe// nam phyed tsam na sa 'tsho ma yi rmi lam du ni 'di dag rmis// sa 'di thams cad rtse mor ldan pa'i ri dang bcas te g.yos par gyur// shing ljon rnams kyang rlung gis bskyod nas rtsa nas 'thon te sa la sgyel// nyi ma zla ba skar ma'i rgyan dang bcas te mkha' las sa la lhung // lag pa g.yon pas skra yang rab tu 'bal zhing cod pan lhung ba mthong // lag pa chad la de bzhin rkang pa'ang chad cing bdag ni sgren mor mthong // bdag gi mu tig do shal nor bu gser gyi 'og pag chad par mthong // nyal khri de yi rkang pa bzhi chag sa yi steng na nyal ba mthong // rgyal po'i gdugs kyi yu ba spras pa dpal ldan mdzes pa chag par mthong // rgyan rnams kun kyang rnam par 'thor cing chu yis khyer bar gyur pa dang // khyim thab rgyan yang gos dang cod pan bcas te mal steng 'thor bar mthong // grong khyer dag nas me sgron phyir byung grong khyer mun pas non pa dang // rin po che las byas pa'i dra ba mdzes pa'ang chad par gyur pa rmis// mu tig do shal 'phyang ba lhung nas rgya mtsho chen pos dkrugs pa dang // de yi tshe na ri yi rgyal po ri rab gnas nas g.yos pa rmis// shAkya'i bu mo'i rmi lam du ni 'di 'dra 'di dag rmis gyur nas// de sad mig nas mchi ma zag cing rang gi khyo la 'di skad smras// lha cig rmi lam 'di 'dra rmis pa cir 'gyur ba ni bka' stsol cig // bdag ni dran pa 'khrul cing mig kyang 'khrul la yid ni mya ngan non// de yis de thos ka la ping ka rnga sgra tshangs dbyangs sgra snyan pas// sa 'tsho ma la smras pa khyod ni rab tu dgar 'gyur sdig pa med// sems can gang dag bsod nams sngon spyad de dag rmi lam 'di 'dra rmi// sdug bsngal du mas nyen pa rmi lam 'di 'dra rmi ba ga la yod// khyod kyis sa ni rab tu g.yos pa dang // ri rtser bcas te sa la lhung rmis pa// lha dang klu dang srin po 'byung po'i tshogs// kun gyis khyod mchod gtso mor byed par 'gyur// khyod kyis shing rnams rtsa nas 'thon rmis shing // lag pa g.yon pas skra 'bal rmis pa ni// sa 'tsho myur du nyon mongs dra ba bcad// 'dus byas dag las lta ba'i dra ba 'byin// khyod kyis nyi zla sa la lhung rmis shing // skar ma rnams kyang lhung bar rmis pa ni// sa 'tsho myur du nyon mongs dgra bcom ste// khyod ni 'jig rten mchod pa bsngags par 'gyur// khyod kyis mu tig do shal 'thor rmis shing // lus kun chad dang sgren mo rmis pa ni// sa 'tsho myur du bud med lus spangs te// ring por mi thogs skyes pa'i lus su 'gyur// khyod kyis khri rkang chag par rmis pa dang // gdugs yu rin chen spras pa chag rmis pa// sa 'tsho myur du chu bo bzhi rgal cing // nga ni 'jig rten gdugs gcig 'gyur ba mthong // khyod kyis rgyan rnams chus khyer rmis pa dang // nga yi gos dang cod pan khri steng rmis// sa mtsho myur du mtshan gyis brgyan nas ni// 'jig rten kun gyis nga la bstod pa mthong // khyod kyis mar me brgya phrag bye ba dag // grong khyer byung nas mun gnag gyur rmis pa// sa 'tsho myur du ma rig rmongs pa'i mun// 'jig rten kun la shes rab snang byed 'gyur// khyod kyis mu tig do shal chad pa dang // gser gyi tsong tsong spras pa chad rmis pa// sa 'tsho myur du nyon mongs dra bcad de// 'dus byas dag las 'du shes skud pa 'byin// sa 'tsho gang phyir nga la gus par ni// rtag tu rim gro mchog gis mchod byed na// khyod la ngan 'gro med cing mya ngan med// myur du dga' zhing mchog tu dga' ba 'thob// ngas ni sngon chad sbyin pa gya nom byin// tshul khrims bsrungs dang rtag tu bzod pa bsgoms// de bas nga la dad pa gang rnyed pa// de dag thams cad dga' zhing rab dga' rnyed// 'khor bar bskal pa bye ba mtha' yas su// ngas ni byang chub lam mchog rnam par sbyangs// de bas nga la dad pa gang byed pa// de dag thams cad ngan song gsum po chad// dga' ba 'thob kyis mi dga' ma skyed cig // tshim pa thob par gyis la mgu skyed cig // dga' dang mchog tu dga' ba myur 'thob ste// khyod kyi rmi ltas bzang gis sa 'tsho nyol// sngon chad dge ba'i las ni gang dag bsags gyur pa// mi mchog rnams ni mngon par 'byung ba'i dus bab tshe// mtshan ma 'di dag bsod nams gzi brjid bsags pa dang // dpal gyi gzi brjid snying po can des rmi bar 'gyur// de ni rkang pa dag dang lag pa chen po yis// rgya mtsho chen po bzhi po dag gi chu dkrug dang // sa 'di thams cad sna tshogs mal char gyur pa dang // ri bo lhun po mchog kyang sngas su gyur pa rmi// rmi lam na ni 'od rab bkye bas 'jig rten na// mun pa mun nag chen po rnam par bsal ba dang // sa las gdugs shig byung bas 'jig rten gsum khyab dang // 'od kyis reg pas log lhung sdug bsngal rab zhi rmi// dkar nag srog chags bzhi zhig rkang pa ldag pa dang // kha dog bzhi pa'i bya 'ongs kha dog gcig sgyur dang // mchog tu ngan pa smad pa ngan skyugs ri la yang // 'dzegs nas 'gro yang de na gos pa med pa rmi// rmi lam na ni chu bo chu yis rab gang nas// srog chags bye ba khrag khrig mang po khyer ba las// der ni grur byas bsgral te gzhan dag bsgral nas ni// de yis 'jigs med mya ngan med mchog thang bkod rmi// rmi lam na ni nad pa mang po nad btab pa// nad med gzi brjid bral zhing stobs kyang nyams rnams la// de ni sman par gyur nas rtsi sman mang byin pas// nad btab sems can khrag khrig mang po thar byed rmi// ri rab ngos la seng ge'i khri la 'dug nas ni// slob ma thal mo sbyar cing lha rnams phyag 'tshal la// bdag ni g.yul las rgyal zhing lha rnams nam mkha' las// kun tu dga' ba'i sgra sgrog par ni rmi lam rmi// bkra shis brtul zhugs bzang po yongs su rdzogs par yang // byang chub sems dpa' rmi lam rnam pa de dag rmi// de thos nas ni 'di ni ring por mi thogs par// mi dang lha yi lhar 'gyur snyam ste lha mi dga'// rmi lam gyi le'u ste/ bcu bzhi pa'o// // dge slong dag de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gis rgyal po chen po zas gtsang ma la yang ma byas shing // phas gnang ba med par mngon par 'byung ba 'di ni bdag la mi rigs te/ byas pa gzo ba ma yin par 'gyur ro snyam nas/ de mtshan mo mi nyal tsam na rang gi gnas kyi khang nas byung ste/ rgyal po zas gtsang ma'i khang phyin nas 'dug go// byang chub sems dpa' 'dug ma thag tu khang thams cad kyang 'od kyis gsal bar gyur to// de nas rgyal po sad pa dang / 'od de mthong ste mthong nas kyang myur ba myur bar nyung rum la smras pa/ kye nyung rum ci nyi ma shar tam/ gang gis na 'di 'od kyis rnam par mdzes/ nyung rum gyis smras pa/ lha da dung du dgung phyed kyang ma bas so// lha gzhan yang nyi ma'i 'od ni shing dang rtsig pa thal mi phyin// lus la gdung bar bgyid cing tsha bar rab tu bgyid// nang par dus na ngang pa dag dang rma bya dang // ne tsho khu byug ngur pa dag kyang rang sgra 'byin// 'od 'di lha mi'i yid du mchi zhing bde ba ste// rab tu sim bgyid dge bgyid gdung bar bgyid ma lags// shing dang rtsig pa thal phyung sgrib pa yong ma mchis// yon tan ldan pa gcig cig deng ni 'dir byon nges// rgyal po de ni mi dga' phyogs bcur bltas pa dang // sems can dag pa pad ma'i mig can de mthong nas// de ni mal nas ldang bar 'dod na ma nus te// rnam dag blo can dam pa pha la gus pa bskyed// de ni rgyal po'i mdun du 'dug nas 'di skad smras// lha cig bdag ni mngon par 'byung ba'i dus bab rigs// bgegs kyang ma mdzad mi dgyes pa yang ma mdzad cig // rgyal po gnyen bcas yul 'khor bcas te bzod par gsol// rgyal po de ni mchi mas mig gang 'di skad smras// khyod ni phyir ldog pa yi dgos pa ci zhig yod// bdag la dam pa ci slong smros shig thams cad sbyin// bdag dang pho brang 'khor dang yul 'khor 'di phan thogs// de'i tshe byang chub sems dpas snyan pa'i tshig smras pa/ lha cig dam pa bzhi 'tshal de ni bdag la stsol// gal te stsal bar spyod na mnga' ni khyod la mchis// 'on tang rtag tu khyim na gzims shing 'byung mi 'gyur// lha cig bdag ni rga bas tshugs par mi 'gyur zhing // rtag tu mdog bzang dar la bab par gnas pa dang // nad ma mchis pa thob cing nad kyis mi btab dang // tshe dpag ma mchis pa dang rgud par mi 'gyur 'tshal// rgyal pos tshig thos shin tu sdug bsngal nyam thag ste// gzhon nu gnas min slong bas bdag la mthu med do// bskal par gnas pa'i drang srong rnams kyang nam du yang // rga na 'chi ba'i 'jigs dang rgud las ma thar to// rga na 'chi ba'i 'jigs dang rgud par mi 'gyur ba// lha cig gal te mchog bzhi 'di dag mi stsol na// gzhan yang mchog cig gsol gyis rgyal po gsan du gsol// 'di nas shi 'phos nying mtshams sbyor bar mi 'gyur mdzod// mi yi dam pa'i tshig ni de skad thos pa dang // sred pa bsrabs te bu la chags pa yongs su gcod// phan byed 'gro ba thar byed rjes su yi rang ngo // khyod kyi bsam pa rnams ni yongs su rdzogs gyur cig // dge slong dag de nas byang chub sems dpa' slar song ste/ rang gi khyim du phyin nas mal na 'dug pa dang / de song ba'am 'ongs par sus kyang ma tshor ro// dge slong dag de'i nam nangs pa dang / rgyal po zas gtsang mas shAkya'i tshogs thams cad bsogs te de'i lo rgyus rnams smos nas/ gzhon nu ni mngon par 'byung na da ji ltar bya zhes smras so// shAkya rnams kyis smras pa/ lha bsrung bar bgyi'o// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ shAkya'i tshogs 'di ni mang la/ de ni gcig pur gyur pas mthus mngon par 'byung ba'i nus pa de la ma mchis so// de nas shAkya de dag dang rgyal po zas gtsang mas shAkya gzhon nu 'thab chos sbyangs pa/ 'os su gyur pa/ 'phong bslabs pa/ tshan po che chen po'i stobs dang ldan pa lnga brgya byang chub sems dpa' bsrung ba'i phyir grong khyer gyi shar sgor bkod de/ byang chub sems dpa' bsrung ba'i phyir shAkya gzhon nu re re la yang 'khor shing rta lnga brgya lnga brgya dang / shing rta re re la yang 'khor dpung bu chung lnga brgya lnga brgya bkod do// byang chub sems dpa' bsrung ba'i phyir/ de bzhin du grong khyer gyi lho dang nub dang byang gi sgor yang shAkya gzhon nu 'thab chos sbyangs pa 'os su gyur pa/ 'phong bslabs pa tshan po che chen po'i stobs dang ldan pa lnga brgya lnga brgya dang / shAkya gzhon nu re re la yang 'khor shing rta lnga brgya lnga brgya dang / shing rta re re la yang 'khor dpung bu chung lnga brgya lnga brgya bkod do// byang chub sems dpa' bsrung ba'i phyir shAkya rgan rabs rgan rabs rnams kyang lam gyi bzhi mdo dang / sum mdo dang / lam po che mang po thams cad na gdod cing 'khod do// rgyal po zas gtsang ma yang shAkya gzhon nu lnga brgyas bskor cing mdun gyis bltas te/ rta dang glang po che dag la zhon nas rang gi khyim sgo na mel tshe byed do// skye dgu'i bdag mo chen mo gau ta mIs kyang rang gi bran mo'i tshogs la smras pa/ mar me dri ma med pa bus la nor bu thams cad rgyal mtshan rtse mor thogs// mu tig rgyan phreng rnams kyang spyangs la khyim 'di kun tu 'od kyis snang bar byos// glu dbyangs dag kyang sbyor la do mod g.yel ba med par mel tshe dam du gyis// gzhon nu ci nas ma tshor bar ni 'gro bar mi 'gyur tshul du bsrung ba gyis// go bgos lag na lag cha ral gri dang // mdung thung mda' dang mtshon cha rtse gnyis thogs// sdug pa'i bu ni bsrung bar bya ba'i phyir// kun kyang rab tu bsgrim pa chen po gyis// sgo kun chod la gtan par dam du chud// sgo 'phar sra ba rked par gtan chug la// dus la ma bab par ni sgo ma dbye// sems can dam pa 'di ni shor ta re// nor bu do shal mu tig do shal thogs// me tog zla gam seng ge shing lo ris// ska rags sor gdub rna rgyan chings shing thogs// rkang gdub dag kyang shin tu legs par thogs// lha mi phan pa glang po dregs bzhin 'gro// gal te blo bur mngon par byung da re// ci nas mi bde rnyed par ma gyur par// de lta de ltar nan tan cher gyis shig // bud med gang dag mdung thung thogs pa dag // dri ma med pa mal na 'dug pa bskor// ci nas gnyid kyis log par ma gyur par// phye ma leb bzhin mig gis bsrung bar gyis// rgyal bu 'di ni bsrung bar bya ba'i phyir// khyim 'dir rin po che yi dra ba bres// gling bu dag kyang rab tu 'bud cing long // do mod rdul dang bral ba bsrung ba gyis// phan tshun gcig la gcig ni sbron byos te// do mod ma nyal shin tu bsrung ba gyis// rgyal srid dang ni yul 'khor spangs nas su// khyim nas mngon du 'byung bar gyur ta re// 'di ni mngon par byung bar gyur na go// rgyal po'i pho brang 'di kun nyams mi dga'// rgyal po'i rigs rgyud yun ring gnas pa yang // rgyal po'i rigs dang rgyud ni chad par 'gyur// dge slong dag de nas gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon lnga rtsen la sogs pa gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po nyi shu rtsa brgyad dang / 'phrog ma'i bu lnga brgya rnams gcig tu 'dus nas 'di skad ces smras te/ grogs po dag do mod byang chub sems dpa' mngon par 'byung gis khyed cag de la mchod pa byed pa'i las la spro bgyis shig // rgyal po chen po bzhi yang lcang lo can gyi pho brang du zhugs nas gnod sbyin gyi 'khor chen po la smras pa/ grogs po dag do mod byang chub sems dpa' mngon par 'byung gis khyed kyis bcibs pa'i rkang lag nas theg la 'byung bar gyis shig // gnod sbyin gyi 'khor gyis smras pa/ sku ni sred med bu yi stobs ldan rdo rje lta bur mi phyed sra la lci// sems can kun gyi dam pa de ni brtson 'grus stobs ldan g.yo ba mi mnga' ste// ri yi dam pa lhun po chen po rmang nas phyung ste nam mkhar gzung nus kyi// rgyal po'i yon tan lhun po ri lci bsod nams ye shes gnas pa sus kyang gang du bkur mi nus// rnam thos kyi bus smras pa/ mi gang nga rgyal 'gying ba de la ston pa lci// gang dag dga' gus gnas pa de dag yang bar tshor// bsam pa thag pas brtson par byos la gus pa yis// bya yis sha kham bzhin du yang bar shes par gyis// kho bo mdun nas 'gro yis khyed cag rnams kyis bcibs pa theg // byang chub sems dpa' mngon par 'byung tshe bsod nams mang po // dge slong dag de nas lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams la smras pa/ kye grogs po dag do mod byang chub sems dpa' mngon par 'byung gis de la khyed thams cad mchod pa'i las la spro bar gyis shig // de na lha'i bu zhi ba'i blo gros zhes bya ba des 'di skad ces smras so// bdag gis ni ser skya'i gnas kyi grong khyer chen po'i skyes pa dang / bud med dang khye'u dang bu mo thams cad gnyid kyis log par bgyi'o// lha'i bu rtse ba bkod pa zhes bya ba des 'di skad ces smras so// bdag gis ni rta dang glang po che dang / bong bu dang / rnga mo dang / ba lang dang / ma he dang / skyes pa dang / bud med dang /
