rmi lam ltar lta ba phyin ci log gis yongs su zin pa/ rgya mtsho dgang dka' ba ltar ngoms mi shes par byed pa/ tshwa chu ltar skom par byed pa/ sbrul gyi mgo ltar reg par bya dka' ba/ g.yang sa chen po ltar mkhas pa rnams kyis yongs su spangs pa/ shes rab can rnams kyis 'jigs pa dang bcas pa dang / rtsod pa dang bcas pa dang / nyes pa dang bcas pa dang / skyon dang bcas par shes nas rnam par spangs pa/ rig pa rnams kyis smad pa/ 'phags pa rnams kyis bshungs pa/ mkhas pa rnams kyis ma bsngags pa/ mi mkhas pa rnams kyis yongs su bzung ba/ byis pa rnams kyis bsten pa yin no// de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di yang smras so// mkhas pa rnams kyis sbrul gyi mgo bzhin spangs// ngan skyugs snod bzhin mi gtsang rnam par spangs// 'dun pa dge ba thams cad 'jig byed par// 'dod pa shes nas nga ni dga' mi skye// de'i tshe 'dun pa zug rngus zug pa bzhin du skad phyung ste/ ngu zhing de nas mig nas mchi ma zag la/ sdug bsngal bzhin tshig 'di skad ces smras so// lha cig gang gi don du 'di na kha cig brtul zhugs rnam pa mang po rtsom ste pags pa 'chang // skra dang sen mo ag tsom ring du 'jog cing de bzhin shing shun gyon la yan lag skams shing brtul zhugs gnas// sred dang ni ldam ldum dag dang drus ma 'bras za kha cig spyi'u tshugs 'dug dang ba lang brtul zhugs gnas// ji ltar bdag cag 'gro ba'i gtso bo khyad 'phags 'khor los sgyur ba mchog dang de bzhin 'jig rten skyong ba dang // brgya byin rdo rje 'chang dang 'thab bral lha dbang 'phrul bar 'gyur snyam tshangs pa'i 'jig rten bsam gtan bde ba 'dod// mi yi dam pa khyod kyi rgyal srid 'di ni shin tu 'byor cing rab tu rgyas la shin tu lo legs pa// de bzhin kun dga'i ra ba dag dang skyed mos tshal dang khang mthon po rnam par rgyal ba'i khang pa mtshungs// bud med 'di dag rnams kyang pi bang dang ni gling bu dag dang glu dang rol mo'i dbyangs sgra len cing mchis// dga' bar bgyid dang gar dang glu dbyangs sbyar ba shin tu bslabs pa 'di dag spyod cing des pa ma bzhud cig // byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ 'dun pa nyon cig 'dod pa'i rgyus ni sngon gyi tshe rabs dag na bcings dang btsas dang brdegs dang bsdigs pa sdug bsngal brgya dag ngas ni bzod byas 'dus byas rnams la nga yis yid byung byas ma gyur// sngon chad bag med dbang du song zhing gti mug dkrugs la lta ba'i dra bas dkrigs shing mun gyur chos 'di mi shes pa las byung ste bdag tu 'du shes 'dzin dang tshor ba po las 'das// dngos po 'di dag thams cad g.yo zhing 'gyur la mi rtag sprin dang mtshungs shing glog dang 'dra ste zil pa'i thigs pa 'dra zhing gsob gsog snying po med la bdag yod ma yin stong par gyur pa ste// nga yi yid ni yul la chags pa med kyis 'dun pa rta rgyal dam pa bsngags ldan nga byin ngas sngon bsams pa'i bkra shis rdzogs kyis thams cad zil gnon chos kun dbang phyug chos rgyal thub par 'gyur// 'dun pas smras pa/ pad ma 'dab ma rgyas pa 'dra ba'i mig ldan zhing // do shal nor bu rin chen sna tshogs rnams kyis brgyan// mkha' la sprin tshogs dag las byung ba'i glog 'dra ba// mal na rnam par mdzes pa 'di la mi gzigs sam// pi ldir dang ni khar rnga dag dang sgra snyan dang // rdza rnga dag dang gling bu glu dbyangs len pa dang // bya bang rma bya ka la ping ka sgra 'byin pa// mi'am ci yi khyim 'dra 'di yang dor lags sam// su ma na dang ud pa la dang pAr shi ka / tsam pa ka dang dri mchog phreng ba me tog brgyus// dus kyi a ga ru mchog bdug pas rab bdugs dang // byug pa dam pa de dag la yang mi gzigs sam// shin tu dri bda' dri ldan ro bro gya nom dang // skyu rum dag dang bshos gtsang shin tu legs sbyar dang // skyems kyi ro yang kha ra bcas par rab sbyar ba// 'di la'ang mi gzigs par ni lha khyod gang du bzhud// grang ba'i dus na byug pa dro ba dam pa dang // tsha ba'i dus na tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po dang // ka shi pa yi na bza' bzang po mang po dang // de dag la yang mi gzigs lha khyod gang du bzhud// lha yul dag na lha rnams dag ni ci 'dra bar// 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga po 'di dag rab 'byor pa// dga' zhing bde dang ldan la dgyes par rol mdzod de// de nas shAkya'i dam pa nags tshal bzhud par mdzod// byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ 'dun pa ngas ni bskal pa mtha' yas dpag tu med par gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg dang mi dang lha yi 'dod pa rnam pa sna tshogs spyad kyang ngoms par gyur pa med// rgyal po'i sras mchog gyur te dbang phyug byas shing gang tshe gling bzhi dag tu 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal por gyur nas rin chen sna bdun ldan zhing bud med dag gi nang na 'dug pa dang // sum cu rtsa gsum dbang dang 'thab bral rab kyi lha dbang byas shing de dag nas ni shi 'phos 'dir 'ongs sprul pa'i lha yi nang na yid 'ong dpal ldan dam pa nga yis sngon chad spyad// lha yi gnas su dbang sgyur bdud kyi dbang po byas shing 'dod pa 'byor pa mchog la spyad kyang ngoms ma gyur na da ci dman pa 'di la bsten pas nga ngoms 'gyur ram de ni gnas min no// gzhan yang 'dun pa nga ni sdug bsngal mya ngan dgon pa'i 'khor bar gnas pa nyon mongs gdug pas dkrugs shing nyam ngas rtag tu khyer te mgon med skyabs med cing // gti mug ma rig mun pa dag na rga dang na dang 'chi ba'i 'jigs pa dag gis nyen la skye ba'i sdug bsngal dgra yis kun tu gnod cing rnam par gnod pa'i 'gro ba 'di bltas nas// ngas 'dir chos kyi gru bzang gtong dang tshul khrims brtul zhugs bzod pa brtson 'grus stobs can dag gi shing tshogs bsogs te sbyar nas lhag pa'i bsam pa snying po ldan pa rdo rje lta bus brtan por gzungs btab sbyar// gru der nga nyid zhugs nas bdag nyid rgal te bdag gis 'gro ba mtha' yas pa dag 'khor ba'i chu bo 'da' bar che ba khro ba'i dba' rlabs ldan pa 'dod chags 'dzin khri glong 'khyil dgra yis rnam par dkrugs pa rgal bar dka' las bsgral lo snyam ste nga sems de 'dra'o// de phyir srid 'tsho dgrar bcas lta ba'i 'dzin khri dang // nyon mongs srin po yod pa 'di las bdag rgal te// bdag nyid rgal bar gyur nas 'gro ba mtha' yas pa// rga med shi med zhi ba'i thang la dgod par bya// de'i tshe 'dun pa de bas kyang rab tu ngu zhing 'di skad ces smras so// lha de ltar nges par mdzad dam/ byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ 'dun pa nga yis nges par byas pa nyon// sems can dgrol phyir phan par bya phyir brtson// mi g.yo las kyang mi g.yo gnod pa med// ri rgyal lhun po lta bur brtan mi g.yo// 'dun pas smras pa/ jo jo'i nges pa ci 'dra ba zhig lags/ byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ rdo rje'i gnam lcags dgra sta mdung thung mda' char dang // lcags bskol glog gi tshogs ltar rab tu 'bar ba dang // ri rtse kun tu 'bar ba mgo steng rab 'bab kyang // nga ni khyim la 'dod pa'i phyir yang mi skyed do// de'i tshe lha'i bu nam mkha' la 'khod pa dag gis ca co dang ga zha'i sgra brgya stong phyung ste/ me tog gi char yang phab nas tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// yul rnams la ni yid kyang ma chags shing // sems can dag pa snying rje snying brtser ldan// blo gros mchog ldan rgyal gyur rgyal gyur cig // mgon po 'gro la mi 'jigs sbyin mdzad pa// mkha' la rdul gnag du ba mjug dag // mi chags bzhin du skyes mchog thugs mi chags// dri med yul gyi bde bas mi gos te// chu las pad ma ji ltar 'phags pa bzhin// dge slong dag de nas lha'i bu zhi ba'i blo gros dang / lha'i bu rtse ba bkod pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i nges pa rig nas ser skya'i gnas kyi grong khyer chen po'i skyes pa dang / bud med dang / khye'u dang / bu mo thams cad gnyid kyis log par byas so// sgra thams cad kyang mi grag par byas so// dge slong dag de nas byang chub sems dpas grong khyer gyi skye bo thams cad gnyid kyis log par rig // nam gyi gung la bab par rig // skar ma'i bdag po rgyal dang ldan par rig // da kho na mngon par 'byung ba'i dus la bab par rig nas 'dun pa la smras pa/ 'dun pa dang skyo bar ma byed par rta bsngags ldan legs par brgyan te ma thogs par nga la byin/ byang chub sems dpas tshig de skad smras ma thag tu/ de nas skad cig de nyid la rgyal po chen po bzhis/ byang chub sems dpa'i tshig thos nas/ rang rang gi gnas nas byung ste/ byang chub sems dpa' la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir rang rang gi bkod pas rings pa rings par yang ser skya'i gnas kyi grong khyer chen por 'ongs so// de na dri za'i bdag po rgyal po chen po yul 'khor srung ni dri za bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag du ma dag dang lhan cig tu sil snyan dang glu dbyangs sna tshogs len cing shar phyogs nas 'ongs par gyur te/ 'ongs nas kyang ser skya'i gnas kyi grong khyer chen po la bskor ba byas te/ ji ltar 'ongs pa'i shar phyogs nyid du gnas nas byang chub sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal zhing 'dug go// rgyal po chen po 'phags skyes po ni grul bum mu tig gi do shal sna tshogs lag na 'phyang ba/ nor bu rin po che sna tshogs thogs pa/ spos chu sna tshogs kyis gang ba'i bum pa thogs pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag du ma dag dang lhan cig tu lho phyogs nas 'ongs par gyur te/ 'ongs nas kyang ser skya'i gnas kyi grong khyer chen po la bskor ba byas te/ ji ltar 'ongs pa'i lho phyogs nyid du gnas nas/ byang chub sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal zhing 'dug go// rgyal po chen po mig mi bzang ni klu mu tig gi do shal sna tshogs lag na 'phyang ba/ nor bu rin po che sna tshogs thogs pa/ spos kyi phye ma dang me tog gi char gyi sprin kun nas slong ba'i rlung dal zhing dri zhim pa sna tshogs gtong ba bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag du ma dag dang lhan cig tu nub phyogs nas 'ongs par gyur te/ 'ongs nas kyang ser skya'i gnas kyi grong khyer chen po la bskor ba byas te/ ji ltar 'ongs pa'i nub phyogs nyid du gnas nas/ byang chub sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal zhing 'dug go// rgyal po chen po lus ngan ni gnod sbyin nor bu rin po che skar ma'i 'od zer thogs pa/ lag na mar me thogs pa/ sgron ma 'bar ba lag na thogs pa/ mda' gzhu dang / ral gri dang / mdung thung dang / mtshon rtse gnyis pa dang / rtse gsum pa dang / 'khor lo dang / mtshon rtse gcig pa dang / 'phang mdung la sogs pa mtshon cha sna tshogs thogs pa/ go cha dang ya lad sra ba bgos pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag du ma dag dang lhan cig tu byang phyogs nas 'ongs par gyur te/ 'ongs nas kyang ser skya'i gnas kyi grong khyer chen po la bskor ba byas te/ ji ltar 'ongs pa'i byang phyogs nyid du gnas nas/ byang chub sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal zhing 'dug go// lha'i dbang po brgya byin yang sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha/ lha'i me tog dang / spos dang / phreng ba dang / byug pa dang / phye ma dang / gos dang / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / me tog gi rna rgyan dang / rgyan thogs pa rnams dang / lhan cig tu 'ongs par gyur te/ 'ongs nas kyang ser skya'i gnas kyi grong khyer chen po la bskor ba byas te/ ji ltar 'ongs pa'i steng gi bar snang la 'khor dang bcas te/ byang chub sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal zhing 'dug go// dge slong dag de ltar 'dun pas byang chub sems dpa'i tshig thos nas/ mig mchi mas gang zhing byang chub sems dpa' la 'di skad ces smras so// jo jo khyod ni dus mkhyen pa/ tshod mkhyen pa/ ran pa mkhyen pa lags na/ da ltar ni bzhud pa'i dus dang tshod ma lags na/ ci'i slad du bka' de skad stsal/ byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ 'dun pa da ni dus la bab po// smras pa/ jo jo gang gi dus la bab/ byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ sems can rnams kyi don ni tshol ba na// byang chub rga shi med pa'i gnas thob nas// 'gro ba dgrol zhes nga yis yun ring nas// smon lam btab pa de yi dus la bab// 'di la 'di ni chos nyid de/ de la 'di skad ces bya'o// sa bla ba dang bar snang de bzhin skyong // lha dbang brgya byin rang gi phyogs dang bcas// 'thab bral lha dang dga' ldan 'phrul dga' dang // gzhan 'phrul dbang byed lha rnams brtson par gyur// klu rgyal chu lha dang ni gzi can dang // ma dros pa dang de bzhin rgya mtsho yang // mi mchog mngon par byung ba'i dus bab pas// de dag rnams kyang mchod phyir brtson par gyur// gang dag gzugs na spyod pa'i lha rnams dang // rtag tu bsam gtan spyod yul rab zhi spyad// de dag rnams kyang 'jig rten gsum mchod pa// mi mchog de la mchod phyir mngon par brtson// sngon spyad spyod tshe grogs por gyur pa yi// byang chub sems dpa' phyogs bcur lhags pa yang // rgyal ba mngon par 'byung ba lta byed cing // rjes su 'thun pas mchod pa bya snyam byed// gsang ba'i bdag po bdag nyid chen po de// rdo rje 'bar thogs nam mkha'i dkyil na gnas// lus la go bgos stobs brtson rtsal dang ldan// gsang ba lag na rdo rje 'bar ba thogs// lha'i bu nyi ma zla ba de gnyis kyang // g.yas dang g.yon na rab tu gnas par gyur// sor mo bcu yi thal mo sbyar byas te// mngon par 'byung la rjes su rtog par byed// skar ma rgyal de 'khor dang bcas pa yang // rang gi lus ni rgya chen sprul byas te// mi yi dam pa de yi mdun 'dug nas// yid du 'ong ba'i sgra ni rab 'byin te// skar ma rgyal ldan bzhud pa'i dus la bab// do mod khyod dge bkra shis thams cad grub// bdag kyang khyod dang thabs cig mchi bar bgyi// 'dod chags sel ba bar chad 'byung mi 'gyur// lha'i bu yang dag bskul pos bskul byas pa// stobs dang brtson 'grus 'phags pa myur du bzhengs// sdug bsngal nyen pa'i sems can thams cad sgrol// da ni mngon par 'byung ba'i dus la bab// lha rnams bye ba stong phrag mang po yang // yid 'ong me tog char pa 'bebs shing lhags// de ni skyil mo krung bcas mchog la 'dug // lha yis bskor cing mdzes la gzi brjid 'bar// grong khyer na ni skyes pa bud med khye'u dang bu mo gang yod pa// de dag thams cad yid dal gyur nas nyal te spyod lam rnams las nyams// rta dang glang po ba lang ne tsho khrung khrung rma bya ri skegs rnams// de dag rnams kyang yid dal myur du nyal te de dag gzugs mi mthong // shAkya'i bu gang rdo rje sra ba mtshon cha rtse gnyis thogs bkod dang // glang chen rta dang shing rta rta babs mchog drung bkod pa de dag nyal// rgyal po rgyal bu rgyal po'i skye bo kun kyang gnyid kyis log par gyur// bud med tshogs rnams gnyid log gos bral gcer bur gyur kyang yang ma tshor// de ni tshangs dbyangs yid du 'ong tshig ka la ping ka'i sgra dbyangs kyis// nam phyed 'das te nam gyi gung la bab nas 'dun pa de la smras// 'dun pa rta pho bsngags ldan bzang po legs brgyan legs par nga la byin// gal te nga la byams par sems na bgegs ma byed par myur du byin// 'dun pas tshig thos mchi mas mig gang rang gi jo bo de la smras// sems can kha lo sgyur mchog gar bzhud bcibs pas ci zhig bgyi// dus mkhyen cing ni tshod mkhyen chos spyod gang du'ang gshegs pa'i dus ma lags// khyod kyi sgo bkum gtan pa dam stsal su yang chab sgo 'byed mi 'gyur// brgya byin gyi ni yid kyi sems pa'i dbang gis sgo yang bye bar gyur// 'dun pas de 'dra mthong nas dga' zhing sdug bsngal de ni mchi ma 'khor// kyi hud bdag grogs su yod ji ltar bya zhing phyogs ni gar brgyug snyam// gzi brjid ldan pas drag shul can gyi tshig smras brgya byin 'ba' zhig thos// yan lag bzhi ldan dpung dang bcas pa 'di yang 'di na ci zhig byed// rgyal po rgyal bu rgyal po'i skye bo de dag rnams kyis 'di ma tshor// bud med tshogs kyang gnyid log lha rnams kyis ni grags ldan gnyid log byas// kyi hud 'di yis sngon chad bsams pa'i smon lam thams cad grub gyur cig // lha stong bye ba de dag dga' ba'i yid kyis 'dun pa de la smras// 'dun pa rta mchog bsngags ldan legs par phul cig 'dren pa skyo mi bya// lha dang lha min dag gis rnga dung rdza rnga rol mo khrag khrig byas// 'on kyang lhas bsnyal ba yi grong khyer mchog 'di sad par yong ma gyur// 'dun pa bar snang dri ma med la lha yi 'od rab mdzes la ltos// khyod kyis byang chub sems dpa' bye ba mang po mchod phyir gang lhags ltos// bde sogs khyim thab brgya byin dpung bskor sgo na mdzes par 'dug pa dang // lha dang lha min mi 'am ci tshogs gang dag mchod phyir lhags la ltos// 'dun pa des kyang lha tshig de thos bsngags ldan rta pho de la smras// sems can kha lo sgyur mchog 'di bzhud khyod ni rta skad sgrogs shing shog // de yis dbyar gyi kha dog can de rmig pa gser gyis brgyan byas nas// yid mi dga' bzhin yon tan rgya mtsho mnga' ba'i bcibs par dbul ba byas// mtshan mchog mnga' zhing phan mdzad khyod kyi chibs 'di rigs bzang dge ba lags// khyod kyis sngon chad gang bgos smon lam de grub gyur cig gshegs su gsol// gang dag bgegs bgyid zhi bar gyur cig dgongs pa'i brtul zhugs grub gyur cig // 'gro ba kun la bde dang mtho ris pa dang zhi ba sbyin gyur cig // de ni gang tshe mal nas langs tshe sa 'di thams cad rnam drug g.yos// rta rgyal dam pa zla ba nya ba'i dkyil 'khor 'dra ba de la zhon// skyong ba'i lag pa rnam dag pad ma dri med 'dra bas rta mchog bteg // brgya byin tshangs pa de gnyis de yi mdun na lam ni 'di zhes ston// de yis gsal ba dri ma med pa'i 'od btang sa rnams snang bas gsal// de tshe ngan song kun zhi sems can bde ldan nyon mongs gnod pa med// me tog char bab sil snyan bye ba sgra byung lha dang lha min bstod// thams cad dga' dang ldan nas grong khyer mchog la bskor ba byas te dong // skyes bu chen po song bas grong khyer dam pa'i lha yang yid ni dman par gyur nas 'ongs// mdun du 'dug nas snying rjer ngu ba'i yid ldan de yis pad ma 'dra ba'i bzhin la smras// khyod bral sgren mor mi mdzes sa 'di grong khyer thams cad mun pas kun tu dkrugs par gyur// do mod khyod kyis khab 'di spangs na bdag la dga' bde bgyid pa 'di na 'ga' ma mchis// slan chad bya tshogs rnams kyis sgra dag dang // grags pa mtha' yas khyod ni sad bgyid pa'i// btsun mo'i 'khor gyi gling bu snyan pa dang // bkra shis sgra dang glu sgra thos mi 'gyur// nyon mongs bcom pa khyod ni gshegs gyur na// gdugs mtshan khyod la mchod pa bgyid pa yi// lha dang grub tshogs slan chad mthong mi 'gyur// lha yi dri yang slan chad snom mi 'gyur// phreng ba btags nas zhag lon gyur pa ltar// khyod kyis do mod pho brang de bzhin spangs// khyod bzhud slan chad gzi brjid dpal ma mchis// gar la lta ba bzhin du bdag la gda'// grong khyer kun gyi byin dang stobs phrogs te// 'di ni dgon pa 'dra zhing mdzes ma lags// gang gis sa 'dir 'khor lo stobs can du// lung bstan drang srong tshig ni deng gyur// bsod nams sdong po chen po khyod byung na// sa 'dir shAkya'i stobs ni stobs ma mchis// rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor 'dir gdung yang 'chad// shAkya'i tshogs 'di bsam pa rab tu nyams// dri med dri bral khyod ni gar bzhud par// bdag kyang khyod dang lhan cig mchi bar bgyi// 'on kyang thugs brtse thugs rje bskyed nas ni// khyod kyis pho brang 'di la gzigs su gsol// blo gros ldan pa khyim la bltas nas ni// snyan pa'i nga ros 'di skad tshig smras te// skye 'chi mthar 'byin ma thob bar du ni// nga yis ser skya'i grong khyer 'jug mi bya// rga shi med pa'i gnas mchog 'chi med pa// byang chub dam pa nga yis ma thob par// nga ni ser skya'i gnas su mngon phyogs te// 'greng 'dug nyal dang 'chag par mi bya'o// gang tshe 'gro ba'i gtso bo pa// byang chub sems dpa' de byung zhing // de ni mkha' las 'gro ba'i tshe// lha yi bu mo rnams kyis bstod// 'di ni sbyin pa'i gnas chen yin// 'di ni bsod nams zhing chen yin// 'di ni bsod nams 'dod pa'i zhing // 'chi med 'bras bu sbyin mdzad pa// sems can rnams la thugs rje bas// 'di yis bskal pa bye mang du// sbyin dang dul dang sdom pa yis// 'dis ni byang chub yang dag bsgrubs// 'di yi tshul khrims yongs su dag // brtul zhugs bzang zhing spyod ma nyams// 'dod pa dag dang longs spyod rnams// don du mi gnyer tshul khrims srung // sems can yongs su bskyab pa'i phyir// 'di ni rtag tu bzod pa gsung // yan lag nying lag gcad gyur kyang // khro ba mi mnga' sdang mi mnga'// 'di ni rtag tu brtson 'grus ldan// bskal pa bye bar skyo mi mnga'// 'di yis byang chub yang dag bsgrubs// mchod sbyin dag ni bye ba mdzad// 'di rtag bsam gtan bsam gtan pa// thugs ni zhi zhing rab tu zhi// nyon mongs thams cad bsregs nas ni// sems can bye ba 'grol bar 'gyur// 'di ni shes rab chags mi mnga'// rtog dang rnam par rtog ldan las// grol zhing thugs ni rnam grol te// rang byung ba yi rgyal bar 'gyur// 'di ni rtag tu byams thugs ldan// thugs rje yi ni pha rol byon// dga' dang btang snyoms bsam gtan pa// tshangs pa'i lam gyi cho ga mkhyen// 'di ni shin tu lha yi lha// lha rnams kyis ni mchod pa'i 'os// thugs dge dag cing dri ma bral// yon tan khrag khrig pha rol byon// 'jigs pas nyen pa rnams kyi skyabs// mig med rnams kyi sgron ma ste// gnod pa rnams kyi skyabs kyang lags// ring nas na ba'i sman pa lags// rgyal po dam pa chos kyi rgyal// dbang po lta bur spyan stong mnga'// tshangs pa lta bur rang byung gyur// lus dang sems ni rab sbyangs pa// brtan zhing shes rab rab tu mang // dpa' zhing thugs ni 'dod chags bral// nyon mongs 'joms pas dpa' bo ste// ma rgyal dgra las rgyal ba lags// seng ge lta bur bsnyengs pa spangs// glang po lta bur rab dul thugs// khyu mchog lta bur mnga'// me tog lta bur khrims dri gda'// ston pa lhun po ltar mi g.yo// dog sa lta bur gsos su gyur// rin chen 'byung gnas ltar mi 'khrugs// 'di ni phung po'i bdud las rgyal// 'di ni 'chi bdag bdud nams des// smra ba'i seng ge 'dra bar shog // dge slong dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' mngon par byung nas shAkya'i yul dang / kau ta'i yul dang / gyad yul las 'das te me ne ya'i yul gyi grong rdal nu tshol cig // de dag gis phyi nang du btsal kyang ma rnyed nas skye dgu'i bdag mo chen mo gau ta mI smre sngags 'don te/ sa la 'gre ldog cing rgyal po zas gtsang ma la 'di skad ces smras so// rgyal ldan pa// kyi hud bdag gi shangs legs smin legs smin mtshams bar na dri med mdzod spu gnas pa po// kyi hud bdag gi dpung mgo rab zlum gzhu 'dra'i rked pa e ne'i byin pa rked pa zlum// kyi hud bdag gi nags tshal gel ba'i lha mo de yi grogs su gyur pa dpal yon ldan// 'dun pa kho mo shin tu sdug bsngal gter bstan nas ni mig phyung 'dra bas mig byin cig // 'dun pa rgyal ba kun gyis pha dang ma dag ste rtag ma yin// byis pa 'du shes kyis bzung lta ba phyin ci log pas skye dang 'chi 'pho gnas par gyur// de yis sngon chad rga shi ldan pa'i 'dus byas dag la grogs po 'ga' yang med ces bstan// khyod mchog tu yid mi dga' zhing sa 'tsho ma yi tshig ni thos gyur nas// de ni nga ro 'thon cing tshig tu smras pa sa 'tsho ma khyod bdag tshig legs par gson// nam gyi gung thun bud med tshogs rnams thams cad rab tu gnyid kyis log ste dben gyur pa// de yi tshe na bsod nams brgyas 'phags de yis bdag la bsngags ldan nga la byin zhes gsung // de skad tshig thos nas ni de ma thag tu bdag gis khyod ni gzims mal gzims la bltas// de tshe khyod kyi sdug pa 'di ni gshegs kyis sa 'tsho bzhengs zhes sgra skad chen po phyung // lha yis tshig de bkag par gyur pas bud med rnams las 'ga' tsam zhig kyang sad ma gyur// bdag ni rab tu ngu zhing rta yi rgyal po brgyan pa bgyis nas mi mchog de la phul// bsngags ldan drag shul can gyi gzi ldan sgra byung de yi sgra ni rgyang grags tsam tu grags// 'on kyang lha yis gnyid kyis log par bgyis pas grong khyer pa las 'ga' yang sad ma gyur// gser dang dngul dang nor bu rnams kyis g.yogs pa'i sa la bsngags ldan rkang lag rab tu brdabs// de las snyan dang 'jigs dang mdzes pa'i sgra byung 'on kyang mi las 'ga' tsam sad ma gyur// de yi bar skabs skar ma rgyal dang ldan gyur zla ba skar ma dag kyang mkha' la gnas// mkha' las lha rnams bye ba thal mo sbyar te btud nas phyag kyang rab tu 'tshal// gnod sbyin srin po tshogs rnams nye bar gnas shing 'jig rten skyong ba rdzu 'phrul che ldan bzhis// pad ma'i ze ba lta bur rnam dag dri med lag pas bsngags ldan gyi ni rkang lag bteg // bsod nams gzi brjid brgyas 'phags de yang ku mu da dang par sha lta bu de la bcibs// sa ni rnam pa drug tu rab tu g.yos shing sangs rgyas zhing rnams dri med 'od kyis khyab// bde sogs khyim thab brgya byin lha yi gtso bo nyid kyis de tshe chab sgo dbye ba bgyis// de ni bye ba khrag khrig lha yis mdun du bdar te lha dang klu yis mchod nas gshegs// bsngags ldan gyis ni 'du shes tsam gyis de na 'jig rten mgon po mkha' las bkur bar shes// lha dang lha ma yin tshogs dbang por bcas pa de dag bcibs te bde bar gshegs pa gshegs// lha yi bu mo glu dbyangs mkhas pa rnams kyang byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan rab brjod cing // de dag bsngags ldan la yang stobs 'thud byed cing snyan la yid du 'ong ba'i sgra yang 'byin// bsngags ldan 'jig rten 'dren pa myur ba myur bar khyer la skyo ba mi dga' ma skyed cig // 'jig rten mgon po mnyes par byas na khyod la 'jigs dang ngan song ngan 'gro med par 'gyur// lha rnams re re zhing yang bdag la 'jig rten mgon po bcibs par mngon du dga' bar gyur// yul sa 'di na bye ba lha yi rkang pa dag gis non par ma gyur cung zad med// bsngags ldan nam mkha'i skabs na sna tshogs spras shing mdzes pa'i lam gnas rin chen stegs bu ni// rnam pa sna tshogs dag gis brgyan cing lha yi bdug pa snying po mchog bdug sa 'di la ltos// bsngags ldan dge ba'i las 'dis sum cu rtsa gsum lha gnas shin tu legs par sprul pa der// lha yi bu mos bskor cing mdun gyis bltas la lha yi 'dod pa'i dga' bas dga' bar gyis// legs pa sa 'tsho ma khyod phyir zhing ma bshums dgyes par mdzod cing mchog tu dgyes par mdzod// mi mchog byang chub brnyes nas lha yis mdun du bdar ba ring por mi thogs gzigs par 'gyur// sa 'tsho mi rnams gang dag legs pa'i las bgyis de dag rtag tu bshums par bgyi ma lags// de ni bsod nams gzi brjid brgyas 'phags lags kyis dgyes par mdzod la bshum mo ma mdzad cig // rgyal po mngon par byung ba de na lha dang mis mchod pa yi bkod pa gang lags pa// bkod pa de ni sa 'tsho bdag gis dgung bdun bar du brjod kyang rdzogs par brjod mi nus// khyod kyis 'gro la phan mdzad pa la bsnyen bkur mdzad pas brnyes mchog bsam gyis mi khyab brnyes// bdag gis bsams na khyod kyang mi yi dam pa de ni ci 'dra de 'drar 'gyur snyam bgyid// mngon par 'byung ba'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// // 'phags pa rgya cher rol pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po bcu gcig pa/ dge slong dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis 'dun pas rgyal po zas gtsang 'bras kyang 'di nyid tsam mo// dge slong dag ngas zas su 'bras 'bru gcig zos pas lus myur du snga ma bzhin du gyur te/ e ma'o dge sbyong gau ta ma nya mad ku ra'i mdog 'dra'o// sngon 'di'i mdog mdzes pa gsal bar gyur pa de yang med par gyur to zhes bya ba'i bar du'o// dge slong dag ngas 'di snyam du bsams te/ bdag gis de bas kyang zas chung ngu nyid la nan tan bya'o snyam mo// dge slong dag ngas mngon par shes te/ ngas zas su til 'bru gcig pu kho na ste gnyis su med pa zos pa nas/ de'i kha dog 'jam po med par gyur to zhes bya ba'i bar du'o// dge slong dag ngas 'di snyam du bsams te/ dge sbyong dang bram ze gang dag kha cig zas mi za bas dag par sems te/ bdag gis kyang thams cad kyi thams cad du zas mi za bar nan tan bya'o snyam nas/ dge slong dag de nas zas mi za bar 'dug go// dge slong dag ngas zas ma zos pas lus shin tu skams shing nyam chung ba dang rid par gyur to// 'di lta ste dper na ldum bu a si ta ka'i tshigs pa dang / ka li ka'i tshigs pa bas kyang nyis 'gyur dang / sum 'gyur dang / bzhi 'gyur dang / lnga 'gyur dang / bcu 'gyur gyis nga'i yan lag dang / nying lag skems par gyur te/ 'di lta ste rtsib logs ni srog chags kar ka ta ka'i rtsib logs dang / bzhon pa'i bres khang lta bur gyur to// sgal tshigs ni lan bu blas pa lta bur gyur to// mgo'i thod pa ni ku ba kha bo lta bur gyur to// mig gi 'bras bu ni khron pa'i skar ma lta bur gyur to// dge slong dag nga legs par ldang ngo snyam nas lus kyis bskyod na/ sgur por gyur te 'gyel to// sha thang ste langs nas rdul gyis lus yog pa/ lag pas phyis pa dang / ba spu rul pa thams cad lus las lhags so// gang sngon nga kha dog mdzes shing 'jam par gyur pa de yang 'di ltar bdag nyid spong ba rtsub por btang ba'i phyir med par gyur to// nga'i spyod yul gyi grong na gnas pa'i skye bo nyen kor ba rnams kyang // 'di ltar e ma'o dge sbyong gau ta ma ni gnag go// e ma'o dge sbyong gau ta ma ni sngo bsangs so// e ma'o dge sbyong gau ta ma ni nya mad ku ra'i mdog 'dra'o// sngon 'di'i kha dog mdzes pa gsal bar gyur pa de yang med par gyur to snyam du shes so// de'i tshe rgyal po zas gtsang ma yang nyin re zhing byang chub sems dpa'i drung du pho nya gtong ngo // dge slong dag de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' snga ma bzhin du 'jig rten du bya ba rmad du byung ba bstan pa dang / bya ba nyams pa'i sems can rnams las dang bya ba la gzud pa dang / bsod nams kyi tshogs rnams brjod pa dang / ye shes chen po'i yon tan bstan pa dang / bsam gtan gyi yan lag rnams rnam par dbye ba'i phyir til 'bru gcig dang / rgya shug 'bru gcig dang / 'bras 'bru gcig gis lo drug gi bar du dka' ba spyod pa bstan te yid dman pa med do// byang chub sems dpa' lo drug gi bar du skyil mo krung bcas nas/ ji ltar 'dug pa bzhin du gnas te/ spyod lam nyams pa med do// nyi mas bab nas kyang grib ma la ma song ngo // grib ma las kyang nyi ma la ma song ngo // rlung dang nyi ma dang char pa'i skyabs ma btsal to// sha sbrang dang / sbrang bu dang / sdig sbrul ma bskrad do// bshang ba dang / gci ba dang / mchil ma dang / snabs ma bor ro// bskum pa dang / smyang ba ma byas so// glos phab pa'am/ khas buba'am/ gan rkyal ma yin par gnas pas gnas so// sprin chen po dang / yul ngan chen po dang / char pa dang / ser ba dang / ston dang / dpyid dang / dgun gang yin pa de dag gis kyang byang chub sems dpa'i lus la ma phog go// tha na byang chub sems dpas lag pas kyang ma bskyabs so// dbang po yang ma bkag go// dbang po'i yul yang ma blangs so// gang dag der 'ong ba grong gi gzhon nu'am/ grong gi gzhon nu ma'am/ ba lang rdzi'am/ phyugs rdzi'am/ rtswa thun nam/ shing thun nam/ lci thun de dag kyang byang chub sems dpa' la rdul khrod kyi 'dre yin pa snyam du sems shing de la rtsen te/ de las sa skud do// der byang chub sems dpa' lo drug po de dag gis lus ngan pa dang / god pa dang rid par gyur te/ de'i rna ba gnyis su rtswa 'am shing bal bcug nas sna'i bu ga gnyis su 'byin to// sna'i bu ga gnyis su bcug nas rna ba'i bu ga gnyis su 'byin to// rna ba'i bu ga gnyis su bcug nas khar 'byin to// khar bcug nas rna ba dang sna'i bu gang 'byin to// snar bcug nas rna ba dang / sna dang khar 'byin to// lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po gang dag byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan mngon sum du gyur pa de dag nyin mtshan du gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' la mchod pa byed do// smon lam yang 'debs so// de na byang chub sems dpa' lo drug gi bar du dka' ba spyod pa ston cing lha dang mi khrag khrig phrag bcu gnyis tshang ba dag theg pa gsum la yongs su smin par byas so// de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ byang chub sems dpa' khyim byung ba// yon tan dag dang ldan pa de// sems can don dang phan pa'i phyir// thabs dang ldan pa'i bsam pa skyes// snyigs ma lnga yi dus kyi tshe// chos dma' mos pa'i 'jig rten po// las dang bya bor 'jig rten du// 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir skyes par gyur// mu stegs tshogs kyis rab tu gang // ltad mo dang ni ltas su lta// lus la gnod pa bya ba byed// byis pa de dag dag par sems// g.yang sa me dang mya ngam 'jug // sgren mo sa dang lci bas skud// lus ni yongs su gdung ba'i phyir// gdung ba lnga la brtson dang ldan// lag pa brkyang ste rgyu ba dang // mi mkhas kha cig lag pa ldag // bum pa khar gzhong las mi len// sgo dang ka bas chod mi len// gang na khyi yod pa nas min// 'dug ce'am tshur shog ces las min// khyim nas kha zas gcig len pas// bdag ni dag par 'gyur snyam sems// mar dang 'bru mar bu ram zho// nya dang sha dang 'o ma spong // ldam ldum sre da pad ma'i rtsa// gzegs dang ba lang lci ba za// rtsa ba 'bras bu lo ma za// ku sha tshal bu la ba lpags// srel byed kha cig sgren mor rgyu// glen pa 'di bden gzhan snyam// lag pa sgreng bar byed pa dang // skra bsgreng ral pa bsgreng ba dag // lam las rab tu rnam par nyams// lam min gnas shing bde 'gro 'dod// rtswa dang gtun shing thal bar nyal// tsher mar nyal zhing tsog pur 'dug // kha cig rkang pa gcig pus 'greng // gdong bstod nyi dang zla la lta// chu mig mtsho dang lteng ka dang // rgya mtsho chu bo nyi zla dang // shing dang ri yi rtse mo dang // rdza dang sa la phyag kyang 'tshal// glen pa de dag gnod mang gis// lus ni yongs su skom par byed// log par lta dang ldan pa dag // myur du ngan song rnams su ltung // nga ni dka' thub brtul zhugs dang // dka' spyad gang zhig lha dang mis// spyad par nus pa ma yin pa'i// dka' spyad drag po rtsom snyam sems// bsam gtan gang zhig rang rgyal gyis// blta bar nus pa ma yin pa'i// rdo rje lta bur brtan gnas pa// mkha' khyab bsam gtan bsam gtan byed// mu stegs brtul zhugs ngan pa yis// dga' ba'i lha mi 'di na yod// de dag yongs su smin bya'i phyir// dka' spyad brtul zhugs drag po brtsams// sa steng ci yang ma bting bar// skyil mo krung ni bcas te 'dug // rgya shug til dang 'bras 'bru gcig // za ba'i cho ga rnam par ston// dbugs dbyung rngub pa rnam par spangs// stobs dang ldan pa g.yo ba med// lo drug bar du bsam gtan mchog // nam mkha' khyab la bsam gtan byed// rtog dang rnam par rtog med pa// g.yo ba med cing sems rgyu med// nam mkha'i khams su khyab pa yi// mkha' khyab bsam gtan bsam gtan byed// de ni nyin las grib mar ram// grib las nyi mar song ma byas// lhun po lta bur mi g.yo ba'i// mkha' khyab bsam gtan bsam gtan byed// rlung dang char dang sha sbrang dang // sdig sprul sbrang bu skyob mi byed// rnam par ma 'khrugs spyod pa yis// mkha' khyab bsam gtan bsam gtan byed// bdag nyid gcig pu'i don gyi phyir// mkha' khyab bsam gtan byed pa min// gzhan du snying rje sems kyis ni// 'jig rten don mang ched du bsgom// grong gi byis pa ba lang rdzi// shing thun dag dang rtswa thun dag// de la rdul khrod 'dre snyam sems// de la sa yis skud byed cing // mi gtsang ba yang 'thor bar byed// de dag gnod pa mang byed kyang // g.yo ba med cing 'khrugs med par// mkha' khyab bsam gtan bsam gtan byed// mtho ba med cing dma' ba med// lus ma bsrungs par chos ma reg // bshang ba mi byed gci mi byed// sgra yis mi 'jigs gzhan mi lta// sha dang khrag rnams skams gyur te// lags pa rtsa rgyus rus pa lus// sgal tshigs dag ni lto bar snang // lan bu blas pa ci bzhin no// gang dag lhag par byas lha dang // lha min gnod sbyin dri za klu// yon tan ldan pa mngon sum bas// nyin dang mtshan du mchod pa byed// ji ltar mkha' 'dra'i sems ldan 'di// mkha' khyab bsam gtan bsam gtan byed// de 'drar bdag cag myur gyur ces// smon lam dag kyang 'debs par byed// snying rje'i blo yis 'jig rten gyi// don mang phyir byed ma gtogs par// bdag phyir ma yin bde blos min// bsam gtan ro ni myang phyir min// phas kyi rgol ba rab tu bcom// mu stegs blo nyams zil gyis mnan// mgo reg byang chub ga la yod// byang chub bskal mang rnyed dka' zhes// 'od srung la ni tshig smras pa'i// las dang bya ba rab tu bstan// skye bo dag ni dga' bya'i phyir// mkha' khyab bsam gtan bsam gtan byed// lha mi khrag khrig bcu gnyis tshang // theg pa gsum la rab tu btul// de yi ched du blo gros bzang // mkha' khyab bsam gtan bsam gtan byed// dka' ba spyad pa'i le'u zhes bya ba ste/ bcu bdun pa'o// // dge slong dag bdud sdig can yang byang chub sems dpa' lo drug gi bar du dka' ba spyad pa spyod pa'i tshe phyi bzhin 'brang ste/ glags bltas skabs btsal kyang nam yang glags cung zad kyang ma rnyed do// de glags ma rnyed nas yi chad de yid la gcags bzhin du song ngo // de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ dgon pa nyams ni dga' ba dang // nags tshal gel pa sgra med dang // lteng rgyas kyi ni shar phyogs na// chu klung nai ran dza na der// spong ba'i phyir ni brtson par byas// rtag tu mthu rtsal brtan pa po// grub dang bde ba thob bya'i phyir// brtson pas rab tu rtul de la// bdud ni 'jam zhing snyan pa'i tshig // smra bar byed cing 'ongs par gyur// kye srog gces kyis 'tsho bar gyis// gson na chos ni spyod par 'gyur// gson tshe bya ba gang yod pa// de dag byas na mya ngan med// khyod ni mdog nyams dman par gyur// khyod ni shi la thug cing 'dug // 'chi ba'i cha ni stong snyed tsam// cha gcig tsam cig gson par zad// sbyin pa dag ni rtag tu byin// me yi sbyin sreg sbyin sreg byos// 'on kyang bsod nams chen por 'gyur// spong ba yis ni ci zhig bya// spong ba'i lam ni sdug bsngal te// sems dul ba ni bya dka' zhes// de tshe bdud kyis de skad tshig // byang chub sems dpa' de la smras// de skad smra ba'i bdud de la// byang chub sems dpas 'di skad smras// sdig can myos pa'i rtsa lag po// khyod ni rang gi don phyir 'ongs// nga la bsod nams chud zad kyang // don du gnyer ba med do bdud// gang dag bsod nams don du gnyer// de la de skad smra ba'i rigs// 'tsho ba'i mtha' ni 'chi yin pas// mi 'chi snyam du nga mi sems// tshangs par spyod la gzhol gyur pas// phyir ldog par ni mi bya'o// chu klung dag gi chu rgyun kyang // rlung gis rnam par skems byed na// spangs pa nyid kyi khrag tsam lta// 'di yis ci phyir skams mi 'gyur// khrag ni skams par gyur pa dang // de yi 'og tu sha skams 'gyur// sha ni zad par gyur pa dang // phyir zhing sems ni dang bar 'gyur// phyir zhing 'dun dang brtson 'grus dang // ting nge 'dzin kyang gnas par 'gyur// nga ni de ltar gnas pas na// tshor ba dam pa thob gyur kyang // lus dang srog la mi lta ste// sran thub dag par gyur la ltos// nga la 'dun pa yod gyur cing // brtson 'grus dang ni shes rab yod// nga yi brtson 'grus bskyod nus pa// 'jig rten de ni ngas ma mthong // srog chad shi ba ches bla ste// 'tsho ba ngan pa de lta min// g.yul ngor shi ba legs pa ste// pham nas gson pa de lta min// sdar ma dpung las mi rgyal te// dpa' bo dpung las rgyal bar 'gyur// rgyal yang de ni rlom sems med// bdud khyod las ni myur rgyal bya// 'dod pa khyod kyi dang nyid kyis bkrus so// de lus ngal te chad nas rdzing nas 'byung snyam pa dang / bdud sdig can phrag dog gi chos dang ldan pas rdzing bu gang ba mthon po zhig sprul to// rdzing de'i 'gram na shing sgrub byed ces bya ba chen po zhig yod do// byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten dang 'thun par bya ba dang / lha mo la phan gdags pa'i phyir shing de'i lha mo la smras pa/ lha mo shing gi yal ga smod cig // des kyang shing yal ga smad nas byang chub sems dpa' de la 'jus te byung ngo // byung nas kyang shing sgrub byed de'i drung du phyag dar khrod pa chos gos snam sbyar du byas nas drubs te/ deng sang du'ang de phyag dar khrod pa drubs pa zhes ming du grag go// de nas gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu 'od dri ma med pa zhes bya ba des/ lha'i gos ngur smrig gi tshon du btsos pa rung ba dge sbyong gi tshul dang 'thun pa dag byang chub sems dpa' la phul lo// byang chub sems dpas kyang de dag blangs te/ snga dro sham thabs dang chos gos bgos nas spyod yul gyi grong du phyogs pa dang / de na lha rnams kyis lteng rgyas kyi sde dpon gyi grong na dga' byed ces bya ba'i grong mi zhig yod pa'i bu mo legs skyes ma la nam phyed tsam na smras pa/ khyod kyis gang gi phyir mchod sbyin byas pa de brtul zhugs de nyams 'og tu chud nas de kha zas rags pa bzang po bza' bar sems kyis/ sngon khyod kyis bdag gi zas zos nas byang chub sems dpa' bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar shog shig ces smon lam btab pa gang yin pa'i khyod kyi bya ba de gyis shig // dge slong dag de nas grong mi dga' byed kyi bu mo legs skyes mas lha de dag gi tshig de thos nas myur ba myur bar ba stong gi 'o ma lan bdun du snying khur byas pa bzang po mchog tu 'gyur ba snying po can blangs te/ blangs nas kyang 'o ma de 'bras sar pa sar pa dag dang / phru ba sar par blugs nas thab sar bar btsugs te/ kha zas de sgrub bo// de sgrub pa na snga ltas 'di dag snang ste/ 'o ma de'i nang na dpal be'u dang / bkra shis pa dang / g.yung drung 'khyil pa dang / pad ma dang / sdong ris la sogs pa bkra shis rnams snang ngo // de nas des 'di snyam du bsams te/ ltas 'di lta bu 'di dag snang ba las na/ byang chub sems dpas zas zos nas byang chub 'thob par 'gyur du the tsom med do snyam pa dang / rgya mtsho pa shes shing cho ga shes pa'i mtshan mkhan phyogs der phyin par gyur nas/ des kyang bdud rtsi 'thob pa nyid du lung bstan to// de nas legs skyes mas thug pa de tshos pa dang thang la bzhag ste/ me tog gis gtor/ spos chus gtor nas gus par stan bting ste/ bran mo gong ma zhes bya ba la smras pa/ gong ma song la bram ze bos shig // ngas ni 'o thug sbrang rtsi can 'di blta'o// jo mo legs so zhes de'i ltar mnyan nas/ shar phyogs logs su song ba dang / des byang chub sems dpa' mthong ngo // de bzhin du lho phyogs logs su song na yang byang chub sems dpa' mthong ngo // de bzhin du nub dang byang phyogs logs su song na yang de dang der des byang chub sems dpa' mthong ngo // de'i tshe na gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu rnams kyis gzhan mu stegs can thams cad tshar bcad par gyur pas 'ga' tsam yang mi snang ngo // de nas de slar log ste jo mo la 'di skad ces smras so// gang dang gang du mchis kyang de dang de na dge sbyong mdzes pa gda' ba las/ dge sbyong ngam bram ze gzhan ni 'ga' yang mi gda'o// legs skyes mas smras pa/ de nyid bram ze yin te/ de'i phyir 'di brtsams kyis/ gong ma song la de nyid bos shig // jo mo legs so zhes smras te/ gong ma song nas byang chub sems dpa'i rkang pa gnyis la gtugs te legs skyes ma zhes bgyi bas spyan 'dren to zhes smras so// dge slong dag de nas byang chub sems dpa' grong pa'i bu mo legs skyes ma'i khyim du song ste stan bting ba la 'dug go// dge slong dag de nas grong pa'i bu mo legs skyes mas 'o thug sbrang rtsi can gyis gser gyi snod chen po bkang ste/ byang chub sems dpa' la phul lo// de nas byang chub sems dpas 'di snyam du bsams te/ legs skyes mas kha zas 'di lta bu 'di byin pa 'di bdag gis deng zos te/ the tsom med par bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bya'o snyam mo// de nas byang chub sems dpas zas de blangs nas grong pa'i bu mo legs skyes ma la 'di skad ces smras so// che zhe gser gyi snod chen po 'di ji ltar bya/ des smras pa/ khyod snoms shig // byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ kho bo la ni snod 'di lta bu mi dgos so// legs skyes mas smras pa/ ci dgyes su mdzod cig // bdag ni snod ma mchis par su la yang zas mi stsol to// de nas byang chub sems dpas zas de thogs te/ lteng rgyas nas byung nas dro la bab pa dang / klu'i klung chu bo nai ran dza na'i ngogs su song ste/ zas dang chos gos rnams phyogs gcig tu bzhag nas/ byang chub sems dpa' lus bsil bar bya ba'i phyir klung nai ran dza na'i nang du zhugs so// dge slong dag byang chub sems dpa' khrus byed pa'i tshe/ lha'i bu brgya stong du ma dag 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir lha'i a ga ru dang / tsan dan gyi phye ma dang / byug pa dag klung du ldugs shing lha'i me tog kha dog sna tshogs dag kyang chu'i nang du 'thor ro// de'i tshe klung chen po nai ran dza na lha'i spos rnams dang / me tog rnams kyis gang bar gyur te 'bab bo// byang chub sems dpa' spos chu gang gis khrus byas par gyur pa de lha'i bu bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong dag gis blangs te mchod rten du bya ba dang / mchod par bya ba'i phyir rang rang gi gnas su khyer ro// byang chub sems dpa'i skra dang ag tshom gang yin pa de dag kyang grong pa'i bu mo legs skyes mas bkra shis pa yin no snyam nas/ mchod rten du bya ba dang / mchod par bya ba'i phyir khyer ro// byang chub sems dpa' klung nas byung nas 'dug par 'dod de gling la lta'o// de nas klung nai ran dza na'i klu'i bu mo gang yin pa de sa'i 'og nas byung ste/ yid las byung ba'i seng ge'i khri byang chub sems dpa' la phul nas/ byang chub sems dpa' de la 'dug ste/ grong pa'i bu mo legs skyes ma la snying brtse ba nye bar bzung nas/ ji tsam dgos par 'o thug sbrang rtsi can de 'thungs so// 'thungs nas kyang gser gyi snod chen po de la ma chags par chur bor ro// bor ma thag tu klu'i rgyal po rgya mtshos mchod pa'i 'os yin no zhes dad pa dang gus pa bskyed de blangs nas rang gi gnas su song ngo // de nas mig stong pa grong khyer 'jig pa nam mkha' lding gi gzugs su sprul nas kha rdo rje'i mchur bsgyur te/ klu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho las gser gyi snod chen po de dbrog tu brgal na ma nus nas rang gi gzugs kyis gus par byas te/ bslangs nas mchod rten du bya ba dang / mchod par bya ba'i phyir sum cu rtsa gsum gyi gnas su khyer ro// khyer nas kyang snod chen po'i dge 'dun gyi dus ston byas te/ deng sang du'ang sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams lo gcig bzhin du snod chen po'i dus ston byed do// seng ge'i khri de yang klu'i bu mo de nyid kyis mchod rten du bya ba dang / mchod par bya ba'i phyir khyer ro// dge slong dag byang chub sems dpas zas rags pa zos ma thag tu byang chub sems dpa'i bsod nams kyi stobs dang / shes rab kyi stobs kyis skad cig de nyid la lus la snga ma'i kha dog bzang po rgyas pa dang / skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis dang / dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu dang / 'od 'dom gang ba yang byung bar gyur to// de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ lo drug bar du brtul zhugs nyams 'og chud byas bcom ldan blo gros 'di snyam sems// gal te bdag ni 'di ltar rid bzhin bsam gtan mngon shes ye shes stobs ldan pa// shing gi rgyal po'i drung du song ste thams cad mkhyen nyid 'tshang rgyar bya na ni// de dag na yang bdag gis phyi ma'i skye bo dag la snying brtse ma byas 'gyur// bsod nams ngan ngon tsam dang ldan pa'i lha mi 'di dag ngan pas ye shes tshol// de dag lus ni nyam chung gyur na bdud rtsi 'tshang rgya byed par mi nus pas// kha zas rags pa dam pa zos te lus kyi mthu stobs bskyed pa byas na ni// shing gi rgyal po'i drung du song ste thams cad mkhyen nyid 'tshang rgyar bya bar bsams// grong pa'i bu mo sngon chad spyod pa spyad pa legs skyes ma zhes bya ba de// 'dren pa brtul zhugs grub par shog ces de lta'i yid kyis rtag tu mchod sbyin byed// de ni lha yis bskul ba thos nas de tshe 'o thug sbrang rtsi can blangs te// klung gi 'gram du song nas dga' ba'i yid kyis nai ran dza na'i ngogs na 'dug // bskal pa stong du spyod pa spyad cing dbang po zhi la rab tu zhi ba de// lha dang klu yi tshogs dang drang srong dag gis bskor te nai ran dza na ra 'ongs// pha rol brgal nas sems can sgrol ba blo gros ldan pa khrus byar bsams nas ni// thub pa dag pa dri med 'jig rten snying brtse phyir ni klung du zhugs te 'khru// bye ba phrag stong lha dag dga' ba'i yid kyis spos rnams dang ni phye ma dag // klung du 'thor zhing sems can dam pa bkru ba'i don du chu la gang bar byed// byang chub sems dpa' dri med nges pa bkrus te ngogs na 'dug par shes gyur nas// lha stong rab tu dga' ste sems can dag pa bkrus pa'i chu de mchod phyir khyer// ngur smrig bzang po dri ma med pa'i gos dag lha yi bu yis de la byin// rung ba dag dang sham thabs bgos nas bcom ldan 'das ni chu klung ngogs na 'dug // klu yi bu mo dga' zhing rab tu mgu ba'i yid kyis seng ge'i khri yang bshams// de la 'jig rten dag gi mig byed yid kyang rab tu zhi ba de 'dug nas// blo gros ldan pa legs skyes ma des gser gyi snod du kha zas blugs te byin// rkang par phyag 'tshal nas ni de dag kha lo sgyur ba bdag gis gsol zhes byas// blo gros ldan pas ji tsam dgos par zas kyang zos nas snod ni chur bor te// de ni grong khyer 'jig pa lha yi bla mas bdag gis mchod par bya zhes khyer// gang tshe rgyal bas kha zas rags pa dam pa zos pa de yi skad cig la// de yi lus kyi stobs dang gzi brjid dag dang dpal yang snga mkho bzhin du gnas// legs skyes ma dang lha rnams dag la chos gtam byas nas don kyang mang du byas// seng ge ngang pa'i stabs dang glang po'i dbang po'i 'gros kyis byang chub shing drung chas// nai ran dza na'i le'u zhes bya ba ste/ brgyad pa'o// // dge slong dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' klung nai ran dza nar khrus byas te/ zas zos nas lus kyi mthu stobs bskyed de/ bdud las rnam par rgyal bar bya ba'i phyir rnam pa bcu drug dang ldan pa'i sa phyogs shing gi rgyal po byang chub chen po'i drung ga la ba der skyes bu chen po'i stabs gang yin pa'i stabs des song ste/ mi bskyod pa'i stabs dang / dbang po'i mchod sdong lta bu'i stabs dang / ri'i rgyal po lhun po ltar shin tu brtan pa'i stabs dang / mi dngom pa ma yin pa'i stabs dang / ya yo med pa'i stabs dang / 'tshe ba med pa'i stabs dang / rings pa ma yin pa'i stabs dang / sdod pa med pa'i stabs dang / 'khrugs pa med pa'i stabs dang / 'khyor pa med pa'i stabs dang / 'drud pa med pa'i stabs dang / zhum pa med pa'i stabs dang / ha cang mi gti mug med pa'i stabs dang / chags pa med pa'i stabs dang / seng ge'i stabs dang / dad pa'i rgyal po'i stabs dang / klu'i rgyal po'i stabs dang / sred med kyi bu'i stabs dang / sa la mi reg pa'i tsam du mtho ba/ steng du rin po che'i dra ba bres pa/ lha'i gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan gyis legs par brgyan par sprul to// mda' rgyang gang tsam/ mda' rgyang gang tsam gyi zhing rin po che sna bdun gyi shing ta la stegs bu de bas mtho ba mngon par sprul te/ shing ta la thams cad rin po che brgyus pas phan tshun 'brel bar 'dug go// shing ta la gnyis gnyis kyi bar du rdzing spos chus yongs su gang ba gser gyi bye ma bdal ba/ me tog ud pa la dang / pad ma dang / ku mu da dang / pad ma dkar po la sogs pas gang ba/ rin po che'i stegs bus bskor ba/ nor bu rin po che bai dU r+yas them bya ne tso dang / ri skegs dang / khu byug dang / ka la ping ka dang / shang shang te'u dang / ngang pa dang / ngur pa dang / khrung khrung dang / rma bya brgya stong ni bskor ba byed/ bkra shis brgya 'gro'i 'jigs dang mi phrad mi khom mi 'gyur te// lha yi nang du 'dod pa'i bde ba rnyed nas tshangs pa'i gnas yangs 'gro bar 'gyur// lo drug bar du dka' ba spyad pa spyad nas 'di ni byang chub shing drung bzhud// kun kyang dga' zhing rab tu mgu ba'i yid kyis de la mchod pa legs par gyis// de ni stong gsum rgyal po dbang phyug dam pa chos kyi dbang phyug rgyal po ste// brgya byin tshangs pa nyi zla'i grong khyer dag na de dang mnyam pa gang yang med// gang btsas tshe na zhing rnams bye ba khrag khrig rnam pa drug tu g.yos gyur pa// de ni de ring bdud kyi dpung las rgyal bar mdzad phyir shing chen mchog drung bzhud// gang gi spyi gtsug tshangs pa'i gnas 'dir gnas kyang blta bar nus pa ma yin zhing // gang gi sku la mtshan rab dam pa ldan zhing sum cu rtsa gnyis legs brgyan la// gang gi gsung 'dir yid du 'ong zhing snyan la rnar 'thad tshangs dbyangs sgra snyan cing // gang gi thugs ni rab zhi khro dang bral ba de la mchod pa byed du 'dong // gang dag blo gros brgya byin tshangs pa'i 'dod dang // gal te sa gsum dag na sangs rgyas nyid 'dod de dag 'dren pa mchod par gyis// gang gis rgya mtshor bcas pa'i sa dang de bzhin rin po che rnams mtha' yas dang // khang skar khung bsil khang mang ldan pa dang zung du sbrel dang bzhon pa dang // me tog phreng ba shin tu mdzes pas brgyan pa skyed mos tshal gyis rab brgyan dang // rkang lag mgo dang mig rnams yongs su btang ba de ni byang chub snying por zhugs// dge slong dag de ltar stong gsum gyi tshangs pa chen po de skad cig de la stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir phyin te/ lag mthil ltar mnyam par gyur pa/ gyo mo dang rdo med pa dang / nor bu dang / mu tig dang / bai dUr+ya dang / dung dang / man shel dang / byu ru dang / gser dang / dngul mang ba/ rtswa sngo zhing 'jam la g.yas su 'khyil cing g.yung drung 'khyil pa ka tsa lin di ka'i gos ltar reg na bde ba dag gis stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams khyab pa 'dir phyin to// de'i tshe rgya mtsho chen po thams cad sa lta bur gyur kyang chu na rgyu ba'i sems can rnams la gnod pa cung zad kyang med do// 'jig rten gyi khams de ltar brgyan pa 'di phyogs bcu'i brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten skyong ba rnams kyis mthong nas byang chub sems dpa' la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya stong legs par brgyan to// byang chub sems dpa' la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis kyang lha'i dang mi'i las shin tu 'das pa'i mchod pa bkod pa rnams kyis phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing dpag tu med pa brgyan par gyur to// sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag thams cad kyang bkod pa'i rgyan sna tshogs kyis brgyan pas sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig lta bur snang bar gyur to// 'jig rten gyi bar dag dang / ri nag po dang / khor yug dang / khor yug chen po dag kyang mi snang bar gyur to// sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag thams cad ni byang chub sems dpa'i 'od kyis gsal bar snang ngo // byang chub kyi snying po yongs su skyong ba'i lha'i bu bcu drug yod de// 'di lta ste/ lha'i bu ud ka li zhes bya ba dang / lha'i bu mud ka li zhes bya ba dang / skye dgu'i bdag po dang / dpa' stobs dang / dpung rgyan stobs dang / rab brtan dang / sa 'dzin dang / snang byed dang / dri ma med dang / chos kyi dbang phyug dang / chos kyi tog dang / 'gro grub dang / mig thogs pa med dang / bkod pa chen po dang / tshul khrims rnam dag dri ldan dang / pad ma'i 'od de/ lha'i bu bcu drug po de dag ni byang chub kyi snying po yongs su skyong ba dag ste/ thams cad kyang phyir mi ldog pa'i bzod pa thob pa sha stag go// de dag gis kyang byang chub sems dpa' la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir byang chub kyi snying po brgyan te/ dpag tshad brgyad cu khor yug tu rin po che sna bdun gyi stegs bu rim pa bdun gyis ni bskor/ shing ta la'i phreng ba rim bdun dang / rin po che'i dril bu g.yer ka'i dra ba rim bdun dang / rin po che brgyus pa rim pa bdun gyis ni bskor/ 'dzam bu'i chu bo'i gser gyi glegs bam rin po che thams cad kyis spras pa dag dang / gser gyi tsong tsong dag dang / 'dzam bu'i chu bo'i gser gyi pad ma dag gis ni khebs par byas/ snying po mchog gi spos kyis ni bdugs/ rin po che'i dra ba ni bres so// phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams tha dad pa dag na shing sna tshogs mngon par 'phags pa/ bzang ba mngon du mchod pa/ lha yul ba dang / mi yul ba gang dag na yod pa de dag thams cad kyang byang chub kyi snying po der snang bar gyur to// phyogs bcu dag na chu nas skye ba dang / thang las skye ba'i me tog rnam pa sna tshogs gang dag yod pa de dag thams cad kyang byang chub kyi snying po der snang bar gyur to// phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams tha dad pa dag na/ byang chub sems dpa' gang dag bsod nams dang / ye shes kyi tshogs tshad med pa'i bkod pa dag gis byang chub kyi snying po brgyan par byed pa de dag kyang byang chub kyi snying po der snang bar gyur to// de ltar lha'i bu byang chub kyi snying po yongs su skyong ba dag gis byang chub kyi snying por bkod pa de 'dra ba dag sprul par gyur te/ de dag lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dag gis mthong nas rang rang gi gnas la dur khrod tsam gyi 'du shes skyed par gyur to// bkod pa de dag mthong nas shin tu ngo mtshar cher 'dzin te/ e ma'o bsod nams kyi rnam par smin pa'i rgyu 'thun pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa legs so zhes ched du brjod pa'ang ched du brjod do// byang chub kyi shing gi lha mo bzhi yod de 'di lta ste/ 'od ma dang / snyan ldan dang / yid dang / mdangs ldan ma ste/ byang chub kyi shing gi lha mo bzhi po de dag gis kyang byang chub sems dpa' la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir byang chub kyi shing rtsa ba phun sum tshogs pa/ sdong po phun sum tshogs pa/ yal ga dang / lo ma dang / me tog dang / 'bras bu sna tshogs phun sum tshogs pa/ khrun dang sboms phun sum tshogs pa mdzes pa/ blta na sdug pa/ shin tu 'gel ba/ 'phang du shing ta la bdun srid tsam du mtho ba/ de dang 'tsham par 'gel ba/ bkra ba/ blta na sdug pa/ yid du 'ong ba/ rin po che sna bdun gyi stegs bu rim bdun gyis bskor ba/ rin po che'i shing ta la'i phreng ba rim pa bdun dang / rin po che'i dril bu g.yer ka'i dra ba rim pa bdun dang / rin po che brgyus pa'i phreng ba rim pa bdun gyis kun nas bskor cing phyi rim bskor ba/ shing yongs 'du sa brtol dang 'dra ba/ mig gis blta bas mi ngoms pa bskyed do// gang du byang chub sems dpa' 'dug nas byang chub mngon par rdzogs par byang chub par 'dod pa'i sa phyogs de ni stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdo rje'i dkyil te/ sra ba/ snying po yod pa/ mi phyed pa/ rdo rje'i rang bzhin du gnas par gyur pa'o// dge slong dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' byang chub kyi snying por 'gro ba na lus las rnam pa 'di lta bu'i 'od 'gyed de/ 'od des ngan song thams cad zhi bar gyur to// mi khom pa thams cad bcad par gyur to// ngan 'gro'i tshor ba thams cad bskams par gyur to// sems can gang dag dbang po ma tshang ba de dag ni dbang po yongs su rdzogs pa thob par gyur to// nad kyis btab pa rnams ni nad sos par gyur to// mi bde ba thams cad ni bde ba thob par gyur to// 'jigs pas nyen pa rnams ni dbugs phyin pa thob par gyur to// bcing bas bcings pa rnams ni bcings pa las grol bar gyur to// sems can dbul po rnams ni longs spyod dang ldan par gyur to// nyon mongs pas gdungs pa rnams ni yongs su gdung ba med par gyur to// bkres pa rnams ni lto 'grangs par gyur to// skom pa rnams ni skom pa med par gyur to// sbrum ma rnams ni bde bar btsas par gyur to// zhum pa nyam chung ba rnams ni stobs phun sum tshogs par gyur to// de'i tshe sems can gang la yang 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang / gti mug dang / khro ba dang / chags pa dang / tha ba dang / gnod sems dang / phrag dog gi gnod pa med par gyur to// de'i tshe sems can gang yang 'chi ba med/ 'pho ba med/ skye ba med do// de'i tshe sems can thams cad byams pa'i sems dang / phan pa'i sems dang ldan zhing gcig la gcig pha mar 'du shes bskyed par gyur to// de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ mnar med pa la thug pa'i bar// dmyal ba mi bzad snang ba yi// sems can rnams kyi sdug bsngal zhi// bde ba'i tshor ba thob par 'gyur// dud 'gro'i skye gnas sems can rnams// phan tshun gnod byed ji snyed pa// thub chen 'od kyis reg pas na// de dag byams pa'i sems kyang skyes// 'jig rten rnams// bkres skom nyen pa ji snyed pa// byang chub sems dpa'i gzi brjid kyis// de dag zas skom rnyed par gyur// mi khom thams cad chad gyur cing // ngan 'gro rnams kyang skams par gyur// sems can thams cad bder gyur te// lha yi bde bas rab tu tshim// mig dang rna ba med pa dang // gzhan yang gang dag dbang po nyams// de dag dbang po kun rdzogs shing // yan lag thams cad mdzes par gyur// 'dod chags zhe sdang la sogs pa'i// nyon mongs rnams kyis sems can gang // gnod gyur de tshe nyon mongs kun// zhi bar gyur te bde dang ldan// smyos pa dag ni dran ldan zhing // dbul po dag kyang nor dang ldan// nad kyis btab pa nad sos shing // bcing bas bcings pa grol bar gyur// ser sna med cing dgra med de// gnod sems dang ni rtsod pa dag // phan tshun byed pa med gyur te// de tshe byams pa'i sems su gnas// pha dang ma dag bu gcig la// ji ltar phangs par sems pa ltar// de bzhin sems can phan tshun du// de tshe bu phangs bzhin du sems// byang chub sems dpa'i 'od dra yis// phyogs bcu'i phyogs ni kun tu yang // gang gA'i bye ma'i grangs snyed kyi// zhing rnams bsam gyis mi khyab gsal// ri bo nag po rnams dang ni// khor yug dag kyang mi snang gyur// rgya chen zhing rnams de dag kun// gcig po ji bzhin de ltar snang // lag mthil lta bur gyur pa ste// byang chub sems dpa' mchod pa'i phyir// zhing rnams thams cad legs brgyan pas// thams cad rin chen nyid du snang // byang chub snying po'i rim gro pa// lha ni de ltar bcu drug yod// dpag tshad brgyad cu'i sa khyon nang // byang chub snying po brgyan par gyur// zhing rnams bye ba mtha' yas na// bkod pa chen po gang yod pa// byang chub sems dpa'i gzi brjid kyis// de dag thams cad der yang snang // lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang // mi'am ci dang lto 'phye che// rang rang gzhal med khang rnams la// dur khrod tsam du shes par gyur// 'dir ni bkod pa de mthong nas// lha dang mi rnams ngo mtshar gyur// bsod nams gang gi rgyu 'thun 'dir// phun sum 'di 'dra 'di legs 'tshar// lus dang ngag dang yid rnams kyis// brtson par byed pa med par yang // de yi yid la 'dod pa dang // bsam pa thams cad rab tu 'grub// ji ltar bsam pa gzhan dag kyang // sngon spyod tshe na rdzogs gyur pa// las de'i rnam par smin pa yis// 'di 'dra'i phun sum tshogs 'di byung // byang chub shing gi lha mo bzhis// lha yi shing ni yongs 'du ba// de bas khyad par 'phags pa yis// byang chub snying por brgyan par byas// byang chub snying po'i bkod pa gang // lha yis mngon par 'dus byas pa// yon tan de dag tshig gis ni// thams cad brjod par yong mi nus// dge slong dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i lus las 'od phyung ba rnam par dag pa/ dri ma med pa/ lus dang sems tshim par byed cing dga' bskyed pa/ nyon mongs pa thams cad sel ba/ sems can la dga' ba dang / bde ba dang / dad pa dang / mchog tu dga' ba thams cad skyed pa des klu'i rgyal po nag po'i gnas snang bar byas par mthong nas/ de'i tshe klu'i rgyal po nag po rang gi 'khor gyi mdun du 'dug ste tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// gang phyir bdag gi gnas 'di gser gyi 'od kyis brgyan par lha der gyur pa las// ji ltar 'khor ba 'jig gi 'od mdzes mthong zhing gser zhes bya ba mthong ba dang // ji ltar 'od srung chos kyi rgyal po skyon med pa yi dri med 'od mthong ltar// mtshan mchog ldan zhing phan mdzad ye shes 'od ldan pa zhig 'byung du the tshom med// sngon chad nyes par byas pa'i las kyis bdag gi khyim ni shin tu mun pas gang // khyim 'di na ni nyi ma zla ba dag gis rgya cher 'od kyang yong mi snang // me dang nor bu dag dang dri med glog dang skar ma rnams kyi 'od mi snang // brgya byin 'od dang tshangs pa'i 'od dang lha min rnams kyi 'od kyang mi snang na// de ring khyim 'di'i nang du nyi ma'i 'od 'dra ba yi dge bas mdzes gyur la// sems kyang dga' bskyed cing lus kyang bde bar gyur la lus ni bsil gyur te// lus kyi steng du bye tshan 'bab pa de yang bdag la bsil bar gyur pa las// bskal pa bye ba mang por spyad pa byang chub shing drung bzhud par shin tu gsal// klu yi me tog mdzes dang bzang la dri zhim gos dang mu tig do shal dang // rgyan dang gdu bu dag dang phye ma rnams dang bdug pa mchog rnams myur thogs la// glu dbyangs dag dang rol mo'i dbyangs sgra sna tshogs gyis shig rnga dang rdza rnga bzang // brdung zhing 'gro bla kun gyis mchod 'os phan pa mdzad la mchod pa byed du 'deng // de ni langs te klu yi bu mo rnams dang lhan cig phyogs bzhir bltas pa dang // de nas ri bo lhun po lta bur gzi brjid rnams kyis legs par brgyan pa zhig // lha dang lha min bye ba dag dang tshangs pa'i dbang dang gnod sbyin rnams kyis bskor// dga' ba'i yid kyis de la mchod byed shul ni 'di zhes ston cing 'dong ba mthong // klu yi rgyal de rab tu dga' zhing mgu nas 'jig rten mchog la mchod byas te// gus dang bcas pas de yi rkang pa gnyis la phyag 'tshal thub pa'i mdun du 'dug // klu yi bu mo rnams kyang dga' zhing mgu ba'i yid kyis thub la mchod pa byed// me tog rnams dang spos dang byug pa dag kyang 'thor zhing sil snyan rnams kyang byed// klu yi rgyal po rab tu dga' nas thal sbyar yang dag yon tan rnams kyis bstod// 'dren pa 'jig rten dam pa dgung zla nya ba'i zhal 'dra mthong bar gyur pa legs// bdag gis sngon chad drang srong rnams kyi mtshan ma mthong ba khyod kyang de 'dra ste// de ring khyod kyis bdud kyi dpung rnams bcom ste bzhed pa'i go 'phang brnyes par 'gyur// gang gi don du sngan chad dul dang sbyin dang bsdams shing bdog pa kun btang la// gang gi don du dul dang tshul khrims byams dang snying rje ba dang bzod pa bsgoms// gang gi don du brtson 'grus brtan dang bsam gtan dgyes dang shes rab 'bar mdzad pa// khyod kyi smon lam de dag thams cad rab tu rdzogs nas de ring rgyal bar 'gyur// ji ltar ljon shing lo ma me tog 'bras bur bcas pa byang chub shing la 'dud// ji ltar bum pa chab kyis gang ba stong dag khyod la bskor ba rab bgyid cing // ji ltar tsa sha'i tshogs rnams rab tu dga' ste snyan pa'i sgra skad 'byin pa dang // ji ltar ngang pa khrung khrung tshogs kyang mkha' la mchi zhing tshul du shis ldan par// dang ba'i yid kyis drang srong la ni bskor ba bgyid las de ring dgra bcom 'gyur// ji ltar gser gyi kha dog lta bur mdzes pa'i 'od rnams zhing ni brgyar mchis te// ji ltar ngan song mtha' dag zhi bar bgyid cing skye dgu'i sdug bsngal thar bgyid dang // ji ltar nyi ma zla ba'i gnas kyi rgyun tshad bser ma'ang dal bus ldang ba las// srid pa gsum du skye dang rga ba thar mdzad pa yi ded dpon de ring 'gyur// ji ltar lha rnams 'dod pa'i dga' ba spangs te khyod la mchod du lhags pa dang // tshangs dang tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don dang lha rnams bsam gtan bde ba spangs pa dang // gang yang srid pa gsum na dbang phyug dam pa mchis pa thams cad 'dir lhags las// srid pa gsum du skye rga thar ba mdzad pa'i sman pa'i rgyal po de ring byon// ji ltar lha rnams dag gis phyag dar bgyis pa'i shul de nas ni khyod gshegs la// bcom ldan 'khor ba 'jig dang gser zhes bgyi dang 'od srung dag kyang de nas gshegs// ji ltar pad ma bzang po dri ma ma mchis rnam dag dog sa brtol byung ste// de la stobs chen ldan pa zhabs kyi gom pa 'dor las de ring dgra bcom 'gyur// bye ba khrag khrig stong phrag du ma'i gang gA klung gi bye ma snyed kyi bdud// de dag rnams kyis byang chub shing drung nas ni khyod la bskyod pa'am g.yos ma nus// mchod sbyin khrag khrig phrag stong rnam pa du ma gang gA klung gi bye ma snyed// khyod kyis mdzad cing 'gro la phan phyir spyad pa des na 'dir ni rnam par mdzes// rgyu skar zla bar bcas shing skar ma nyi mar bcas pa mkha' las sar ltung gda'// ri mchog chen po rang gi gnas nas g.yo zhing rgya mtsho skams par 'gyur yang gda'// skyes bu mkhas pa la las khams bzhi po dag re re nas ni ston nus gda'// khyod ni shing gi rgyal po'i drung du gshegs nas byang chub ma thob bzhengs mi gda'// gang gi slad du kha lo sgyur ba mthong zhing mchod bgyis yon tan brjod pa dang // byang chub tu yang spro bas bdag gis rnyed pa 'phel ba rgya chen rnyed par gyur// bur bcas bdag dang klu yi bu mo thams cad skye gnas 'di las thar gyur cing // glang po dregs pa'i stabs su bzhud pa khyod kyi stabs des bdag cag mchi bar bgyi// dge slong dag de ltar klu'i rgyal po nag po'i chung ma dam pa gser 'od ces bya ba klu'i bu mo rin po che'i gdugs sna tshogs thogs pa dang / sil snyan sna tshogs thogs pa dang / mu tig gi do shal sna tshogs thogs pa dang / nor bu rin po che sna tshogs thogs pa dang / lha'i dang mi'i phreng ba brgyus pa sna tshogs thogs pa dang / pog phor sna tshogs thogs pa dang / sil snyan dang glu dbyangs sna tshogs len pa rab tu mang pos yongs su bskor cing mdun du bdar te/ byang chub sems dpa'i gan du 'dong zhing rin po che'i me tog sna tshogs mngon par gtor te tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis kyang bstod do// 'khrul pa mi mnga' mi bsnyengs mi 'dzem bag mi tsha// ma zhum mi dman rab tu dgyes par gdul dka' ba// ma chags mi sdang ma rmongs brkam pa mi mnga' ba// chags bral rnam grol drang srong khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// sman pa zug rngu bral ba gdul ba 'dul mdzad pa// 'gro ba sdug bsngal rnams las thar mdzad sman pa mchog // gnas dang skyabs ma mchis shing dman pa mkhyen nas ni// 'jig rten gsum 'dir gnas dang skyabs su khyod dgyes par mdzod// shing dbang drung du gshegs la bsnyengs pa mi mngar bzhugs// bdud kyi sde las rgyal mdzod nyon mongs dra ba drol// sngon gyi rgyal dbang rnams kyis ji ltar sangs rgyas ltar// byang chub zhi ba dam pa mchog tu 'tshang rgyar mdzod// khyod kyis gang gi don du bskal pa bye mang du// 'gro ba sgrol ba'i don du dka' ba spyad pa mdzad// khyod kyis dgongs pa rdzogs te dus la da bab kyis// shing dbang drung du gshegs te byang chub mchog reg mdzod// dge slong dag de nas byang chub sems dpas 'di snyam du bsams te/ sngon gyi de bzhin gshegs pa de dag ci zhig la bzhugs nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas snyam mo// de nas des yang 'di snyam du bsams te/ rtswa bting nas bzhugs so snyam mo// de nas gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i tshogs brgya stong bar snang la 'khod pa dag gis byang chub sems dpa'i sems kyi yongs su rtog pa sems kyis shes nas tshig 'di skad ces smras so// de de bzhin no// skyes bu dam pa de de bzhin te/ sngon gyi de bzhin gshegs pa de dag rtswa bting ba la bzhugs nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so// dge slong dag byang chub sems dpas lam gyi g.yas rol na rtswa 'tshong bkra shis pa zhes bya ba rtswa sngo ba/ 'jam pa/ shin tu gzhon pa/ nyams dga' ba/ lcang lor 'khril bar 'dug pa/ g.yas su 'khyil ba/ rma bya'i mgrin pa lta bu/ ka tsa lin da'i gos ltar bsags kha cig dbang po'i mchod sdong 'dra'i// dri med tog thogs byang chub snying po der yang lhags// kha cig mkha' las nor bu rin chen dra ba 'thor// zla ba zla thang skyes rnam mdzes man dA ra// par sha tsam pa ka dang sna ma'i me tog phreng // byang chub sems dpa' shing rgyal drung na bzhugs la 'thor// kha cig rkang pa gnyis kyis sa ni rab bskyod la// sa bskyod nas kyang skye bo dga' bar byed cing lhags// kha cig ri bo lhun po lag na thogs byed la// bar snang gnas te me tog skon bu 'thor zhing lhags// kha cig rgya mtsho bzhi po mgo la thogs nas ni// sa la spos chu 'thor te chag chag 'debs shing lhags// kha cig rin chen mchod sdong sna tshogs thogs nas ni// rgyang ring 'dug ste byang chub sems dpa' ston cing lhags// kha cig tshangs pa lta bur zhi ba'i gzugs bsgyur te// yid zhi rab zhi gnas shing bsam gtan bsam gtan pa// de dag ba spu dag las byams dang snying rje dang // dga' dang btang snyoms tshad med yid 'ong sgra 'byin lhags// kha cig brgya byin lha ltar stong phrag khrag khrig gi / lha rnams dag gis mdun du bdar nas lhags gyur cing // de dag byang chub shing drung phyin nas thal sbyar te// brgya byin thogs pa'i nor bu rin chen sna tshogs 'thor// kha cig phyogs bzhi dag gi skyong ba ji lta bar// dri za srin po mi'am ci yis yongs bskor te// glog ltar gsal ba'i me tog char pa 'bebs shing lhags// dri za mi'am ci yi skad kyis brtan pa bstod// kha cig me tog rgyas pa'i ljon shing 'bras bur bcas// me tog bcas shing mchog gi dri ni rab 'byin la// lo mar sangs rgyas sras po lus phyed gnas thogs lhags// btud nas sa yi snying por me tog rnams kyang 'thor// kha cig pad ma ud pa la pad ma dkar po rgyas// pad ma'i snying por sum cu rtsa gnyis mtshan ldan gnas// de 'drar me tog rgyas pa'i rdzing bu thogs te lhags// chags med yid ldan byang chub sems dpa' mkhas la bstod// kha cig lhun po lta bur lus chen bsgyur te lhags// bar snang gnas nas rang gi lus kyang rab tu 'dor// bor ma thag tu me tog phreng ba rnams su gyur// stong gsum dag gi rgyal ba'i zhing rnams khebs par byed// kha cig mig gnyis sreg pa'i bskal pa lta bu dang // de bzhin chags pa dang ni 'jig par ston cing lhags// de dag lus las chos kyi sgo mo mang grag ste// de dag thos pas sems can khrag khrig sred pa spong // kha cig mchu ni bim pa 'dra la bzhin mdzes shing // kha bzhin rdzogs la mi'am ci 'dra'i sgra sgrogs lhags// do shal sna tshogs legs brgyan bu mo chas pa 'dra// de la lta bas lha yi tshogs rnams ngoms mi 'gyur// kha cig rdo rje lta bur mi phyed lus can de// rkang pas 'og gi chu yi phung po 'bog cing lhags// nyi ma 'dra zhing zla ltar bzhin rgyas snang byed la// 'od byed nyon mongs skyon rnams bcom pa kha cig lhags// kha cig rin po ches brgyan lag na rin chen thogs// zhing mang bye ba stong dag khebs par byed cing lhags// sems can mang la phan dang bde dang tshim bya'i phyir// rin chen me tog dam pa dri zhim char pa 'bebs// kha cig gzungs chen rin po che yi mdzod gyur cing // ba spu rnams nas mdo sde khrag khrig rab brjod la// spobs par ldan zhing blo gros ldan la blo mchog ldan// rgyags zhing rab dregs skye bo rtogs par byed cing lhags// kha cig ri bo lhun po rnga ltar thogs nas ni// rab tu rdung zhing mkha' las yid 'ong sgra 'byin lhags// de yi sgra ni phyogs bcur bye ba'i zhing song ste// bdud rtsi ma thob ston pa do mod 'tshang rgyar sgrog // byang chub kyi snying por bkod pa'i le'u zhes bya ba ste nyi shu pa'o// // dge slong dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' dag gis byang chub kyi snying por bkod pa rnam pa de lta bu de dag mngon par byas par gyur to// byang chub sems dpa' nyid kyis kyang phyogs bcu dag gi sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad na byang chub kyi snying po'i rgyan bkod pa ji snyed cig yod pa de dag thams cad byang chub kyi snying po der kun tu bstan to// dge slong dag de nas byang chub sems dpa' byang chub kyi snying po la 'dug nas 'di snyam du sems te/ 'dod pa'i khams 'di'i bdag po dbang phyug dbang sgyur ba bdud sdig can de la bdag gis ma sbran par bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba de ni bdag gi mi chas/ bdag gis bdud sdig can bskul bar bya'o// de las rnam par rgyal na 'dod pa na spyod pa'i lha la sogs pa thams cad tshar bcad par 'gyur ro// 'on tang bdud kyi 'khor na bdud kyi ris kyi lha'i bu sngon dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa 'khod pa dag gis nga'i seng ge rnam par rol pa mthong na bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed par 'gyur ro snyam mo// dge slong dag de nas byang chub sems dpas de ltar bsams nas de'i tshe smin mtshams kyi bar gyi mdzod spu nas bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad 'joms par byed pa zhes bya ba'i 'od zer gcig phyung ste/ 'od zer des stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di thams cad kyi bdud kyi gnas thams cad snang bar byas nas mog mog por byas te rab tu g.yos par byas par yang gyur to// stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di thams cad kyang snang ba chen pos yongs su khyab par gyur to// bdud sdig can gyis 'od de las rnam pa 'di lta bu'i sgra 'di yang thos so// sems can shin tu dag pa bskal mang spyod spyad pa// zas gtsang sras pos rgyal srid dag ni rab spangs te// phan byed de ni bdud rtsi mngon par 'dod pas byung // byang chub shing drung 'ongs kyis de ring bsgrim par gyis// de ni bdag kyang rgal la gzhan yang sgrol bar byed// de ni bdag nyid grol bas gzhan yang grol bar byed// de ni bdag kyang dbugs phyin gzhan dag dbugs kyang 'byin// yongs su mya ngan 'das nas gzhan dag mya ngan zlo// ngan song gsum po ma lus stongs par byed par 'gyur// lha mi rnams kyi grong khyer gang bar byed par 'gyur// phan pa byed pa de ni bdud rtsi thob gyur nas// bsam gtan mngon shes bdud rtsi bde mchog sbyin par 'gyur// gang tshe rang byung nyid kyis chos char mngon phab tshe// nag po'i rtsa lag khyod kyi grong khyer stongs byed 'gyur// stobs med pas kyang stobs med 'gyur te dpung nyams 'gyur// phyogs ni phyogs min ci bya gar 'gro shes mi 'gyur// dge slong dag de ltar bdud sdig can bskul ba'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis bskul nas rmi lam rnam pa sum cu rtsa gnyis rmis so// rnam pa sum cu rtsa gnyis gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ bdag gi gnas mun dang mtshungs// mche ba dag ni glang po'i mche ba 'dra// kha gdong de 'dra'i dpung rnams der yang lhags// lus kyi dbyibs ni chu srin 'dra ba ste// mig gi 'bras bu gnyis ni rab tu 'bar// rna ba dag ni rung ba'i gzugs can gnod sbyin lhags// gshol thogs 'khor lo thogs shing mig sgyur dang // ri rtse chen po lag na thogs pa dang // rlung dang rdo dang gnam lcags rab 'bebs shing // gnod sbyin 'jigs su rung ba der yang lhags// rlung ni rab tu gtong zhing char yang 'bebs// brgya phrag stong gi glog kyang rab tu 'byin// 'brug gi sgra yang sgrog cing shing ljon sgyel// byang chub shing gi lo ma tsam mi g.yo// char pa rab tu 'bebs shing rlung yang gtong // chu bo 'bebs shing chu yis sa yang gang // de ltar 'jigs su rung ba mtshan mo byung // de yi nub mo sems med shing yang sgyel// thams cad dbyibs mi sdug cing gzugs mi sdug // 'jigs pa'i gzugs ldan de dag mthong nas kyang // yon tan mtshan dang gzi brjid ldan pa po// lhun po lta bur sems ni g.yo ba med// sgyu ma 'dra zhing rmi lam mtshungs pa na bdud sdig can gyis rang gi bu de dag la smras pa/ yu bu cag ci 'dra ba'i dpung gis byang chub sems dpa' gdul bar bya/ de na g.yas rol nas bdud kyi bu ded dpon zhes bya bas pha la tshigs su bcad de
