thos dang // bya rog rdo 'phangs mod la 'byer ba bzhin// sngangs skrag snying gas thams cad rab tu byer// de nas bdud sdig can sdug bsngal zhing yid mi bde ste/ yi ma rangs la skyengs bzhin du nga rgyal gyi zil gyis non pas ma song la phyir yang ma log cing bros kyang ma bros te phyir bltas nas yang dpung rnams la smras pa/ khyed lhan cig 'dus te cung zad cig sdod cig // rnam pa 'di lta bu'i sems can rin po che glo bur du chud mi gzan par kho bos rjes su 'chags pas 'di bslang bar nus sam mi nus sad par bya'o// de nas bdud sdig can gyis rang gi bu mo rnams la smras pa/ bu mo khyed deng ste byang chub kyi snying por song la byang chub sems dpa' 'dod chags dang bcas pa'am/ 'on te 'dod chags med/ ci gti mug can nam/ 'on te shes rab can/ ci ldongs pa zhig gam/ 'on te phyogs shes pa zhig gam/ 'on te dpung gnyen med pa zhig gam/ dman pa zhig gam brtan pa zhig yin pa bgoms shig // tshig de thos nas bdud kyi bu mo de dag byang chub kyi snying po ga la ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' ga la ba der song ste phyin nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i mdun du 'khod de/ bud med kyi sgyu rnam pa sum cu rtsa gnyis nye bar bstan to// rnam pa sum cu rtsa gnyis gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ de'i nang nas kha cig ni bzhin phyed 'gebs pa dang / kha cig ni nu ma mkhrang zhing 'bur ba ston pa dang / kha cig ni cung zad 'dzum pas so'i phreng ba ston pa dang / kha cig ni lag pa brkyang ste bya rmyangs byed cing mchan khung ston pa dang / kha cig ni shing thog bim pa ltar dmar ba'i mchu ston pa dang / kha cig ni mig phyed btsums te byang chub sems dpa' la lta zhing // bltas nas myur ba myur bar 'dzums pa dang / kha cig ni nu ma phyed g.yogs te ston pa dang / kha cig ni gos snyil bar byas te/ gser gyi phag ska dang bcas pa'i rked pa ston pa dang / kha cig ni gos du ku la srab mo gyon te/ gser gyi phag ska dang bcas pa'i rked pa ston pa dang / kha cig ni rkang gdub sgra sil sil 'byin pa dang / kha cig ni nu ma'i bar nas phreng ba gcig nye bar ston pa dang / kha cig ni brla phyed tsam brdzes pa nye bar ston pa dang / kha cig ni mgo dang phrag pa dag la bya 'dab sbed dang / ne tso dang / ri skegs 'dug par nye bar ston pa dang / kha cig ni byang chub sems dpa' la mig zur gyis lta ba dang / kha cig ni gos legs par bgos kyang bgo ma legs pa lta bur bcos pa dang / kha cig ni rked pa dang / gser gyi phag ska skyod pa dang / kha cig ni 'khrul ba ltar 'chos shing sgeg ste phan tshun 'chag pa dang / kha cig ni gar byed pa dang / kha cig ni glu len pa dang / kha cig ni bsgegs shing ngo tsha ba ltar yang 'chos pa dang / kha cig ni chu shing rlung gis bskyod pa ltar brla sgul ba dang / kha cig ni brjid pa'i sgra 'byin pa dang / kha cig ni seng ras bgos te gser gyi phag ska dril bu can bcings nas dgod cing 'chag pa dang / kha cig ni gos dang rgyan rnams sa la 'dor zhing ngo tsha ba ltar slar yang len pa dang / kha cig ni gsang ba dang / gsal ba'i rgyan thams cad nye bar ston pa dang / kha cig ni lag pa spos kyis bskus pa ston pa dang / kha cig ni mkhur ba bskus shing rna cha yang ston pa dang / kha cig ni mgo yang g.yogs shing bzhin yang g.yogs la skad cig tsam gyis ston pa dang / kha cig ni sngon rgod rgod pa dang / dga' dga' ba dang / rtse rtse ba phan tshun dran par byed cing yang ngo tsha ba ltar 'dug pa dang / kha cig ni gzhon nu'i gzugs dang / bu ma btsas pa'i gzugs dang / na chung tshad la bab pa'i gzugs ston pa dang / kha cig ni 'dod pa dang ldan pas byang chub sems dpa' la sgugs pa dang / kha cig ni byang chub sems dpa' la me tog sil mas 'thor ba dag ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i mdun du 'dug nas byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa la rtog cing gdong du yang blta ste/ 'di ci chags pa'i dbang pos blta 'am 'on te mig rgyang ring du blta 'am/ g.yo'am mi g.yo zhes bltas na/ byang chub sems dpa'i bzhin dag cing dri ma med la sgra gcan las thar ba'i zla ba'i dkyil 'khor lta bur 'dug pa dang / nyi ma thog ma shar ba lta bu dang / gser gyi mchod sdong lta bu dang / pad ma 'dab ma stong pa rgyas pa lta bu dang / gtor bar bya ba gtor ba'i me lta bu dang / lhun po ltar mi g.yo ba dang / khor yug ltar mngon par 'phags pa dang / dbang po shin tu bsrungs pa dang / glang po ltar sems shin tu dul bar mthong ngo // de nas bdud kyi bu mo de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' shin tu chags par bya ba'i phyir glu dang gar du sbyar ba'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// dus kyi dam pa sos ka bzang la bab// zhugs shing me tog rgyas kyis dgyes par rol// khyod kyi gzugs ni gzugs bzang mdzes pa ste// mtshan gyis spras pa'i dbang du bdag cag 'gyur// bdag cag skyes pa legs skyes dbyibs legs te// lha mi bde ba'i rkyen du bdag cag byung // byang chub rnyed dkas thugs ni slar sgyur la// myur du bzhengs te dar la bab pa spyod// khyod kyi ched du chas nas rab tu brgyan te lhags gyur pa// lha yi bu mo legs par brgyan pa 'di dag rnams la gzigs// gzugs 'di bltas nas shing rul lta bur srog tsam lus pa yang // chags par 'gyur na chags pas dga' ba su zhig chags mi 'gyur// skra 'jam shin tu dri zhim dri dang ldan// cod pan rna cha 'dab ris bzhin rgyas la// dpral ba legs shing legs byugs bzhin dang ldan// pad ma rgyas pa lta bur mig yangs legs// kha bzhin zla ba nya ba lta bu ste// shing tog bim pa smin 'dra'i mchu dang ldan// dung dang kun da kha ba dkar so ldan// sdug pa dga' la chags pa rnams la gzigs// nu ma shin tu mkhrang zhing rgyas la 'bur// lto ba'i rked na gnyer gsum shin tu mdzes// rked pa 'khor sa lta bur yangs shing mdzes// na chung shin tu mdzes la mgon po gzigs// glang po'i sna 'dra ba yi brla ldan zhing // lag pa gdu bus chal par gang ba can// rked pa gser gyi phag ska rab mdzes brgyan// khyod kyi bran mo 'di la mgon po gzigs// ngang pa'i stabs ldan dal gyis mchi bgyid pa// 'jam zhing yid 'ong 'dod ldan mdzes smra ba// rnam pa 'di ltar shin tu legs brgyan la// lha yi dga' ba rnams la shin tu mkhas// glu dang rol mo'i dbyangs sgra gar rab bslabs// dga' ba'i ched du mdzes pa'i gzugs can skyes// 'dod la rab dga' gal te mi bzhed na// 'jig rten dag na khyod ni shin tu bslus// mi glen nor gyi bde ba mi shes 'ga'// gter mthong nas ni 'bros par bgyid pa ltar// khyod kyang 'dod chags mi mkhyen rang lhags pa// na chung rnams la mi spyod de dang 'dra// dge slong dag de nas byang chub sems dpa' mig mi 'dzums par 'dzum dmul te/ bzhin gyi 'dzum phyung zhing // dbang po rnam par ma 'khrugs pa dang / lus ma bcos pa dang / brjid pa dang / ma chags pa dang / mi sdang ba dang / ma rmongs pa dang / ri'i dbang po ltar mi g.yo ba dang / ma zhum pa dang / ma gyur pa dang / 'dzem pa med pa/ blo shin tu legs par gnas pa dang / nyon mongs pa rnams shin tu spangs pa'i phyir rang gi kha na las pa'i ye shes kyi sgo dang / 'jam zhing snyan pa'i tshig dang / tshangs pa las lhag pa'i nga ro dang / bya ka la ping ka'i sgra dbyangs dang / snyan pa dang / yid du 'ong bas bdud kyi bu mo de dag la tshigs su bcad pas slar smras pa/ 'dod pa sdug bsngal mang po shing sdug bsngal rtsa ba ste// mi mkhas rnams la bsam gtan rdzu 'phrul dka' thub nyams par byed// bud med 'dod pa'i yon tan chog pa med ces mkhas pas smras// nga ni mi mkhas rnams la shes rab chog par byed par 'gyur// 'dod pa bsten na srid pa phyir zhing rnam par 'phel 'gyur te// dper na mi 'ga' la la tshwa chu 'thungs par gyur pa bzhin// de la zhugs pa bdag gi don min gzhan gyi don kyang min// nga ni bdag gi don dang gzhan gyi don la spro ba yin// khyod kyi gzugs ni chu bur dag dang dbu ba mtshungs shing 'dra// sgyu ma'i tshon ltar rang gi blo yis rnam par bsgrubs pa ste// rmi lam dag na rtse ba lta bur mi brtan mi rtag kyang // byis pa mi mkhas rnams kyi sems ni rtag tu rmongs par byed// mig ni chu yi chu bur mtshungs shing 'dra ste pags pas g.yogs// khrag brlang mkhrang zhing 'bur ba dper na nad kyi 'bras dang mtshungs// lto ni gcin dang phyi sa sogs te shin tu mi gtsang ba// sdug bsngal 'khrul 'khor las dang nyon mongs pa las yang dag byung // byis pa'i blo can dag ni rmongs gyur phyin ci log pa yis// lus gang la ni sdug par rtog pa mkhas pa de lta min// sdug bsngal rtsa bar gyur pa'i 'khor bar yun ring 'khor byed na// sems can dmyal ba rnams su sdug bsngal mi bzad mang po myong // rked pa nas ni rab tu yid mi 'ong ba'i dri can 'dzag // brla dang byin pa rkang pa dag ni 'khrul 'khor lta bur gnas// nga yis khyed la yang dag brtags na sgyu ma ji bzhin te// phyin ci log gi rgyu dang rkyen las byung bar gyur pa yin// 'phags pa'i ye shes lam las gol ba phyin ci log gyur pa// me dang dug gi lo ma 'dra zhing sbrul chen khros 'dra ba// 'dod pa'i yon tan yon tan min zhing yon tan nyams mthong na// de la byis pa bde ba'i 'du shes skyed cing brgyal bar gyur// mi gang 'dod pas bud med rnams kyi khol por gyur pa dang // gang zhig chos kyi dga' ba bor te 'dod pas dga' byed cing // dga' la brkam pa de ni tshul khrims lam las gol gyur cing // bsam gtan lam gol blo nyams ye shes las ni rab ring gnas// nga ni 'dod chags zhe sdang lhan cig gnas pa ma yin te// rtag dang sdug dang bdag dang lhan cig gnas par byed ma yin// mi dga' ba dang dga' dang lhan cig gnas pa ma yin la// nga yi sems ni rab tu grol te mkha' la rlung dang 'dra// gal te khyed 'dra'i 'gro ba kun gyis 'dir ni gang gyur la// bskal par de dag rnams dang lhan cig 'dre zhing gnas kyang ni// nga la tha ba med cing chags med gti mug mi 'gyur te// rgyal ba rnams kyi thugs ni nam mkha' mtshungs shing 'dra phyir ro// lha dang lha mo shin tu dri med la// khrag dang rus pa med cing rab bzang ba// de dag kun kyang 'jigs pa cher gnas te// rtag dngos bral zhing ther zug med phyir ro// de nas bdud kyi bu mo bud med kyi sgyu rnams shin tu bslabs pa de dag de bas kyang cher 'dod chags dang / rgyags pa dang / dregs pa bskyed de/ steg pa bstan nas lus rnams brgyan te/ bud med kyi g.yo nye bar bstan nas byang chub sems dpa' la rngod do// de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ bu mo'i nang na gces mchog sred dang dga' dang dga' can lhan cig tu// bdud kyis btang ba shin tu tshul du shis par rings par lhags gyur te// shing gi lcug ma gzhon nu lo mar bcas pa rlung gis bskyod pa bzhin// gar byed cing ni rgyal po'i sras po shing drung 'dug la rngod par byed// dus kyi nang na dam pa mchog tu bgyi ba sos ka'i dus 'di ste// skyes pa dag dang bud med dga' bar bgyid cing mun pa rdul yang bcom// khu byug dang ni ngang pa rma bya sgra 'byin bya tshogs rnams kyis gang // 'dod pa'i yon tan dga' ba myong bar bgyi ba'i dus la da bab bo// bskal pa stong du tshul khrims dga' zhing brtul zhugs dka' thub spyad gyur pa// ri yi rgyal po lta bur mi g.yo nyi ma shar ma thag pa'i gzugs// 'brug bsgrags lta bur sgra snyan dbang po sgra bsgrags 'dra ba po// 'gro la phan pa byed pa de yis don dang ldan pa'i tshig smras pa// 'dod pa rtsod dang dgra dang 'thab dang nyon mongs bcas dang 'jigs byed pa// byis pa'i skye bos nye bar bsten gyi mkhas pa'i skye bos rtag spangs pa// gang du bde gshegs rnams kyis bdud rtsi brnyes pa'i dus la bab gyur gyis// do mod bdud las rgyal te stobs bcu rnams dang ldan pa dgra bcom 'gyur// sgyu rnams bstan nas smras pa zhal ras pad ma 'dra ba gsan du gsol// khyod ni rgyal po dbang phyug dam pa sa bdag stobs dang ldan par 'gyur// bud med dam pa'i tshogs kyis sil snyan stong dag rab tu bgyid 'gyur na// thub pa'i cha byad kyis ni ci bgyis spongs la dga' ba bsten du gsol// byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ nga ni srid pa gsum na dbang phyug lha dang mi rnams kyis mchod la// chos kyi 'khor los 'gro zhing stobs bcu'i stobs dang ldan pa'i rgyal por 'gyur// slob dang mi slob bu rnams khrag khrig rtag tu 'dud pa mngon du byed// chos kyi dga' bas dga' yi yul la nga yi yid ni dga' ma yin// de dag gis smras pa/ re shig dar la bab pa ma yol dang po thor bur gyur pa dang // khyod ni re shig snyun gyis ma btab mi shis bgres par ma gyur dang // ji srid dar la bab cing bdag cag grogs kyang dar la bab gyur pa// de srid bar du 'dzum pa'i zhal gyis 'dod pa'i dga' ba spyad du gsol// byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ ji srid do mod dal ba dam pa 'chi med dkon pa rnyed pa dang // ji srid lha dang lha min grong khyer mi khom sdug bsngal spangs pa dang // ji srid rga dang na dang 'chi ba'i dgra yis dkrugs par ma gyur pa// de srid nga ni 'jigs med grong khyer 'gro ba'i lam mchog bsgom par bya// de dag gis smras pa/ lha yi gnas na sum cu rtsa gsum bdag po lha mos bskor ba dang // 'thab bral 'thab bral rab dang dga' ldan rab dang bdud kyi grong khyer na// lha mchog bstod pa bzhin du bud med dbang du gyur nas 'dod dga' la// rol cing spyod la bdag cag rnams dang lhan cig dgyes pa rgya chen mdzod// byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ 'dod pa rtswa rtse'i zil thigs bzhin du myur la ston ka'i sprin dang mtshungs// klu yi bu mo khro ba lta bur shin tu 'jigs par byed pa yin// brgya byin 'thab bral rab lha dga' ldan pa dag bdud kyi dbang du song // 'phags min rnams kyis 'dod pa sdug bsngal ldan pa 'di la su zhig dga'// de dag gis smras pa/ shing mchog 'di dag lo ma gzhon dang ldan zhing me tog rgyas gyur la// shang shang te'u dang khu byug sgra 'byin bung ba sgra 'byin ldan pa gzigs// sa las rtswa 'khrungs rab sngo 'jam zhing snum la lcang lo can mchis pa// nags mchog mi ci tshogs kyis bsten par na chung rnams dang dgyes par mdzod// byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ lo mar bcas pa'i shing rnams 'di dag dus kyi dbang gis me tog rgyas// bung ba dag kyang bkres dang skom pas nyen nas me tog rnams su lhags// gang zhig dus na sa las skyes pa rnams kyang nyi mas skams par 'gyur// nga 'dir sngon gyi rgyal ba rnams kyis spyad pa bdud rtsi nges par spyad// bdud kyi bu mo rnams kyis smras pa/ zla 'dra'i zhal mnga' gzigs shig pad ma sar pa 'dra ba'i kha bzhin can// snyan cing yid du 'ong ba'i tshig ldan so ni dngul dang kha ba 'dra// 'di 'dra lha yi gnas na dkon na mi yi gnas nag la mchis// gang dag lha mchog rnams kyis rtag tu 'dod par bgyi ba khyod kyis brnyes// byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ lus ni ngan skyugs mi gtsang srin bu'i rigs kyis gang ba shig shig po// myur du 'gyes shing 'jig pa bde ba ma yin rnams dang ldan par mthong // rgyu bar bcas dang mi rgyu ba yi 'gro la bde ba mchog byed pa// go 'phang 'chi 'pho med pa skye bo mkhas pas mchod pa de thob bya// de dag 'dod pa'i sgyu rtsal drug cu rtsa bzhi myong bar gyur pa ste// rkang gdub gser gyi phag ska 'khrol zhing gos kyang shig shig byas nas ni// 'dod pa'i mda' yis phog pa rgyags pa 'dzum zhing 'di skad smras// jo jo khyod la nongs pa ci zhig bgyis na 'di dag bsten mi bgyi// srid pa kun gyis nyes pa rig nas rdul dang bral bas 'di skad smras// 'dod pa ral gri mdung thung rtse gsum sbrang rtsi can gyi spu gri 'dra// sbrul gyi mgo dang me mur 'dra bar ngas 'dir rab tu rig pas na// bud med yon tan 'phrog pas de phyir nga yis bud med tshogs rnams spangs// bud med yon tan rnam pa mang po khrag khrig bye ba de dag gis// gang gi tshe na glang po'i phru gu'i stabs can de brjod ma nus tshe// ngo tsha skyengs nas thub pa'i rkang pa gnyis la rab tu phyag 'tshal te// dga' zhing mgu ba bskyed nas phan pa byed pa de la bstod pa byas// pad ma dri ma med pa'i snying po 'dra zhing ston zla lta bu'i zhal// mar gyis sbyin bsreg bgyis pa'i 'od 'phro me 'dra gser gyi ri 'dra ba// srid pa brgya nas spyad cing dgongs dang smon lam btab pa grub gyur cig // bdag nyid rgal nas sdug bsngal dag dang ldan pa'i 'gro ba bsgral du gsol// de dag rnams kyis dong ka'i shing dang tsam pa ka 'dra rnam mang bstod// mchog tu gyur pa'i ri ltar mi g.yo ba la bskor ba byas nas ni// song ste pha yi rkang la mgo bos phyag 'tshal 'di skad tshig kyang smras// yab cig lha dang mi yi bla ma de la khong khro spangs na legs// bzhin ni 'dzum par gyur nas pad ma'i 'dab ma 'dra ba'i mig gis lta// de ni chags pas skye bo mi lta de la khro gnyer mchis ma lags// lhun po g.yo zhing rgya mtsho skams la nyi zla ltung bar 'gyur yang gda'// srid pa gsum gyi nyes mthong de ni bud med rnams kyi dbang mi 'gyur// de nas bdud sdig can gyis tshig de skad thos nas de bas kyang cher sdug bsngal zhing yid mi bde la/ yi ma rangs shing tshig pa za ba'i yid kyis rang gi bu mo de dag la smras pa/ kye mi shes shing glen te/ khyed kyi gzugs dang da rod ma mthong ngam// ji ltar gyur na de byang chub kyi snying po las bslang bar ma nus/ de nas bdud kyi bu mo de dag gis rang gi pha la tshigs su bcad pas slar smras pa/ snyan cing 'jam por smra yang chags pa ma mchis te// gsang ba chen po lta yang sdang ba mchis ma lags// spyod lam dag dang spyod pa lta yang rmongs ma mchis// lus rnams thams cad rtogs kyang bsam pa shin tu zab// bud med nongs pa rgya chen the tshom ma mchis rtogs// 'dod las dben pa'i yid ldan 'dod chags chags ma mchis// gang zhig de yi sems dang spyod pa yongs 'tshal ba// lha yul mi yul 'di na lha mi de ma mchis// de la bud med sgyu rnams gang lags bstan na yab// chags bcas gang lags de yi snying zhu 'gyur rigs na// de dag mthong yang de yi sems ni gcig ma g.yos// ri dbang rgyal po bzhin du de ni mi g.yo g.yo ma mchis// bsod nams gzi brjid brgyas bltam yon tan gzi brjid rdzogs// bskal pa bye ba mang por tshul khrims brtul zhugs spyad// lha dang tshangs pa sems can gzi brjid rnam dag dge / de dag de yi rkang par mgos gtugs phyag kyang 'tshal// sde dang bcas pa'i bdud rnams bcom nas sngon chad kyi// rgyal bas bzhed pa byang chub dam pa 'thob 'gyur nges// yab cig bdag cag g.yul ngor 'thab pa mi 'tshal te// stobs ldan dag dang 'thab par sbyor 'di tshegs rab che// yab cig mkha' la nor bu rin chen gtsug phud can// rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' khrag khrig gus par gnas// rin chen 'byung gnas yan lag me tog phreng bas brgyan// stobs bcu mnga' bas mchod phyir 'dir btang rnams la gzigs// gang dag sems pa ma mchis gang dag sems ma mchis// shing ri lha dbang gnod sbyin mkha' lding dbang po dag // yon tan ri bor mngon par 'dud cing phyogs pa las// yab cig do mod slar log na ni legs pa 'dra// gzhan yang gang gi pha mthar mi phyin der ni rkyal mi bgyi// gang zhig rtsa nas mi phyin de ni brko mi bgyi// gang la bzod pa yang gsol de ni dkrug mi bgyi// gang gis yid mi bde bar 'gyur ba de mi bgyi// dge slong dag de nas de'i tshe shing gi lha mo brgyad la 'di lta ste/ dpal ldan dang / 'phel mo dang / dka' thub dang / dge ma dang / mkhas ma dang / mdangs stobs dang / bden smra dang / ldan ma ste/ de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' la yang dag par mchod nas dpal rnam pa bcu drug gis byang chub sems dpa' 'phel bar byed/ mngon du stod par byed de/ sems can dam pa khyod ni dgung zla yar gyi ngo ltar mdzes pa'o// blo rnam par dam pa khyod ni gdugs dang po shar ba ltar lhang nge ba'o// sems can dam pa khyod ni chab kyi nang na pad ma ltar rab tu rgyas pa'o// sems can dam pa khyod ni nags dang nags 'dab na rgyu ba'i seng ge ltar sgrogs pa'o// sems can dam pa khyod ni rgya mtsho'i dbus na ri'i rgyal po ltar mdzes pa'o// sems can dam pa khyod ni khor yug gi ri ltar mngon par 'phags pa'o// sems can dam pa khyod ni rgya mtsho ltar rin po ches bltams shing gting dpag dka' ba'o// 'jig rten gyi mgon po khyod ni nam mkha' ltar thug pa ma mchis shing thugs kyi rgya che ba'o// sems can rnam par dag pa khyod ni dog sa ltar sems can thams cad kyi 'tsho bar gyur cing thugs shin tu brtan pa'o// sems can dam pa khyod ni mtsho ma dros pa ltar rtag tu dang zhing thugs rnyog pa mi mnga' ba'o// sems can dam pa khyod ni rlung mar ltar 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad la rtag tu mi chags shing thugs gnas ma mchis pa'o/ sems can dam pa khyod ni gzi brjid kyi rgyal po ltar rlom sems can thams cad spangs shing bsnyen par dka' ba'o// sems can dam pa khyod ni sred med kyi bu ltar thul bar dka' zhing stobs dang ldan pa'o// 'jig rten gyi mgon po khyod ni byang chub kyi snying po las mi bzhengs pas dam bcas pa brtan pa'o// sems can dam pa khyod ni dbang po'i lag gis 'phangs pa'i rdo rje ltar slar mi ldog pa'o// sems can dam pa khyod ni ring por mi thogs par stobs bcu dang ldan par byon pas brnyes pa legs par brnyes pa'o// dge slong dag de ltar byang chub kyi shing gi lha mo rnams kyis dpal rnam sdig can phyir ma log go// de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ lha yi tshogs kyis yang dag bskul ba thos kyang bdud ni phyir log ma gyur te// slongs shig rgyob shig 'di ni brlag par gyis shig srog kyang sbyin par ma byed cig // 'di ni rang nyid rgyal nas nga yi yul nas gzhan yang sgrol bar byed par 'gyur// langs te bros pa ma gtogs dge sbyong 'di la thar gzhan cung zad med ces smras// byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ ri yi rgyal po lhun po gnas nas g.yo srid 'gro ba thams cad med 'gyur srid// skar ma'i tshogs rnams thams cad zla ba bcas par mkha' las sa la ltung yang srid// sems can kun gyi bsam pa gcig byed 'gyur srid rgya mtsho chen po skam srid kyi// nga 'dra shing gi rgyal po'i drung na 'dug pa la ni g.yo ba yong mi srid// bdud kyis smras pa/ kho bo 'dod pa'i dbang phyug 'jig rten 'di kun dbang // lha dang lha min tshogs bcas mi dang dud 'gro rnams// kho bos khyab ste thams cad kho bo'i dbang du 'gyur// kho bo'i yul na 'dug pa longs la tshig bzhin gyis// byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ gal te 'dod dbang khyod yin gsal bar khyod dbang min// yang dag nga ltos nga yang chos kyi dbang phyug yin// gal te ngan 'gror mi 'gro khyod ni 'dod dbang phyug // dbang med khyod ni lta bzhin byang chub ngas thob 'gyur// bdud kyis smras pa/ dge sbyong bdag nyid gcig pu dgon par ci zhig byed// khyod kyis gang btsal de dang phrad par sla ma yin// rab 'gro shes ldan la sogs dka' thub rab bsgrims kyang // go 'phang mchog de ma thob mir gyur khyod ci smos// byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ khro ba'i zil non blo dang lha yul 'dod pa dang // bdag la rtag dang mi rtag snyam du gnas pa dang // yul du 'gro bas gnas pa thar snyam gnas pa yi// drang srong mi shes sngon du 'gro bas dka' thub spyad// de dag yang dag don dang bral zhing skyes bu smra// khyab dang phyogs gcig ches dang kha cig rtag ces smra// lus can lus min yon tan min dang yon tan can// byed pa po dang byed po min zhes gzhan dag 'dzer// stan 'dir 'dug ste nga rgyal bcom pas sde dpung bcas// khyod pham byas te byang chub rdul med deng thob nas// 'gro ba 'di la 'byung dang byung dang mya ngan 'das// sdug bsngal zhi ba bsil ba'i dngos po bstan par bya// bdud ni khros shing 'khrugs te tshig pa zos nas mdun du rtsub pa'i tshig tu smras pa dge sbyong 'di zung shig // gcig pu dgon par bor bar gyur pa 'di ni nga yi mdun nas zung la song ste myur du dbang du gyis// nga yi khyim du myur du song la shing sgrog dang ni lcags sgrog phrugs su chug ste sgo ba byed du chug // sdug bsngal nyen nas ku co rnam pa mang po 'don cing lha yi khol po yin par bdag gis bdag mthong byos// byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ nam mkha' la ni ri mo rnam pa sna tshogs cha cha ris ris phye ste so sor bri bar nus kyang srid// phyogs dang phyogs mtshams 'gro ba'i shugs can rlung ni mi yis rab tu bsgrims te zhags pas bcing du nus kyang srid// nyi ma zla ba mun pa rab rib med byed mkha' las sa la ltung bar byed pa nus srid kyi// khyod dang 'dra ba rab tu mang po bgrang las 'das pa dag gis shing drung nas ni nga bskyod nus mi 'gyur// bdud dpung stobs dang ldan pa langs te ha zhes zer// dung dang rnga dang rdza rnga mchog gi sgra 'byin langs// bdud dpung shin tu 'jigs pa 'di dag mthong nas ni// kyi hud bu sdug khyod cis ma rung gyur ces zer// 'dzam klung gser dang tsam pa'i snying po 'dra bar ser// shin tu gzhon nu lha mis bstod cing mchod pa'i 'os// khyod deng g.yul ngo chen por rab tu brlag 'gyur te// dbang pos lha min lta bur bdud kyi dbang du 'gyur// tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang ka la ping ka'i sgra skad kyis// bde bar gshegs pas gnod sbyin srin tshogs de la smras// mi mkhas gang zhig nam mkha' skrag par byed 'dod pa// de ni shing mchog rtsi reg shog ces// sems can rnams kyis mtshungs med sems kyis byang chub smon// dge slong dag de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub kyi shing drung na seng ge'i gdan la bzhugs te mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas/ skad cig de la sangs rgyas kyi rnam par rol pa dpag tu med pa mdzad de/ de dag ni bskal par yang bstan par sla ba ma yin no// de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ sa ni lag mthil lta bur mnyam par gnas par gyur/ 'dab ma brgya pa rgyas pa 'od dang ldan pa byung // lha rnams brgya stong byang chub snying por rab tu 'dud// seng ge sgra yi mtshan ma dang po 'di 'dir mthong // stong gsum shing brgya dag dang ri rnams du ma dang / ri yi rgyal po lhun po byang chub snying por 'dud// stobs bcu'i gan du song ste brgya byin tshangs pa 'dud// 'di yang mi yi seng ge byang chub snying por rol// sku las 'od zer brgya stong dag ni rab bkye ste// rgyal ba'i zhing mchog khyab nas ngan song gsum po zhi// de nas skad cig yud tsam mi khom skams par gyur// sems can gang la'ang tha ba rgyags sdang gnod pa med// 'di yang mi yi seng ge gdan la bzhugs pa'i rol// nyi zla nor bu me dang glog dang lha yi 'od// 'od dang ldan pa'i rlabs kyis zil mnan lam me min// 'gro ba gang gis kyang ni ston pa'i gtsug mi mthong // 'di yang mi yi seng ge gdan la bzhugs pa'i rol// phyag gi mthil gyis reg nas sa yang rnam drug g.yos// de yi bdud kyi sde rnams shing bal bzhin du dkrugs// bdud ni mda' thogs sa la ri mo gang 'dri ba// 'di yang mi yi seng ge gdan la rol pa lags// mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i le'u zhes bya ba ste nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa'o// // de nas gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu rnams kyis byang chub kyi snying po la bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa la bskor ba byas te/ lha'i tsan dan gyi phye ma'i char mngon par phab nas/ tshul dang 'thun pa'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis bstod do// 'jig rten gsal bar mdzad pa byung // 'jig rten mgon po 'od mdzad pa// 'jig rten ldongs par gyur pa la// nyon mongs spangs pa mig sbyin pa// khyod ni g.yul las rnam par rgyal// bsod nams dag gis dgongs pa rdzogs// dkar po'i chos rnams kun du rdzogs// khyod ni 'gro ba tshim mdzad 'gyur// sdig pa mi mnga' 'dam las rgal// gau ta ma ni thang la bzhugs// sems can gzhan dag rlung chen gyis// khyer ba rnams kyang sgrol bar 'gyur// shes rab chen po khyod 'phags te// 'jig rten dag na zla ma mchis// 'jig rten chos kyis khyod mi gos// chab na mchis pa'i pad ma bzhin// 'jig rten ring nas gnyid log 'di// mun pa'i phung pos gtibs pa la// khyod ni shes rab sgron me yis// rab tu sad par mdzad pa spyod// 'tsho ba'i 'jig rten ring nas ni// nyon mongs nad kyis gzir ba la// nad rnams kun las thar mdzad pa// sman pa'i rgyal po yang dag byung // 'jig rten mgon po khyod byung bas// mi khom rnams ni stongs par 'gyur// lha rnams dang ni mi dag kyang // bde ba rnams dang ldan par 'gyur// skyes bu khyu mchog des pa khyod// lta bar gang dag 'dong bgyid pa// de dag bskal pa stong rnams su// nam yang ngan 'gror mchi mi 'gyur// gang dag chos nyan 'gyur ba rnams// de dag mkhas shing nad med dang // zag dang phung po zad pa dang // 'jigs pa med pa rnams su 'gyur// nyon mongs bcings pa bcad nas ni// kun kyang len pa ma mchis par// myur du rab tu grol 'gyur te// dge ba mchog gi 'bras bu 'thob// de dag 'jig rten sbyin gnas te// sbyin pa rnams ni blang ba'i 'os// de dag yon phul mi chung ste// kun kyang mya ngan 'das rgyu lags// dge slong dag de ltar gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa la mngon par bstod nas thal mo sbyar te/ de bzhin gshegs pa la phyag 'tshal zhing phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de nas 'od gsal gyi lha'i bu rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub kyi snying po la bzhugs pa la me tog dang / bdug pa dang / spos dang / phreng ba dang / byug pa dang / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan rnam pa sna tshogs rnams kyis cho ga bzhin du mchod nas lan gsum bskor ba byas te/ tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod do// thub pa thugs zab gsung ni shin tu snyan// thub mchog tshangs dbyangs glu ltar gsung snyan mchog // byang chub rab mchog shin tu dam pa brnyes// dbyangs kun mthar phyin khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// khyod skyabs khyod gling khyod ni dpung gnyen te// khyod ni 'jig rten mgon po byams thugs mdzad// khyod ni sman pa'i dam pa zug rngu 'byin// gso ba phan mdzad khyod ni dam pa mchog // mar me mdzad pa gzigs ma thag tu khyod// byams dang thugs rje'i sprin gyi dra ba bsgrubs// mgon po bdud rtsi'i rgyun gyi char phob la// lha mi rnams kyi gdung ba zhi bar mdzod// khyod ni srid gsum mi gos pad ma 'dra// khyod ni mi g.yo mi bskyod lhun po 'dra// khyod ni thugs dam mi g.yo rdo rje bzhin// yon tan mchog kun mnga' ste zla ba 'dra// dge slong dag de ltar 'od gsal ba'i lha rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa la mngon par bstod nas thal mo sbyar te/ de bzhin gshegs pa la phyag 'tshal zhing phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de nas lha'i bu rab tshangs pa la sogs pa tshangs ris kyi lha rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub kyi snying po la bzhugs pa la nor bu rin po che bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du mas spras pa'i rin po che'i dra bas bkab ste lan gsum bskor ba byas nas tshul dang 'thun pa'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod do// dge ba dri med shes rab 'od dang gzi brjid ldan// mtshan gyi dam pa sum cu rtsa gnyis mchog mnga' ba// dran dang ldan zhing blo gros ldan pa ye shes mnga'// mnyel ba mi mnga' khyod la mgo bos phyag 'tshal lo// dri gsum dri mi mnga' ba dri med dri ma bral// 'jig rten gsum du grags shing rig pa gsum brnyes pa// rnam par thar pa dam pa gsum gyi mig sbyin pa// spyan gsum dri ma mi mnga' khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// dus ngan rnyog pa bsal zhing rab tu zhi thugs ldan// thugs brtse thugs rjes 'phags pa 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa// thub pa dgyes pas 'phags pa thugs ni rab zhi ba// khyod ni yid gnyis grol bar mdzad pa btang snyoms dgyes// brtul zhugs dka' thub 'phags pa 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa// rang spyod rnam par dag cing spyod pa'i pha rol byon// bden pa bzhi po ston pa rnam thar dgyes pa po// grol bar gyur nas 'gro ba gzhan yang grol mdzad pa/ stobs dang brtson 'grus ldan pa'i bdud po 'dir lhags pa// shes rab brtson 'grus de bzhin byams pas pham mdzad nas// khyod kyis go 'phang dam pa 'chi ba med pa brnyes// g.yon can dpung rnams bcom pa khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// dge slong dag de zhing phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de nas bdud kyi bu dkar po'i phyogs pa de dag de bzhin gshegs pa ga la ba der song ste phyin pa dang / rin po che'i gdugs dang / bla re chen po rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa mngon par bkab nas thal mo sbyar te/ de bzhin gshegs pa la tshul dang 'thun pa'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod do// khyod stobs shin tu rgya che ba dang bdud dpung drag po bdag cag mngon sum ste// bdud dpung rab 'jigs chen po de yang khyod kyis skad cig gcig la pham par mdzad// khyod ni bzhengs par ma gyur sku yang mi g.yo gsung yang brjod pa ma mdzad de// thub pa don kun 'grub pa 'jig rten gsum gyis mchod pa khyod la bdag phyag 'tshal// bdud kyi bu mo bye ba khrag khrig stong phrag du ma gang gA'i bye ma snyed// de dag rnams kyis byang chub shing mchog drung nas khyod ni bskyod cing g.yo ma nus// mchod sbyin bye ba khrag khrig stong phrag du ma gang gA'i bye ma snyed mdzad de// byang chub shing drung bzhugs pa des na de ring khyod ni rnam par mdzes pa lags// byang chub spyad pa dam pa spyod mdzad tshe na shin tu sdug pa'i btsun mo dang // phangs pa'i sras dang bran pho bran mo de bzhin skyed mos tshal dang grong khyer dang // yul 'khor grong rdal dag dang rgyal srid rnams dang btsun mo'i 'khor dang glang po dang // dbu dang spyan dang ljags dang de bzhin zhabs btang des na de ring rnam par mdzes// nga ni sangs rgyas 'gyur te bsam gtan rdzu 'phrul blo yi go bgos nas// sems can bye ba khrag khrig mang po sdug bsngal rgya mtshos khyer bar gyur pa rnams// dam chos gru yis nyid kyis bsgral bar bya zhes khyod kyis lan mang gsung brjod pa// khyod kyis smon lam de ni grub lags srog chags rnams kyang sgrol bar mdzad par 'gyur// smra ba'i khyu mchog 'jig rten mig sbyin mdzad pa khyod la bstod pa'i bsod nams de// bdag cag thams cad dga' mgu yid gyur 'tshang rgyar 'gyur bar shog // dge slong dag de ltar bdud kyi bu rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa la mngon par bstod nas thal mo sbyar te/ de bzhin gshegs pa la phyag 'tshal zhing phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de nas lha'i bu gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha'i bu brgya stong du mas yongs su bskor te/ mdun du bdar nas de bzhin gshegs pa la 'dzam bu klung gi gser gyi pad ma dag gis mngon par gtor te/ spyan snga nas tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod do// gsung ni dpyas ma mchis shing ma 'khrul rnam par ma 'khrugs pa// mun rdul bral zhing 'chi med rtogs par thugs su chud par gyur// lha yul mi yul pa yi dpal dang bgyi ba gzhal med 'os// rab tu 'bar ba'i blo gros ldan la mgo bos phyag 'tshal lo// dka' ba mdzad pa nyon mongs spong ba rdul dang dri ma sel// shin tu dga' ba'i gsung gis 'dzin dang sdug bsngal log 'dzin rgya chen 'dor sel te// lha mi blo gros 'dul ba ji lta bzhin du 'dul ba mdzod// zla ba bzhin du mkha' las phyogs bzhi dag tu rnam rgyu ba// srid pa gsum 'dir rmad par rdzogs par byang chub pa la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir bar snang thams cad rin po che'i dra ba dang / dril bu g.yer ka'i dra ba dang / rin po che'i gdugs rnams dang / rin po che'i ba dan rnams dang / rin po che dang dar gyi lda ldi dang / rin po che'i me tog rna rgyan dang / mu tig gi chun khor dang / me tog gi lda ldi sna tshogs rnams lus phyed phyung ba'i lha rnams kyis bzung ba dang / zla gam rnams kyis legs par brgyan nas de bzhin gshegs pa la phul lo// phul nas kyang spyan snga nas tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod do// thub pa mkhas la bdag cag mchis nas ni// 'gro ba'i spyod kun ji bzhin gsal bltas shing // sems can dag pa khyod kyi spyod bltas na// de ltar khyod kyi thugs gcig 'khrul ma mthong // mchod phyir byang chub sems dpa' gang lhags pa// mi yi 'dren pa de dag nam mkha' khyab// 'di ltar de dag nam mkha'i lus lags pas// gzhal med khang rnams la yang gnod ma mchis// bar snang nas ni me tog char bab pa// stong chen byur bur rab tu gang gyur pa// de dag ma lus khyod kyi skur bab kyang // 'bab chu rgya mtshor bab pa bzhin du gyur// gdugs dang me tog rna rgyan me tog phreng // me tog tsam pa ka yi lda ldi dang // rgyan phreng zla ba zla gam rnams kyang 'thor// lha yis gtor kyang 'dres par gyur ma mchis// bar snang thams cad lha yis gang gyur te// 'di la skra tsam gzhag pa'i gnas ma mchis// rkang gnyis mchog la mchod pa bgyid kyang ni// khyod la rgyags pa'am ngo mtshar 'gyur mi mnga'// de ltar bar snang gi lha rnams kyis byang chub kyi snying po la bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa la mngon par bstod nas thal mo sbyar te/ de bzhin gshegs pa la phyag 'tshal zhing phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de nas sa bla'i lha rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir sa gzhi thams cad legs par phyags te byugs nas spos chus chag chag btab ste/ me tog gis chal bar bkang nas ras bcos bu sna tshogs kyi bla re bres te de bzhin gshegs pa la phul nas tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod do// stong gsum rdo rje lta bur mi shigs gnas par gyur// nga 'dir pags pa sha dang rus pa rkang skams kyang // byang chub ma reg nga ni 'di nas mi ldang zhes// rdo rje'i gnas kyis de ni byang chub snying por bzhugs// gal te mi yi seng ge khyod kyis stong gsum kun// byin gyis ma brlabs na ni gang dag rkang mthil gyis// bye ba'i zhing rnams bskyod pa de ltar shugs che ba// byang chub sems dpa' lhags tshe ma lus zhig par 'gyur// sa phyogs gang du sems can dam pa 'chag pa ni// sa yi lha yis rnyed pa rgya chen legs par rnyed// 'jig rten rdul rnams ji snyed khyod kyis snang bar mdzad// stong gsum mchod rten gyur na khyod sku smos ci 'tshal// 'og gi chu yi phung po brgya stong ji snyed dang // sa yi steng na 'gro ba'i 'tsho ba ji snyed pa// stong gsum sa rnams thams cad bdag cag gzung bar bgyi// khyod la kun 'bul ji ltar bzhed bzhin spyad du gsol// gang du khyod ni bzhugs sam 'chag gam mnal ba dang // gau tam bde bar gshegs pa'i sras po nyan thos gang // chos gtam smra dang gang yang de dag mnyan pa dang // dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad byang chub phyir bsngo'o// de ltar sa bla'i lha rnams kyis byang chub kyi snying po la bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa la mngon par bstod nas thal mo sbyar te/ de bzhin gshegs pa la phyag 'tshal zhing phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// mngon par bstod pa'i le'u zhes bya ba ste nyi shu rtsa gsum pa'o// // dge slong dag de ltar mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa lha rnams kyis bstod cing skyil mo krung ma bshig // spyan mi 'dzums par shing gi rgyal po la gzigs shing bsam gtan dang dga' ba'i zas kyi bde ba myong bar byang chub kyi shing drung du zhag bdun 'das par gyur to// de nas zhag bdun 'das pa dang / 'dod pa na spyod pa'i lha'i bu rnams spos chu'i bum pa khri thogs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa ga la ba der lhags so// gzugs na spyod pa'i lha'i bu rnams kyang spos chu'i bum pa khri thogs te// de bzhin gshegs pa ga la ba der dong ste lhags nas/ byang chub kyi shing dang / de bzhin gshegs pa la spos chus bkrus so// lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po bgrang ba las 'das pa dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku la phog pa'i spos chu des rang rang gi lus la bskus so// bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang sems bskyed do// lha'i bu la sogs pa de dag rang rang gi gnas su phyin kyang spos chu de dang ma bral bar gyur te/ spos gzhan la 'dod pa mi skyed do// de dag de bzhin gshegs pa la gus par yid la bya ba las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang / mchog tu dga' ba des bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par gyur to// dge slong dag de nas lha'i bu kun nas me tog ces bya ba 'khor de nyid du 'dus par gyur pa des de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhabs gnyis la gtugs te/ thal mo sbyar nas de bzhin gshegs pa la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ting nge 'dzin gang dang ldan pas de bzhin gshegs pa la dgung bdun du skyil mo krung ma bshig par bzhugs pa'i ting nge 'dzin de'i ming ci zhes bgyi/ dge slong dag de skad ces gsol pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa des lha'i bu de la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// lha'i bu ting nge 'dzin 'di'i ming ni dga' ba'i zas bkod pa zhes bya ste/ ting nge 'dzin 'di dang ldan pas de bzhin gshegs pa zhag bdun du skyil mo krung ma bshig par bzhugs so// dge slong dag de nas lha'i bu kun nas me tog gis de bzhin gshegs pa la tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod do// zhabs ni 'khor los khyab pa po// pad 'dab rdul med stong gzi ldan// lha yi cod pan zhabs gtugs pa// dpal stug zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo// bde gshegs zhabs la phyag 'tshal nas// de tshe lha bu de sems dga'// lha min rab tu zhi byed pa// yid gnyis sel ba'i tshig 'di smras// shAkya'i rigs la dgyes skyed pa// chags sdang gti mug mthar 'byin pa// zhus pa rnams kyang mthar 'byin pa// lha mi'i dogs pa bsal du gsol// dpag med thams cad mkhyen pa nyid// sangs rgyas stobs bcu ci slad du// rgyal ba dog sa'i snying por ni// dgung bdun skyil mo krung ma bshig // 'dab brgya rgyas pa'i spyan mnga' ba// ci zhig gzigs na dgung bdun du// mi yi seng ge rnam dag spyan// spyan mi 'dzums par gzigs pa mdzad// gang gis shing rgyal drung du ni// skyil krung ma bshig dgung bdun bzhugs// smon lam 'di ni khyod kyi 'am// smra ba'i seng ge kun gyi lags// tshems ni mnyam zhing rnam dag pa// stobs bcu'i zhal ni dri rab gda'// ma nor legs par bka' stsol te// lha dang mi rnams dga' bar mdzod// zla 'dra'i zhal gyis bka' stsal pa// ngas bshad lha yi bu nyon cig // ngas ni dris pa de yi lan// cung zad tsam zhig bshad par bya// dper na rgyal po phyogs gang du// gnyen gyi tshogs kyis dbang bskur ba// zhag bdun bar du sa phyogs de// mi 'dor rgyal po'i chos nyid do// de bzhin stobs bcu mnga' ba yang // gang tshe smon rdzogs dbang bskur ba// sa yi snying por zhag bdun du// rgyal ba skyil mo krung mi 'jig // dper na dpa' bo dgra tshogs rnams// ma lus pham byas lta ba ltar// byang chub snying por sangs rgyas kyang // nyon mongs bcom nas gzigs pa mdzad// gti mug byung ba'i 'dod dang khro// de dag 'gro ba'i dgra 'dra ste// chom po chas ni bzang 'dra ba// de dag ma lus ngas 'dir bshig // ngas 'dir nga rgyal rnam dgu dang // gnas med rlom sems rab tu bcom// zag pa thams cad rab tu spangs// nga yi ye shes dam pa skyes// ngas 'dir sred pa'i srid rgyu dang // ma rig bya min byed pa de// bag nyal bcas rtsa dra ba rnams// ye shes gsal ba'i me yis bsregs// ngas 'dir nga dang nga yi dang // nyes zhags ring 'gro rtsa zug pa// sgrib pa'i mdud pa dam po de// ye shes mtshon gyis bcad par gyur// ngas 'dir ring nas nga'i ldan pa// slu ba tha ma rnam 'jig pa// len par bcas pa'i phung po de// ye shes kyis ni yongs su shes// gnyis su rmongs pa log 'dzin pa// tha mar dmyal 'gyur de dag rnams// ngas 'dir ma lus bsal byas te// phyin chad nam yang skyer mi 'gyur// ngas 'dir dge ba'i rtsa ba yi// me yis sgrib pa'i nags tshal bsregs// phyin ci log ni rnam bzhi yang // nga yis ma lus nges par bsregs// 'du shes skud pas brgyus pa yi// rnam rtog phreng ba gnod byed pa// ngas 'dir byang chub yan lag gi// phreng ba sna tshogs rnams kyis bzlog // bgrod dka' drug cu rtsa lnga dang // gti mug sum cu dri ma can// sdig pa dag ni bzhi bcu ngas// sa yi snying po 'dir bsal te// sa yi snying por 'dug nas ngas// sdom pa ma yin bcu drug dang // khams ni rnam pa brgyad dang // khyab pa nyi shu rtsa lnga bsal// nyon mongs chu bo nyi shu dang // 'gro ba 'jigs pa nyi shu brgyad// brtson 'grus mthu dang brtul ba yis// nga 'dir de dag shin tu 'das// de bzhin sangs rgyas bsgyings sgrog pa// lnga brgya ngas 'dir yang dag rtogs// brgya phrag stong du tshang ba yi// chos rnams nga yis yang dag rtogs// ngas 'dir bag nyal ma lus pa// dgu bcu rtsa brgyad rtsar bcas mtha'// kun nas ldang ba'i lo ma rnams// ye shes me yis nges par bsregs// dogs dang yid gnyis kun 'byung ba// lta ba'i chu yis gang gyur pa// mi dge ngogs can sred pa'i klung // shugs drag ye shes nyi mas bskams// tshul 'chos pa dang kha gsag spangs// sgyu dang ser sna phrag dog sdang // nyon mongs dgon pa 'dir bcad// 'dul ba'i me yis rab tu bsregs// 'dir ni rtsod pa'i rtsa ba de// ngan 'gro nyam ngar 'dren byed pa// 'phags la skur pa 'debs pa'i tshig // ye shes mchog gi sman gyis bskyugs// ngas 'dir ye shes yon tan dang // ting 'dzin thob nas ngu ba dang // cho nge 'don dang mya ngan dang // smre ba ma lus mtha' mar phyin// ngas 'dir bden tshul ting nge 'dzin// thob nas chu bo sbyor ba dang // mdud pa mya ngan zug rngu dang // rgyags dang bag med kun las rgyal// ngas 'dir nyon mongs gzings pa yi// srid pa'i ljon shing rtog rtsa brtan// dran pa'i sta res ma lus par// bcad nas ye shes me yis bsregs// ngas 'dir nga snyam nga rgyal te// khams gsum dbang byed stobs che ba// g.yon can ye shes ral gris bcom// lha min dbang la dbang po bzhin// dra ba ma lus sum cu drug // 'jug pa sa yi snying po 'dir// shes rab ral gri stobs ldan pas// bcad nas ye shes me yis bsregs// nyon mongs rtsa ba bag nyal bcas// sdug bsngal mya ngan 'byung de dag // ngas 'dir shes rab dam pa yi// thong lcags kyis ni ma lus bton// rang bzhin gyis dag sems can gyi// shes rab mig 'dir nga yis sbyangs// ye shes mig sman chen po yis// gti mug ling tog rgya chen bsal// 'byung khams bzhi po rgyags pa yi// chu srin gyis dkrugs sred yangs pa// srid pa'i rgya mtsho dran pa dang // zhi gnas nyi ma'i 'od kyis bskams// ngas 'dir yul gyi shing gi tshogs// rnam rtog dud 'thul chags chen me// rab tu 'bar ba rnam thar chu// bsil ba'i khu bas bsad par gyur// ngas 'dir bag la nyal ba'i sprin// ro myang glog 'dra rnam rtog 'brug // brtson 'grus stobs kyi rlung shugs kyis// 'das te kun du gtor bar gyur// ngas 'dir dran pa dri med pa'i// ting 'dzin thob nas sems spyod dgra// srid pa'i khon rgyud ma lus par// shes rab ral gri'i stobs kyis bcad// ngas 'dir rgyal mtshan mchog 'chang ba// shing rta glang po rtas mtho ba// gzugs bsgyur bdud dpung brtson pa'i sde// byams pa thob nas rnam par bcom// mi sdug ting nge 'dzin thob nas// ngas 'dir dbang po drug gi rta// 'dod pa'i yon tan lngas rtas pa// rtag tu rgyags yan ma lus btags// smon med ting nge 'dzin thob nas// ngas 'dir rjes su chags pa dang // khong khro ba dang 'thab pa dang // rtsod spang ma lus mtha' mar phyin// stong pa'i ting nge 'dzin thob nas// ngas 'dir phyi dang nang dag gi// rlom sems kun dang rtog pa dang // rnam par rtog pa yongs su zad// mtshan med ting nge 'dzin thob nas// lha mi srid pa'i rtser thug pa'i// bde ba thams cad ma lus par// nga yis 'dir ni yongs su btang // ngas 'dir rnam thar gsum thob nas// ngas 'dir shes rab stobs kyis ni// srid pa dag gi 'ching ba kun// ma lus kun las grol bar gyur// ngas 'dir rgyu mthong gyur nas ni// rtag dang mi rtag 'du shes dang // bdag dang bdag med bde sdug bsngal// rgyu yi 'du shes gsum las rgyal// ngas 'dir las kyi rnam pa dang // skye mched drug rtsa kun 'byung las// byung ba thams cad shing dbang drung // mi rtag pa yis bsnun te bcad// ngas 'dir ye shes nyi ma yis// gti mug mun pa'i rnyog pa dang // lta gyur rgyags dang khros gang ba// yun ring mun pa bsal snang byas// ngas 'dir brtson 'grus stobs kyi grus// 'dod dang chags pa'i chu srin can// ngar 'dzin lta ngan sred rlabs chu// 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho che las rgal// gang rtogs chags dang gti mug dang // sems kyi rnam par rtog bsregs te// phye leb nags mer lhung 'dra ba// ngas 'dir de ni rjes su rtogs// nga 'dir ring nas song ba yi// bskal pa dpag med bye khrag khrig // 'khor ba'i lam gyis nyon mongs pa// gdung ba med nas ngal yang sos// 'jig rten phan phyir rga shi dang // mya ngan sdug bsngal mthar phyin pa// phas rgol kun gyis ma thob pa// bdud rtsi de ni ngas 'dir rtogs// sred las byung ba'i skye mched kyis// sdug bsngal phung pos sdug bsngal ba// phyis mi 'byung ba 'jigs med kyi// grong khyer 'dir ni ngas phyin to// ngas 'dir nang gi dgra chen po// khyab pa de dag rjes su rtogs// rtogs nas rab tu bsregs te ngas// de dag yang byung gnas med byas// bdud rtsi'i don du bskal pa ni// bye ba khrag khrig rang gi sha// mig dang rin chen mang btang ba// de 'dir nga yis rjes su rtogs// sngon gyi rgyal ba dpag med pas// gang sangs rgyas de ngas 'dir rtogs// gang gi snyan pa nyams dga' ba// sgra ni 'jig rten rnams su grags// rten nas byung ba'i 'gro ba stong // sems kyi skad cig gcig la 'jig // smig rgyu dri za'i grong khyer 'dra// de 'dir nga yis rjes su rtogs// gang gis lag pa'i mthil du ni// shing tog bzhag bzhin 'jig rten khams// thams cad mthong ba'i mig mchog de// nga yis 'dir ni dag par byas// sngon gyi gnas ni ngas 'dir dran// rig pa gsum yang thob par gyur// bskal pa khrag khrig dpag med pa// gnyid kyis log las sad bzhin dran// lha mi nor zhing 'du shes log // phyin ci log gyur gang 'bar ba// de yang de bzhin ma nor bar// ngas 'dir bdud rtsi'i snying khu 'thungs// gang gi don du stobs bcu po// sems can kun la byams pa bsgoms// byams pa'i stobs kyis rgyal gyur nas// ngas 'dir bdud rtsi'i snying khu 'thungs// gang gi don du stobs bcu po// sems can kun la snying rje bsgoms// snying rje'i stobs mi de ngas ma mthong // myur du song ste thub pa de las rang byas nyes pa shogs shig dang // de ni khyod kyis bsam pa bzhin du sngon gyi lus su sgyur bar 'gyur/ de nas de dag dong ste bdag cag gis thams cad mi 'gro ste/ 'breng pa la sogs pa shing rta'i cha rkyen thams cad kyang chad grugs so// shing rta'i 'phang lo rnams kyang lte ba la thug par sa'i nang du nub ste/ thams cad kyis rab tu bsgrims kyang shing rta de dag 'gro bar ma gyur nas/ kha cig ngo mtshar dang skrag par gyur te/ shing rta 'di dag thang la yang thogs par gyur pa 'di la rgyu ni ci zhig yod/ 'di'i 'gyur ba ni ci zhig yin snyam nas/ de dag gis glang bu legs skyes dang grags pa de gnyis 'dren du bcug ste/ me tog ud pa la spar gang dang / sna ma'i me tog gi phreng bas bdas kyang 'gro bar ma gyur nas de dag 'di snyam du sems te/ gang gi phyir 'di gnyis kyang mi 'gro ba las mdun na 'jigs pa 'ga' zhig 'byung du gdon mi za'o snyam nas/ de dag gis sa 'khru ba rta pa dag sngar btang ngo // sa 'khru ba rta pa rnams slar log nas 'jigs pa ci yang med ces smras so// lha mo des kyang rang gi gzugs bstan nas ma 'jigs shig ces dbugs phyung ngo // glang bu de gnyis kyis de bzhin gshegs pa ga la ba de logs su shing rta gyis 'bar ba mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang de dag ngo mtshar du gyur te/ 'di ni ci zhig tshangs pa 'dir phyin tam/ 'on te lha'i dbang po brgya byin nam/ 'on te rnam thos kyi bu'am/ 'on te nyi ma dang gru dang ni mon gre dang // khrums stod dang yang khrums smad dang // nam gru dang ni tha skar dang // bra nye ste ni bdun pa yin// rgyu skar bdun po de dag ni// 'jig rten skyong ba grags ldan pa// byang phyogs logs na yod ces bstan// de dag khyed la kun tu srungs// de dag bdag po rgyal po ni// mi la zhon pa lus ngan po// gnod sbyin kun gyi bdag po ste// nor lhan cig srung bar shog // de la bu ni mang yod la// mkhas shing ming yang 'thun pa ste// dgu bcu rtsa gcig zad par yang // dbang po zhes bya stobs po che// de dag khyed la nad med cing // shis par lhag par skyong gyur cig // byang sdug // de yang khyed la nad med cing // shis par lhag par skyong gyur cig // phyogs na khyed cag bde bar shog // khyed cag sdig par ma gyur cig // lha rnams kun gyis rab bsrungs nas// nor rnams rnyed de ldog par shog // rgyu skar nyi shu rtsa brgyad po// phyogs bzhi dag na bdun bdun gnas// lha yi bu mo sum cu gnyis// phyogs bzhi dag na brgyad brgyad gnas// dge sbyong brgyad dang bram ze brgyad// yul rnams na ni grong rdal brgyad// dbang por bcas pa'i lha brgyad rnams// de dag khyed la kun tu srungs// khyed cag 'gro na'ang bkra shis gyur// ldog pa na yang bkra shis shog // gnyen la lta ba bkra shis gyur// gnyen gyis blta ba'ang bkra shis shog // dbang bcas gnod sbyin rgya chen dang // dgra bcom pa dag snying brtse bas// thams cad du ni bkra shis dang // bdud rtsi shis pa thob par shog // 'dren zla med 'jig rten mgon po yis// de dag 'thun par sbyin pa'i bsngags pa gsungs// khyed rnams kyi ni dge ba'i las 'di yis// sbrang rtsi 'byung zhes bya ba'i rgyal bar 'gyur// 'jig rten rnam par 'dren pa rgyal ba yis// lung bstan chags med 'di ni dang po yin// phyin chad byang chub sems dpa' mtha' yas mang // gang dag lung bstan de dag phyir mi ldog // rgyal bas lung bstan pa ni 'di thos nas// sems ni mgu zhing mchog tu dga' gyur te// de dag spun dang grogs dang lhan cig tu// de dag sangs rgyas chos la skyabs su dong // ga gon dang bzang po'i le'u zhes bya ba ste/ nyi shu rtsa bzhi pa'o// // dge slong dag da ltar de bzhin gshegs pa shing sgrol rgyu'i drung na bzhugs pa dang po mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa gcig pu dben par gshegs te/ nang du yang dag bzhag nas 'jig rten yongs su ma nyams pa'i phyir/ mos pa'i 'du byed kyi ting nge 'dzin las yongs su ma nyams pa zhes bya'o// dran pa las yongs su ma nyams pa'i phyir/ brtson 'grus las yongs su ma nyams pa zhes bya'o// shes rab las yongs su ma nyams pa'i phyir/ dran pa las yongs su ma nyams pa zhes bya'o// rnam par grol ba las yongs su ma nyams pa'i phyir/ shes rab las yongs su ma nyams pa zhes bya'o// rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba las yongs su ma nyams pa'i phyir/ rnam par grol ba las yongs su ma nyams pa zhes bya'o// lus kyi las dang ngag gi las dang yid kyi las thams cad kyi sngon du ye shes 'gro zhing // ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i ye shes dang ldan pa'i phyir/ rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba las yongs su ma nyams pa zhes bya'o// 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i dus la ma chags ma thogs pa'i ye shes mthong ba dang ldan pa'i phyir/ lus kyi las dang ngag gi las dang yid kyi las thams cad kyi sngon du ye shes 'gro zhing // ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i ye shes dang ldan pa zhes bya'o// sgrib pa med pa'i rnam par thar pa brnyes pa'i phyir/ dus gsum la ma chags ma thogs pa'i ye shes mthong ba dang ldan pa zhes bya'o// sems can thams cad kyi spyod pa la 'jug pa la mkhas pa rgyun mi 'chad pa'i phyir/ sgrib pa med pa'i rnam par thar pa brnyes pa zhes bya'o// so sor ci rigs par chos ston pa la mkhas pa'i phyir/ sems can thams cad kyi spyod pa la 'jug pa la mkhas pa rgyun mi 'chad pa zhes bya'o// dbyangs kyi yan lag thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor dam pa pha rol tu phyin pa'i phyir/ so sor ci rigs par chos ston pa la mkhas pa zhes bya'o// sgra thams cad kyi brag ca 'byin pa la mkhas pa brnyes pa'i phyir/ dbyangs kyi yan lag thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor dam pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o// lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po'i skad dang ldan pa zhes bya'o// tshangs pa'i sgra dbyangs bsgrags pa'i dbyangs lta bu zhes bya'o// ka la ping ka'i sgra skad lta bu zhes bya'o// rnga bo che dang / glu dbyangs kyi sgra skad lta bu zhes bya'o// sa'i sgra'i nga ro'i sgra lta bu zhes bya'o// klu'i rgyal po rgya mtshos 'brug sgra bsgrags pa'i sgra skad lta bu zhes bya'o// seng ge dang / khyu mchog tu gyur pa bsgyings pa'i sgra skad lta bu zhes bya'o// sems can thams cad kyi sgra skad bsgrags pa dang 'thun par sgrogs pas tshim par byed pa'i sgra dang ldan pa zhes bya'o// chags pa med cing sgrib pa med par 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dga' bar byed pa'i sgra dang ldan pa zhes bya'o// skad cig las skad thams cad go bar byed pa'i sgra dang ldan pa zhes bya'o// tshangs pa'i dbang pos mchod pa zhes bya'o// lha'i dbang pos bsti stang du byas pa zhes bya'o// klu'i dbang pos phyag byas pa zhes bya'o// gnod sbyin gyi dbang pos zhal du bltas pa zhes bya'o// dri za'i dbang pos nye bar glu blangs pa zhes bya'o// srin po'i dbang pos dbang po dang bas mig mi 'dzums par bltas pa zhes bya'o// lha ma yin gyi dbang pos mngon par btud pa zhes bya'o// nam mkha' lding gi dbang pos rnam par ma gtses par bltas pa zhes bya'o// mi'am ci'i dbang pos mngon par bstod pa zhes bya'o// lto 'phye chen po'i dbang pos blta 'dod pa zhes bya'o// mi'i dbang pos mngon du yang dag par mchod pa zhes bya'o// dgra bcom pa'i tshogs mang pos bsten pa zhes bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' thams cad yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug pa dang / yang dag par gzengs stod pa dang / yang dag par dga' bar mdzad pa zhes bya'o// zang zing med par chos ston pa zhes bya'o// tshig dang / tshig 'bru nyams pa med par 'bras bu yod pa'i chos ston pa zhes bya'o// dus las mi yol bar chos ston pa zhes bya'o// byams pa chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan bsngags pa'i phyogs la 'jug pa cung zad tsam zhig mdor bstan du zad de/ byams pa rgyas par bya ba ni de bzhin gshegs pas bskal pa'am/ bskal pa las lhag par bstan pa 'di'i mthar mi phyin to// de nas de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyis tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag bka' stsal to// zab cing blta dka' phra ba yi// chos kyi 'khor lo rab bskor te// de la pha rol mu stegs can// kun dang bdud kyis mi chud do// kun gzhi med cing spros med pa// skye ba med cing 'byung med la// dben zhing rang bzhin stong pa yi// chos kyi 'khor lo rab bskor to// blang ba med cing dor med la// mtshan ma med cing mtshan nyid med// mnyam pa nyid kyi chos bstan pa'i// 'khor lo sangs rgyas kyis bskor to// ji ltar sgyu ma smig rgyu dang // rmi lam brag ca chu zla dang // de dag 'dra ba'i 'khor lo ni// 'jig rten mgon pos rab bskor to// rten pa'i chos la 'jug byed pa// chad min rtag pa ma yin pa// lta ba thams cad chad pa ni// chos kyi 'khor lo yin zhes brjod// rtag tu nam mkha' mtshungs 'dra zhing // rnam par mi rtog 'od gsal ba// mtha' dang dbung med bstan pa ni// chos kyi 'khor lor 'dir brjod do// yod dang med las rnam grol zhing // bdag dang bdag med rnam spangs la// rang bzhin ma skyes bstan pa ni// chos kyi 'khor lor 'dir brjod do// yang dag mtha' ni mtha' min pa// de bzhin nyid la de bzhin nyid// gnyis su med pa'i chos bstan pa// chos kyi 'khor lor brjod pa yin// mig ni ngo bo nyid kyis stong // de bzhin sna dang rna ba dang // lce dang lus dang sems kyang ni// stong pa'i bdag nyid g.yo ba med// 'di lta bu yi 'khor lo 'di// chos kyi 'khor lo zhes brjod de// sems can mi mkhas rtogs byed pas// des na sangs rgyas zhes brjod do// chos kyi mtshan nyid rang bzhin 'di// gzhan gyis bstan pa med par ni// nga bdag nyid kyis sangs rgyas te// des na rang byung mig dang ldan// chos rnams kun la dbang brnyes pas// chos kyi rje zhes brjod pa yin// chos la tshul dang tshul min mkhyen// des na 'dren par brjod pa yin// ji ltar 'dul bar 'gyur ba la// skye bo dpag tu med btul te// 'dul ba'i pha rol phyin par gyur// des na rnam par 'dren ces brjod// sems can gang dag lam las nyams// de dag rnams la lam mchog bstan// pha rol gyi ni 'gram du bkri// de phyir nga ni rnam par 'dren// bsdu ba'i dngos po shes pa yis// skye bo dag ni ngas bsdus te// 'khor ba'i 'brog las rgal bas na// des na nga ni ded dpon yin// chos rnams kun la dbang sgyur te// des na rgyal ba chos la mnga'// chos kyi 'khor lo rab bskor bas// chos kyi rgyal por brjod pa yin// chos kyi sbyin bdag ston pa yin// chos kyi bdag po bla na med// mchod sbyin legs mdzad don grub pa// dgongs pa rdzogs pa bkra shis grub// dbugs 'byin mdzad pa de gzigs pa// dpa' bo nyon mongs chen po spong // g.yul rnams kun las rgyal gyur pa// grol ba'i skyes bu thar mdzad pa// 'jig rten gyi ni snang gyur pa// shes rab ye shes 'od mdzad pa// mi shes mun pa 'joms pa po// sgron ma 'dzin pa 'od chen ldan// ye shes che ldan sman pa che// nyon mongs pa las gso mdzad pa// sems can nyon mongs zugs rnams la// zug rngu 'byin pa bla na med// mtshan rnams thams cad phun sum tshogs// dpe byad bzang po kun gyis mdzes// sku yis kun tu bzang ba ste// dman pa rnams dang 'thun par mdzad// stobs bcu'i stobs dang shin tu ldan// bsnyengs pa mi mnga' mi bsnyengs pa// ma 'dres rnam pa brgyad kyis// thub pa chen po theg pa mchog // chos kyi 'khor lo rab bskor ba// 'di ni mdo tsam bshad pa yin// de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan bsngags// 'di ni cung zad brjod par zad// sangs rgyas ye shes mtha' yas te// nam mkha' rgya che mnyam pa bzhin// bskal pa zad par brjod kyang ni// sangs rgyas yon tan mi zad do// chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i le'u zhes bya ste/ nyi shu rtsa drug pa'o// // de nas lha'i bu gang dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa la chos kyi rnam grangs 'di rab tu bshad par gsol ba btab par gyur pa dbang phyug dang / dbang phyug chen po dang / dga' bo dang / rab dga' dang / tsan dan dang / mchod pa dang / zhi ba dang // rab tu zhi ba dang / dul ba'i dbang phyug la sogs pa gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu dang mi yi mchog rnams dang // rnam pa mang pos bskal pa du mar mchod byed la// gang zhig dam pa'i chos ni rnam par 'jig pa'i tshe// rang gi lus dang de bzhin srog kyang btang nas ni// zhag gcig bar du mdo sde 'di ni 'dzin byed na// bsod nams 'di ni de bas khyad par 'phags par 'gyur// gang zhig rnam par 'dren pa rnams dang rang rgyal dang // de bzhin nyan thos rnams la mchod pa byed 'dod pa// de yis byang chub sems ni brtan por bskyed byas te// mdo sde 'di ni rtag par rab tu gzung bar bya// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mngon byung gang yin pa// 'di ni legs par bshad pa kun gyi rgyal po yin// mdo sde dkon mchog 'di ni gang na gnas 'gyur ba// de yi khyim du de bzhin gshegs pa rtag tu gnas// gang gis mdo 'di pha rol dag la byin pa dang // tshig gcig brjod pa de yang bskal pa bye bar ni// tshig 'bru rnams las mi nyams don las nyams mi 'gyur// spobs pa dge ba mtha' yas pa dag 'thob par 'gyur// gang zhig chos 'di thos nas rab tu sgrub byed pa// de ni mi yi 'dren pa ma gtogs 'og tu ni// de 'dra ba yi sems can gang yang yod ma yin// de ni rgya mtsho lta bur zad mi shes par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ lha'i bu dbang phyug chen po la sogs pa gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu de dag dang / byams pa la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po thams cad dang / 'od srung chen po la sogs pa nyan thos chen po thams cad dang / tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo dang / lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yi rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// mjug sdud pa'i le'u zhes bya ba ste/ nyi shu rtsa bdun pa'o// // 'phags pa rgya cher rol pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo rdzogs // // rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / mu ni bar ma dang / zhu chen gyi lots+tsha ba ban de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te/ skad gsar chad kyis kyang bcos nas gtan la phab pa//
